Wa kaza_lika a'sarna_ 'alaihim liya'lamu_ anna wa'dalla_hi  haqquw wa annas sa_'ata la_ raiba fiha_, iz yatana_za'u_na bainahum amrahum faqa_lu-bnu_ 'alaihim bunya_na_(n), rabbuhum a'lamu bihim, qa_lal lazina galabu_ 'ala_ amrihim lanattakhizanna 'alaihim masjida_(n).
Sayaqu_lu_na sala_satur ra_bi'uhum kalbuhum, wa yaqu_lu_na khamsatun sa_disuhum kalbuhum rajmam bil gaib(i), wa yaqu_lu_na sab'atuw wa sa_minuhum kalbuhum, qur rabbi a'lamu bi 'iddatihim ma_ ya'lamuhum illa_ qalil(un), fala_ tuma_ri fihim illa_ mira_'an za_hira_(w), wa la_ tastafti fihim minhum ahada_(n).
Wa la_ taqa_lanna lisyai'in inni fa_'ilun za_lika gada_(n),
Illa_ ay yasya_'alla_h(u), wa-zkur rabbaka iza_ nasita wa qul 'asa_ ay yahdiyani rabbi li'aqraba min ha_za_ rasyada_(n).
Wa labisu_ fi kahfihim sala_sa mi'atin sinina wa-zda_du_ tis'a_(n).
Qulilla_hu a'lamu bima_ labisa_, lahu_ gaibus sama_wa_ti wal ard(i), absir bihi wa asmi', ma_ lahum min du_nihi miw waliyy(in), wa la_ yusyriku fi hukmihi  ahada_(n).
Wa-tlu ma_ u_hiya ilaika min kita_bi rabbik(a), la_ mubaddila likalima_tih(i), wa lan tajida min du_nihimultahada_(n).
Wa-sbir nafsaka ma'al lazina yad'u_na rabbahum bil gada_ti wal 'asyiyyi yurida_na wajhahu_ wa la_ ta'du 'aina_ka 'anhum, turidu zinatal haya_tid dunya_, wa la_ tuti' man agfalna_ qalbahu_ 'an zikrina_ wa-ttaba'a hawa_hu wa ka_na amruhu_ furuta_(n).
Wa qulil haqqu mir rabbikum, faman sya_'a falyu'miw wa man sya_'a falyakfur, inna_ a'tadna_ liz za_limina na_ra_(n), aha_ta bihim sura_diquha_, wa iy yastagisu_ yuga_su bi ma_'in kal muhli yasywil wuju_h(a), bi'sasy syara_b(u), wa sa_'at murtafaqa_(n).
Innal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti inna_ la_ nudi'u ajra man ahsana  'amala_(n).
Ula_'ika lahum janna_tu 'adnin tajri min tahtihimul anha_ru yuhallauna fiha_ min asa_wira min zahabiw wa yalbasu_na siya_ban khudram min sundusiw wa istabraqim muttaki'ina fiha_ 'alal ara_'ik(i), ni'massawa_b(u), wa hasunat murtafaqa_(n).
Wa-drib lahum masalar  rajulaini ja'alna_ li'ahadihima_ jannataini min a'na_biw wa hafafna_huma_ bi nakhliw wa ja'alna_ bainahuma_ zar'a_(n).
Kiltal jannataini a_tat ukulaha_ wa lam tazlim minhu syai'a_(w), wa fajjarna_ khila_lahuma_ nahara_(w),
Wa ka_na lahu_ samar(un), faqa_la lisa_hibihi wa huwa yuha_wiruhu_ ana aksaru minka ma_law wa a'azzu nafara_(n).
Wa dakhala jannatahu_ wa huwa za_limul li nafsih(i), qa_la ma_ azunnu an tabida ha_zihi  abada_(w),
Wa ma_ azunnus sa_'ata qa_'imataw wa la'ir rudittu ila_ rabbi la'ajidanna khairam minha_ munqalaba_(n).
Qa_la lahu_ sa_hibuhu_ wa huwa yuha_wiruhu_ akafarta billazi khalaqaka min tura_bin summa min nutfatin summa sawwa_ka rajula_(n).
La_kinna huwalla_hu rabbi wa la_ usyriku bi rabbi ahada_(n).
Wa lau la_ iz dakhalta jannataka qulta ma_ sya_'alla_h(u), la_ quwwata illa_ billa_h(i), in tarani ana aqalla minka ma_law wa walada_(n).
Fa 'asa_ rabbi ay yu'tiyani khairam min jannatika wa yursila 'alaiha_ husba_nam minas sama_'i fatusbiha sa'idan zalaqa_(n).
Au yusbiha ma_'uha_ gauran falan tastati'a lahu_ talaba_(n).
Wa uhita bi samarihi fa asbaha yuqallibu kaffaihi 'ala_ ma_ anfaqa fiha_ wa hiya kha_wiyatun 'ala_ 'uru_syiha_ wa yaqu_lu ya_ laitani lam usyrik bi rabbi ahada_(n).
Wa lam takul lahu_ fi'atuy yansuru_nahu_ min du_nilla_hi wa ma_ ka_na muntasira_(n).
Huna_likal wala_yatu lilla_hil haqq(i), huwa khairun sawa_baw wa khairun 'uqba_(n).
Wa-drib lahum masalal haya_tid dunya_ kama_'in anzalna_hu minas sama_'i fa-khtalata bihi naba_tul ardi fa asbaha hasyiman tazru_hur riya_h(u), wa ka_nalla_hu 'ala_ kulli syai'im  muqtadira_(n).
Al ma_lu wal banu_na zinatul haya_tid dunya_, wal ba_qiya_tus sa_liha_tu khairun 'inda rabbika sawa_baw wa khairun amala_(n).
Wa yauma nusayyirul jiba_la wa taral arda ba_rizataw wa hasyarna_hum falam nuga_dir minhum ahada_(n).
Wa 'uridu_ 'ala_ rabbika saffa_(n), laqad ji'tumu_na_ kama_ khalaqna_kum awwala marrah(tim), bal za'amtum allan naj'ala lakum mau'ida_(n).
Wa wudi'al kita_bu fataral mujrimina musyfiqina mimma_ fihi wa yaqu_lu_na ya_  wailatana_ ma_li ha_zal kita_bi la_ yuga_diru sagirataw wa la_ kabiratan illa_ ahsa_ha_, wa wajadu_ ma_ 'amilu_ ha_dira_(n), wa la_ yazlimu rabbuka ahada_(n).
Wa iz qulna_ lil mala_'ikati-sjudu_ li'a_dama fasajadu_ illa_ iblis(a), ka_na minal jinni fafasaqa 'an amri rabbih(i), afatattakhizu_nahu_ wa zurriyyatahu_ auliya_'a min du_ni wa hum lakum 'aduww(un), bi'sa liz za_limina badala_(n).
Ma_ asyhattuhum khalqas sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa la_ khalqa anfusihim, wa ma_  kuntu muttakhizal mudillina 'aduda_(n).
Wa yauma yaqu_lu na_du_ syuraka_'iyal lazina za'amtum fa da'auhum falam yastajibu_ lahum wa ja'alna_ bainahum maubiqa_(n).
Wa ra'al mujrimu_nan na_ra fa zannu_ annahum muwa_qi'uha_ wa  lam yajidu_ 'anha_ masrifa_(n).
Wa laqad sarrafna_ fi ha_zal qur'a_ni lin na_si min kulli masal(in), wa ka_nal insa_nu aksara syai'in jadala_(n).
Wa ma_ mana'an na_sa ay yu'minu_ iz ja_'ahumul huda_ wa yastagfiru_ rabbahum illa_ ay ta'tiyahum sunnatul awwalina  au ya'tiyahumul 'azu_bu qubula_(n).
Wa ma_ nursilul mursalina illa_ mubasysyirina wa munzirin(a), wa yuja_dilul  lazina kafaru_ bil ba_tili liyudhidu_ bihil haqqa wa-ttakhazu_ a_ya_ti wa ma_ unziru_ huzuwa_(n).
Wa man azlamu mim man zukkira bi a_ya_ti rabbihi fa a'rada 'anha_ wa nasiya ma_ qaddamat yada_h(u), inna_ ja'alna_ 'ala_ qulu_bihim akinnatan ay yafqahu_hu wa fi a_za_nihim waqra_(n), wa in tad'uhum ilal huda_ falay yahtada_ izan abada_(n).
Wa rabbukal gafu_ru zur rahmah(ti), lau yu'a_khizuhum bima_ kasabu_ la'ajjala lahumul 'aza_b(a), bal lahum mau'idul lay yajidu_ min du_nihi mau'ila_(n).
Wa tilkal qura_ ahlakna_hum  lamma_ zalamu_ wa ja'alna_ limahlikihim mau'ida_(n).
Wa iz qa_la mu_sa_ lifata_hu la_ abrahu hatta_ abluga majma'al bahraini au amdiya  huquba_(n).
Falamma_ balaga majma'a bainihima_ nasiya_ hu_tahuma_ fa-ttakhaza sabilahu_ fil bahri saraba_(n).
Falamma_ ja_waza_ qa_la lifata_hu a_tina_ gada_'ana_, laqad laqina_ min safarina_ ha_za_ nasaba_(n).
Qa_ ara'aita iz awaina_ ilas sakhrati fa inni nasitul hu_t(a), wa ma_ ansa_nihu illasy syaita_nu anazkurah(u_), wa-ttakhaza  sabilahu_ fil bahri 'ajaba_(n).
Qa_la za_lika ma_ kunna_  nabg(i), fa-rtadda 'ala_ a_sa_rihima_ qasasa_(n),
Fa wajada_ 'abdam min'iba_dina_ a_taina_hu rahmatam min 'indina_ wa 'allamna_hu mil ladunna_ 'ilma_(n).
Qa_la lahu_ mu_sa_ hal  attabi'uka 'ala_ an tu'allimani mimma_ 'ullimta rusyda_(n).
Qa_la innaka lan tastati'a ma'iya sabra_(n).
Wa kaifa tasbiru 'ala_ ma_ lam tuhit bihi khubra_(n).
Qa_la satajiduni in sya_'alla_hu sa_biraw wa la_ a'si laka amra_(n).
Qa_la fa in-ittaba'tani fala_ tas'alni 'an syai'in hatta_ uhdisa laka minhu zikra_(n).
Fa-ntalaqa_, hatta_ iza_ rakiba_ fis safinati kharaqaha_, qa_la akharaqtaha_ litugriqa ahlaha_, laqad ji'ta syai'an  imra_(n).
Qa_la alam aqul innaka lan tastati'a ma'iya sabra_(n).
Qa_la la_ tu'a_khizni bima_  nasitu wa la_ turhiqni min amri 'usra_(n).
Fa-ntalaqa_, hatta_ iza_ laqiya_ gula_man faqatalah(u_), qa_la aqatalta nafsan zakiyyatam bi gairi nafs(in), laqad ji'ta syai'an nukra_(n).
Qa_la alam aqul laka in naka lan tastati'a ma'iya sabra_
Qa_la in sa altuka 'an sai im ba'daha_ fala_ tusha_hibni qad balaghta mil ladun ni 'udzra_
Fanthalaqa_ hat ta_ iza_ ataya_ ahla qaryatinis tat'ama_ ahlaha_ fa abau ay yudhay yifu_huma_ fawajada_ fiha_ jida_ray yuridu ay yanqad dafa aqa_mah qa_la lau syi'ta lat takhazta 'alaihi ajra_
Qa_la ha_za_ fira_qu baini wa bainik sa unab bi uka bita wili ma_ lam tasti 'alaihi shabra_
Am mas safinatu faka_nat limasa_kina ya'malu_na fil bahri fa aratu an a'ibaha_ wa ka_na wara_ ahum ma likuy ya'khudzu kul la safinatin gasba_
Wa am mal gula_mu faka_na abawa_hu mu'minaini fakhasyina_ ay yurhi qahuma_ thughya_naw wa kufra_
Fa aradna_ ay yubdilahuma_ rab buhuma_ khairam minhu zaka_taw wa aqraba ruhma_
Wa am mal jida_ru faka_na lighula_maini yatimaini fil madinati wa ka_na tahtahu_ kanzul lahuma_ wa ka_na abu_huma_ sa_liha_ fa ara_da rabbuka ay yablugha_ asyud dahuma_ wa yastakhrija_ kanzahuma_ rahmatam mir rab bik wa ma_ fa'altuhu_ an amri za_lika ta'wilu ma_ lam tasti 'alaihi sabra_
Wa yas alu_naka 'an dzil qarnain qul sa atlu_ alaikum minhu zikra_
In na_ mak kan na_ lahu_ fil ardi wa a_taina_hu min kul li sai in sababa_
Fa atba'a sababa_
Hat ta_ iza_ balagha magribas samsi wajadaha_ taghrubu fi ainin hami atiw wa wajada 'indaha_ qauma_ qulna_ ya_ zal qarnaini im ma_ an tu'az ziba wa im ma_ an tat takhiza fihim husna_
Qa_la am ma_ man zalama fasaufa nu'az zibuhu_ sum ma yurad du ila_ rab bihi fayu'az zibuhu_ aza_ban nukra_
Wa am ma_ man a_mana wa amila sha_lihan falahu_ jaza_ anil husna_ wa sanaqu_lu lahu_ min amrina_ yusra_
Sum ma atba'a sababa_
Hat ta_ iza_ balagha mathli'as samsi wajadaha_ tathlu'u ala_ qaumil lamnaj'al lahum min du_niha_ sitra_
Kaza_lik wa qad ahathna_ bima_ ladaihi khubra_
Sum ma atba'a sababa_
Hat ta_ iza_ balagha bainas sad daini wajada min du_nihima_ qaumal la_ yaka_du_na yafqahu_na qaula_
Qa_lu_ ya_ zal qarnaini in na yaju_ja wa ma'ju_ja mufsidu_na fil ardi fahal naj'alu laka kharjan 'ala_ an taj'ala bainana_ wa bainahum sad da_
Qa_la ma_ mak kan ni fihi rab bi khairun fa a'inu_ni biquw watin aj'al bainakum wa bainahum radma_
A_tu_ni zubaral hadid hat ta_ iza_ sa_wa_ bainas sadafain qa_lan fukhu_ hat ta_ idza_ ja'alahu_ na_ran qa_la a_tu_ni ufrig 'alaihi qithra_
Famas tha_'u_ ay yazharu_hu wa mas tata_'u_ lahu_ naqba_
Qa_la ha_dza_ rahmatum mir rab bi fa idza_ ja_ a wa'du rab bi ja'alahu_ dak ka_ wa ka_na wa'du rab bi haq qa_
Wa tarakna_ ba'dhahum yauma idziy yamu_ju fi ba'diw wa nufikha fis su_ri fajama'na_hum jam'a_
Wa 'aradhna_ jahan nama yauma idzil lil ka_firina 'ardha_
Nil lazina ka_nat a'yunuhum fi gita_in 'an zikri wa ka_nu_ la_ yastati'una sam'a_
Afahasibal lazina kafaru_ ay yat takhizu_ iba_di min du_ni auliya_ in na_ a'tadna_ jahan nama lilka_firina nuzula_
Qul hal nunab bi ukum bil akhsarina a'ma_la_
Al lazina dhal la sa'yuhum fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa hum yahsabu_na an nahum yuhsinu_na shun'a_
Ula_ ikal lazina kafaru_ bi a_ya_ti rab bihim wa liqa_ ihi fahabitat a'ma_luhum fala_ nuqimu lahum yaumal qiya_mati wazna_
Za_lika jaza_uhum jahan namu bima_ kafaru_ wat takhadzu_ a_ya_ti wa rusuli huzuwa_
In nal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti ka_nat lahum jan na_tul firdausi nuzula_
Kha_lidina fiha_ la_ yabghu_na 'anha_ hiwala_
Qul lau ka_nal bahru mida_dal likalima_ti rab bi lanafidal bahru qabla antanfada kalima_tu rab bi wa lau ji na_ bimitslihi madada_
Qul in nama_ ana basyarum mitslukum yu_ha_ ilay ya an nama_ ila_hukum ila_huw wa_hid faman ka_na yarju_ liqa_ a rab bihi falya'mal amalan sa_lihaw wa la_ yusrik bi'iba_dati rab bihi ahada_
Ka_f ha_ ya_ 'ai in sha_d
Zikru rahmati rab bika 'abdahu_ zakariy ya_
Iz na_da_ rab bahu_ nida_ an khafiy ya_
Qa_la rab bi in ni wahanal 'azhmu min ni was ta'alar ra'su saibaw wa lam akum bidu'a_ ika rab bi saqiy ya_
Wa in ni khiftul mawa_liya miw wara_i wa ka_natim ra ati 'a_qiran fahab li mil ladunka waliy ya_
Yaritsuni wayaritsu min a_li ya'ku_b waj'alhu rab bi radhiy ya_
Ya_ zakariy ya_ in na_ nubas siruka bighula_minis muhu_ yahya_ lam naj'al lahu_ min qablu samiy ya_
Qa_la rab bi an na_ yaku_nu li ghula_muw wa ka_natim ra ati 'a_qiraw wa qad balaghtu minal kibari 'itiy ya_
Qa_la kadza_lik qa_la rab buka huwa 'alay ya hay yinuw wa qad khalaqtuka min qablu wa lam taku sai a_
Qa_la rab bij'al li a_yah qa_la a_yatuka al la_ tukal liman na_sa tsala_tsa laya_lin sawiy ya_
Fakhraja 'ala_ qaumihi minal mihra_bi fa auha_ ilaihim an sab bihu_ bukrataw wa asyiy ya_
Ya_ yahya_ khudzil kita_ba biquw wah wa a_taina_hul hukma sabiy ya_
Wa hana_nam mil ladun na_ wa zaka_h wa ka_na taqiy ya_
Wa bar ran biwa_lidaihi wa lam yakun jab bara_n ashiy ya_
Wa sala_mun 'alaihi yauma wulida wa yauma yamu_tu wa yauma yub'atsu hay ya_
Wadz kur fil kita_bi maryam idzin tabadzat min ahliha_ maka_nan syarqiy ya_
Fat takhadzat min du_nihim hija_ba_ fa arsalna_ ilaiha_ ru_hana_fatamats sala laha_ basyaran sawiy ya_
Qa_lat in ni a'u_dzu bir rahma_ni minka in kunta taqiy ya_
Qa_la in nama_ ana rasu_lu rab bik li ahaba laki ghula_man zakiy ya_
Qa_lat an na_ yaku_nu li ghula_muw wa lam yamsasni basyaruw wa lam aku baghiy ya_
Qa_la kadza_lik qa_la rab buki huwa alay ya hay yin wa linaj'alahu_ a_ya_tal lin na_si wa rahmatam min na_ wa ka_na amram maqdhiy ya_
Fahamalat hu fan tabadzat bihi maka_nan qashiy ya_
Fa aja_ ahal makha_dhu ila_ jidz'in nakhlah qa_lat ya_ laitani mit ti qabla ha_dza_ wa kuntu nas yam mansiy ya_
Fana_da_ha_ min tahtiha_ al la_ tahzani qad ja'ala rab buki tahtaki sariy ya_
Wa huz zi ilaiki bijidz'in nakhlati tusa_qith alaiki ruthaban janiy ya_
Fakuli was rabi wa qar ri aina_ fa im ma_ tarayin na minal basyari ahadan faqu_li in ni nadzartu lir rahma_ni shauman falan ukal limal yauma insiy ya_
Fa atat bihi qaumaha_ tahmiluh qa_lu_ ya_ maryamu laqad ji'ti sai an fariy ya_
Ya_ ukhta ha_ru_na ma_ ka_na abu_kim ra a sau iw wa ma_ ka_nat um muki baghiy ya_
Fa asa_rat ilaihi qa_lu_ kaifa nukal limu man ka_na fil mahdi shabiy ya_
Qa_la in ni abdul la_h a_ta_niyal kita_ba wa ja'a ani nabiy ya_
Wa ja'alani muba_rakan aina ma_ kuntu wa ausha_ni bis sala_ti waz zaka_ti ma_ dumtu hay ya_
Wa bar ram biwa_lidati wa lam yaj'alni jab ba_ran syaqiy ya_
Was sala_mu 'alay ya yauma wulidtu wa yauma amu_tu wa yauma ub'atsu hay ya_
Za_lika 'isab nu maryam qaulal haq qil lazi fihi yamtaru_n
Ma_ ka_na lil la_hi ay yat takhidza miw waladin subha_nah idza_ qadha_ amran fa in nama_ yaqu_lu lahu_ kun fayaku_n
Wa in nal la_ha rab bi wa rab bukum fa'budu_h ha_dza_ shira_thum mustaqim
Fakh talafal ahza_bu mim bainihim fawailul lil lazina kafaru_ mim mashadi yaumin 'azhim
Asmi'bihim wa abshir yauma ya'tu_nana_ la_kiniz zha_limu_nal yauma fi dhala_lim mubin
Wa andzirhum yaumal hasrati idz qudhiyal amr wa hum fi ghaflatiw wahum la_ yu'minu_n
In na_ nahnu naritsul ardha wa man alaiha_ wa ilaina_ yurja'u_n
Wadz kur fil kita_bi ibra_him in nahu_ ka_na shid diqan nabiy ya_
Idz qa_la li abihi ya_ abati lima ta'budu ma_ la_ yasma'u wa la_ yubshiru wa la_ yughni 'anka sai a_
Ya_ abati in ni qad ja_ ani minal 'ilmi ma_ lam ya'tika fat tabi'ni ahdika shira_than sawiy ya_
Ya_ abati la_ ta'budis saitha_n inas saitha_na ka_na lir rahma_ni ashiy ya_
Ya_ abati in ni akha_fu ay yamas saka adza_bum minar rahma_ni fataku_na lis saitha_ni waliy ya_
Qa_la ara_ghibun anta an a_lihati ya_ ibra_him la il lam tantahi la arjuman naka wah jurni maliy ya_
Qa_la sala_mun 'alaika sa astaghfiru laka rab bi in nahu_ ka_na hafiy ya_
Wa a'tazilukum wa ma_ tad'u_na min du_nil la_hi wa ad'u_ rab bi asa_ al la_ aku_na bidu'a_i rab bi syaqiy ya_
Falam ma tazalahum wa ma_ ya'budu_na min du_nil la_hi wahabna_ lahu_ is ha_qa wa ya'qu_b wa kul lan ja'alna_ nabiy ya_
Wa wahabna_ lahum mir rahmatina_ wa ja'alna_ lahum lisa_na shidqin 'aliy ya_
Wadz kur fil kita_bi musa_ in nahu_ ka_na mukhlashaw wa ka_na rasu_lan nabiy ya_
Wa na_daina_hu min ja_nibit thu_ril aimani wa qar rabna_hu najiy ya_
Wa wahabna_ lahu_ mir rahmatina_ akha_hu ha_ru_na nabiy ya_
Wadz kur fil kita_bi isma_'ila in nahu_ ka_na sha_diqal wa'di wa ka_na rasu_lan nabiy ya_
Wa ka_na ya'muru ahlahu_ bis shala_ti waz zaka_h wa ka_na inda rab bihi mardhiy ya_
Wadz kur fil kita_bi idris in nahu_ ka_na shid diqan nabiy ya_
Wa rafa'na_hu maka_nan 'aliy ya_
Ula_ ikal lazina an'amal la_hu 'alaihim minan nabiy yina min dzur riy yati a_dam wa mim man hamalna_ ma'a nu_hiw wa min dzur riy yati ibra_hima wa isra_ ila wa mim man hadaina_ waj tabaina_ idza_ tutla_ 'alaihim a_ya_tur rahma_ni khar ru_ suj jadaw wa bukiy ya_
Fakhalafa mim ba'dihim khulfun adha_'us sala_ta wat taba'us sahawa_ti fasaufa yalqauna ghay ya_
Il la_ man ta_ba wa a_mana wa 'amila sha_lihan fa ula_ ika yadkhulu_nal jannata wa la_ yuzhlamu_na sai a_
Jan na_ti adninil lati wa'adar rahma_nu iba_dahu_ bil ghaib in nahu_ ka_na wa'duhu_ ma'tiy ya_
La_ yasma'u_na fiha_ laghwan il la_ sala_ma_ wa lahum rizquhum fiha_ bukrataw wa asyiy ya_
Tilkal jan natul lati nu_ritsu min 'iba_dina_ man ka_na taqiy ya_
Wa ma_ natanaz zalu il la_ bi amri rab bika lahu_ ma_ baina aidina_ wama_ khalfana_ wa ma_ baina dza_lik wa ma_ ka_na rab buka nasiy ya_
Rab bus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ fa'bud hu wash thabir li'iba_datih hal ta'lamu lahu_ samiy ya_
Wa yaqu_lul insa_nu a idza_ ma_ mittu lasaufa ukhraju hay ya_
Awa la_ yadzkurul insa_nu an na khalaqna_hu min qablu wa lam yaku sai a_
Fawarab bika lanahsyuran nahum wasysyaya_thina sum ma lanuhdhiran nahum haula jahan nama jitsiy ya_
Sum ma lananzi'an na min kul li si'atin ay yuhum asyad du alar rahma_ni itiy ya_
Sum ma lanahnu a'lamu bil lazina hum aula_ biha_ shiliy ya_
Wa im minkum il la_ wa_riduha_ ka_na 'ala_ rab bika hatmam maqdhiy ya_
Sum ma nunaj jil lazinat taqauw wa nadzaruzh zha_limina fiha_ jitsiy ya_
Wa iza_ tutla_ 'alaihim a_ya_tuna_ bay yina_tin qa_lal lazina kafaru_ lil lazina a_manu_ ay yul fariqaini khairum maqa_maw wa ahsanu nadiy ya_
Wa kam ahlakna_ qablahum min qarnin hum ahsanu atsa_tsaw wari'ya_
Qul man ka_na fidh dhala_lati falyamdud lahur rahma_nu mad da_ hat ta_ idza_ ra au ma_ yu_'adu_na im mal adza_ba wa im mas sa_'ah fasaya'lamu_na man huwa syar rum maka_naw wa adh'afu junda_
Wa yazidul la_hul ladzinah tadau huda_ wal ba_qiya_tush sha_liha_tu khairun 'inda rab bika tsawa_baw wa khairum marad da_
Afara aital lazi kafara bi a_ya_tina_ wa qa_la la u_tayan na ma_law wawalada_
Ath thala'al ghaiba amit takhadza indar rahma_ni ahda_
Kal la_ sanaktubu ma_ yaqu_lu wa namud du lahu_ minal adza_bi mad da_
Wa naritsuhu_ ma_ yaqu_lu wa ya'tina farda_
Wat takhadzu_ min du_nil la_hi a_lihatal liyaku_nu_ lahum iz za_
Kal la_ sayakfuru_na bi'iba_datihim wa yaku_nu_na 'alaihim dhid da_
Alam tara an na_ arsalna_sy syaya_thina 'alal ka_firina ta'uz zuhum azza_
Fala_ ta'jal alaihim in nama_ na'uddu lahum ad da_
Yauma nahsyurul mut taqina ilar rahma_ni wafda_
Wa nasu_qul mujrimina ila_ jahan nama wirda_
La_ yamliku_nas syafa_'ata il la manit takhadza indar rahma_ni ahda_
Wa qa_lut takhadzar rahma_nu walada_
Laqad ji'tum sai an id da_
Taka_dus sama_wa_tu yatafath tharna minhu wa tansyaq qul ardhu wa takhir rul jiba_lu had da_
An da'au lir rahma_ni walada_
Wa ma_ yan baghi lir rahma_ni ay yat takhidza walada_
In kul lu man fis sama_wa_ti wal ardhi il la_ a_tir rahma_ni 'abda_
Laqad ahsha_hum wa ad dahum ad da_
Wa kul luhum a_tihi yaumal qiya_mati farda_
In nal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sha_liha_ti sayaj'alu lahumur rahma_nu wud da_
Fa in nama_ yas sarna_hu bilisa_nika litubasy syira bihil mut taqina wa tundzira bihi qaumal lud da_
Wa kam ahlakna_ qablahum min qarn hal tuhis su minhum min ahadin autasma'u lahum rikza_
Tha_ ha_
Ma_ anzalna_ alaikal qur a_na litasyqa_
Illa tadz kiratal limay yakhsya_
Tanzilam mim man khalaqal ardha was sama_wa_ti 'ula_
Ar rahma_nu 'alal arsyis tawa_
Lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ wa ma_ tahtats tsara_
Wa in tajhar bil qauli fa in nahu_ ya'lamus sir ra wa akhfa_
Al la_hu la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa lahul asma_ ul husna_
Wa hal ata_ka haditsu mu_sa_
Idz ra a_ na_ran faqa_la li ahlihim kutsu_ in ni a_nastu na_ral la'al li a_tikum minha_ biqabasin au ajidu 'alan na_ri huda_
Falam ma_ ata_ha_ nu_diya ya_ mu_sa_
In ni ana rab buka fakh la na'laik in naka bil wa_dil muqad dasi thuwa_
Wa anakh tartuka fastami lima_ yu_ha_
In nani anal la_hu la_ ila_ha il la_ ana fa'budni wa aqimish shala_ta lidzikri
In nas sa_'ata a_tiyatun aka_dun ukhfiha_ litujza_ nafsim bima_ tas'a_
Fala_ yashud dan naka 'anha mal la_ yu.minu biha_ wat taba'a hawa_hu fatarda_
Wa ma_ tilka biyaminika ya_ mu_sa_
Qa_la hiya asha_y atawak ka u 'alaiha_ wa ahus syu biha_ 'ala_ ghanami waliya fiha_ ma a_ribu ukhra_
Qa_la alqiha_ ya_ mu_sa_
Fa alqa_ha_ fa idza_ hiya hay yatun tas'a_
Qa_la khudz ha_ wa la_ takhal sanu'iduha_ siratahal u_la_
Wadh mum yadaka ila_ jana_hika takhruj baidha_'a min ghairi su_ in a_yatan ukhra_
Linuriyakamin a_ya_tinal kubra_
Idzhab ila_ fir'auna in nahu_ thagha_
Qa_la rab bis rah li shadri
Wa yas sir li amri
Wah lul uqdatam mil lisa_ni
Yafqahu_ qauli
Waj'al li waziram min ahli
Ha_ru_na akhi
Usydud bihi azri
Wa asyrik hu fi amri
Kai nusab bihaka katsira_
Wa nadzkuraka katsira_
In naka kunta bina_ bashira_
Qa_la qad u_tita su'laka ya_ mu_sa_
Wa laqad manan na_ 'alaika mar ratan ukhra_
Idz auhaina_ ila_ um mika ma_ yu_ha_
Aniq dzifihi fit ta_bu_ti faqdzi fihi fil yam mi falyulqihil yam mu bis sa_hili ya'khudzhu aduw wul li wa aduwwul lah wa alqaitu alaika mahab batam min ni walitushna'a ala_ aini
Idz tamsyi ukhtuka fataqu_lu hal adul lukum 'ala_ may yakfuluh faraja'na_ka ila_ um mika kaitaqar ra ainuha_ wa la_ tahzan wa qatalta nafsan fanaj jaina_ka minal gham mi wafatan na_ka futu_na_ falabitsta sinina fi ahli mad yana sum ma ji'ta 'ala_ qadariy ya_ mu_sa_
Wash thana'tuka linafsi
Idzhab anta wa akhu_ka bi a_ya_ti wa la_ taniya_ fi dzikri
idzhaba_ ila_ fir'auna in nahu_ thagha_
Faqu_la_ lahu_ qaulal lay yinal la'al lahu_ yatadzak karu au yakhsya_
Qa_la rab bana_ in nana_ nakha_fu ay yafrutha alaina_ au ay yathgha_
Qa_la la_ takha_fa_ in nani ma'akuma_ asma'u wa ara_
Fa'tiya_hu faqu_la_ in na_ rasu_la_ rab bika fa arsil ma'ana_ bani isra_ ila wa la_ tu'adz dzibhum qad ji'na_ka bi a_yatim mir rab bik was sala_mu 'ala_ manit taba'al huda_
In na_ qad u_hiya ilaina_ an nal adza_ba 'ala_ man kadz dzaba wa tawal la_
Qa_la famar rab bukuma_ ya_ mu_sa_
Qa_la rab bunal ladzi a'tha_ kul la sai in khalqahu_ sum ma bada_
Qa_la fama_ ba_lul quru_nil u_la_
Qa_la ilmuha_ 'inda rab bi fi kita_b la_ yadhil lu rab bi wa la_ yansa_
Al ladzi ja'ala lakumul ardha mahdaw wa salaka lakum fiha_ subulaw wa anzala minas sama_i ma_ fa akhrajna_ bihi azwa_jam min naba_tin syat ta_
Kulu_ war'au an'a_makum in na fi dza_lika la a_ya_til li ulin nuha_
Minha_ khalaqna_kum wa fiha_ nu'idukum wa minha_ nukhrijukum ta_ratan ukhra_
Wa laqad araina_hu a_ya_tina_ kullaha_ fakadz dzaba wa aba_
Qa_la aji'tana_ litukhrijana_ min ardhina_ bisihrika ya_ mu_sa_
Falana'tiyan naka bisihrim mitslihi faj'al bainana_ wa bainaka mau'idal la_ nukhlifuhu_ nahnu wa la_ anta maka_nan suwa_
Qa_la mau'idukum yaumuz zinati wa ay yuhsyaran na_su dhuha_
Fatawal la_ fir'aunu fajama'a kaidahu_ sum ma ata_
Qa_la lahum mu_sa_ wailakum la_ taftaru_ 'alal la_hi kadziban fayus hitakum bi'adza_b wa qad kha_ba manif tara_
Fatana_za'u_ amrahum bainahum wa asar run najwa_
Qa_lu_ in ha_dza_ni lasa_hira_ni yurida_ni ay yukhrija_kum min ardhikum bisihrihima_ wa yadz haba_ bi thariqatikumul mutsla_
Fa ajmi'u_ kaidakum sum ma tu_shaf fa_ wa qad aflahal yauma manis ta'la_
Qa_lu_ ya_ mu_sa_  im ma_ an tulqiya wa im ma_ an naku_na aw wala man alqa_
Qa_la bal alqu_ fa idza_ hiba_luhum wa ishiy yuhum yukhay yalu ilaihi min sihrihim an naha_ tas'a_
Fa aujasa fi nafsihi khifatam mu_sa_
Qulna_ la_ takhaf in naka antal a'la_
Wa alqi ma_ fi yaminika talqaf ma_ shana'u_ in nama_ shana'u_ kaidu_sa_hir wa la_ yuflihus sa_hiru haitsu ata_
Fa ulqiyas saharatu suj jadan qa_lu_ a_man na_ birab bi ha_ru_na wa mu_sa_
Qa_la a_mantum lahu_ qabla an a_dzana lakum in nahu_ lakabirukumul ladzi 'al lamakumus sihr fala uqath thi'an na aidiyakum wa arjulakum min khila_fiw wa la ushal liban nakum fi judzu_ in nakhli wa lata'lamun na ay yuna_ asyad du 'adza_baw wa abqa_
Qa_lu_ lan nutsiraka 'ala_ ma_ ja_'ana_ minal bay yina_ti wal ladzi fatharana_ faqdhi ma_ anta qa_dh innama_ taqdhi ha_dzihil haya_tad dunya_
In na_ a_man na_ birab bina_ liyaghfira lana_ khatha_ya_na_ wa ma_ akrahtana_ 'alaihi minas sihr wal la_hu khairuw wa abqa_
In nahu_ may ya'ti rab bahu_ mujriman fa in na lahu_ jahan nam la_ yamu_tu fiha_ wa la_ yahya_
Wa may ya'tihi mu'minan qad 'amilash sha_liha_ti fa ula_ ika lahumud daraja_tul 'ula_
Jan na_tu 'adnin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru kha_lidina fiha_ wa dza_lika jaza_ u man tazak ka_
Wa laqad aihaina_ ila_ mu_sa_ an asri bi'iba_di fadhrib lahum thariqan filbahri yabasal la_ takha_fu darakaw wa la_ takhsya_
Fa atba'ahum fir'aunu bijunu_dihi faghasyiyahum minal yam mi ma_ ghasyiyahum
Wa adhal la fir'aunu qaumahu_ wa ma_ hada_
Ya_ bani isra_ illa qad anjaina_kum min aduw wikum wa wa_'adna_kum ja_nibath thu_ril aimana wa naz zalna_ 'alaikumul man na was salwa_
Kulu_ min thay yiba_ti ma_ razaqna_kum wa la_ tathghau fihi fayahil la 'alaikum ghadhabi wa may yahlil 'alaihi ghadhabi faqad hawa_
Wa in ni laghaf fa_rul liman ta_ba wa a_mana wa 'amila sha_lihan sum mahtada_
Wa ma_ a'jalaka an qaumika ya_ mu_sa_
Qa_la hum ula_i 'ala_ atsari wa 'ajiltu ilaika rab bi litardha_
Qa_la fa in na_ qad fatan na_ qaumaka min ba'dika wa adhal lahumus sa_miriy
Faraja'a mu_sa_ ila_ qaumihi ghadhba_na asifa_ qa_la ya_ qaumi alam ya'idkum rab bukum wa'dan hasana_ afatha_la 'alaikumul ahdu am aradtum ay yahil la 'alaikum ghadhabum mir rab bikum fa akhlaftum mau'idi
Qa_lu_ ma_ akhlafna_ mau'idaka bimalkina_ wa la_kin na_ hum milna_ auza_ram min zinatil qaumi faqadzaf na_ha_ fakadza_lika alqas sa_miriy
Fa akhraja lahum ijlan jasadal lahu_ khuwa_run faqa_lu_ ha_dza_ ila_hukum wa ila_hu mu_sa_ fanasiya
Afala_ yarauna al la_ yarji'u ilaihim qaulaw wa la_ yamliku lahum dharraw wa la_ naf'a_
Wa laqad qa_la lahum ha_ru_nu min qablu ya_ qaumi in nama_ futintum bih wa in na rab bakumur rahma_nu fat tabi'u_ni wa athi'u_ amri
Qa_lu_ lan nabraha 'alaihi 'a_kifina hat ta_ yarji'a ilaina_ mu_sa_
Qa_la ya_ ha_ru_nu ma_ mana'aka idz ra aitahum dhal lu_
Al la_ tat tabi'an afa'ashaita amri
Qa_la yabna um ma la_ ta'khudz bilihyati wa la_ bira'si in ni khasyitu an taqu_la far raqta baina bani isra_ ila wa lam tarqub qauli
Qa_la fama_ khatbuka ya_sa_miriy
Qa_la bashurtu bima_ lam yabshuru_ bihi faqabadhtu qabdhatam min atsarir rasu_li fanabadz tuha_ wa kadza_lika saw walat li nafsi
Qa_la fadz hab fa in na laka fil haya_ti an taqu_la la_ misa_sa wa in na laka mau'idal lan tukhlafah wanzhur ila_ ila_hikal ladzi zhalta 'alaihi a_kifa_ lanuhar riqan nahu_ sum ma lanansifan nahu_ fil yam mi nasfa_
In nama_ ila_hukumul la_hul ladzi la_ ila_ha il la_ hu_ wasi'a kul la sai in 'ilma_
Kadza_lika naqush shu 'alaika min amba_i ma_ qad sabaq wa qad a_taina_ka mil ladun na_ zikra_
Man a'radha 'anhu fa in nahu_ yahmilu yaumal qiya_mati wizra_
Kha_lidina fih wa sa_ a lahum yaumal qiya_mati himla_
Yauma yunfakhu fis su_ri wa nahsyurul mujrimina yauma idzin zurqa_
Yatakha_fatu_na bainahum il labitstum il la_ asyra_
Nahnu a'lamu bima_ yaqu_lu_na idz yaqu_lu amtsaluhum thariqatan il labitstum il la_ yauma_
Wa yas alu_naka 'anil jiba_li faqul yansifuha_ rab bi nasfa_
Fayadzaruha_ qa_'an shafshafa_
La_ tara_ fiha_ iwajaw wa la_ amta_
Yauma idziy yat tabi'u_nad da_'iya la_ iwaja lah wa khasya'atil ashwa_tu lir rahma_ni fala_ tasma'u il la_ hamsa_
Yauma idzil la_ tanfa'usy syafa_'atu il la_ man adzina lahur rahma_nu wa radhiya lahu_ qaula_
Ya'lamu ma_ baina aidihim wa ma_ khalfahum wa la_ yuhithu_na bihi 'ilma_
Wa'anatil wuju_hu lilhay yil qay yu_m wa qad kha_ba hamala zhulma_
Wa may ya'mal minas sha_liha_ti wa huwa mu'minun fala_ yakha_fu zhulmaw wa la_ hadhma_
Wa kadza_lika anzalna_hu qur a_nan arabiy yaw wa shar rafna_ fihi minal wa'idi la'al lahum yat taqu_na au yuhditsu lahum zikra_
Fata'a_lal la_hul malikul haq wa la_ taj'al bil qur a_ni min qabli ay yuqdha_ ilaika wahyuhu_ wa qur rab bi zidni 'ilma_
Wa laqad 'ahidna_ ila_ a_dama min qablu fanasiya wa lam najid lahu_ azma_
Wa idz qulna_ lilmala_ ikatis judu_ li a_dama fasajadu_ il la_ iblis aba_
Faqulna_ ya_ a_damu in na_ ha_dza_ aduw wul laka wa lizaujika fala_ yukhrijan nakuma_ minal jan nati fatasqa_
In na laka al la_ taju_'a fiha_ wa la_ ta'ra_
Wa an naka la_ tazhma u fiha_ wa la_ tadha_
Fawaswasa ilaihis syaitha_nu qa_la ya_ a_damu hal adul luka 'ala_ syajaratil khuldi wa mulkil la_ yabla_
Fa akala_ minha_ fabadat lahuma_ sau a_tuhuma_ wa thafiqa_ yakhshifa_ni 'alaihima_ miw waraqil jan nati wa 'asha_ a_damu rab bahu_ faghawa_
Sum maj taba_hu rab buhu_ fata_ba 'alaihi wa hada_
Qa_lah bitha_ minha_ jami'an ba'dhukum liba'dhin 'aduw fa im ma_ ya'tiyan nakum min ni hudan famanit taba'a huda_ya fala_ yadhil lu wa la_ yasqa_
Wa man a'rada 'an dzikri fa in na lahu_ ma'isyatan dhankaw wa nahsyuruhu_ yaumal qiya_mati a'ma_
Qa_la rab bi lima hasyartani a'ma_ wa qad kuntu bashira_
Qa_la kadza_lika atatka a_ya_tuna_ fanasitaha_ wa kadza_likal yauma tunsa_
Wa kadza_lika najzi man asrafa wa lam yu'mim bi a_ya_ti rab bih wa la'adza_bul a_khirati asyad du wa abqa_
Afalam yahdi lahum kam ahlakna_ qablahum minal quru_ni yamsyu_na fi masa_kinihim in na fi dza_lika la a_ya_til li ulin nuha_
Wa laula_ kalimatun sabaqat mir rab bika laka-na li za_maw wa ajalum musam ma_
Fashbir 'ala_ ma_ yaqu_lu_na wa sab bih bihamdi rab bika qabla thulu_'is samsi wa qabla ghuru_biha_ wa min a_na_ il laili fasab bih wa athra_fannaha_ri la'al laka tardha_
Wa la_ tamud dan na 'ainaika ila_ ma_ mat ta'na_ bihi azwa_jam minhum zahratal haya_tid dun ya_ linaftinahum fih wa rizqu rab bika khairuw wa abqa_
Wa'mur ahlaka bis sa la_ti was thabir 'alaiha_ la_ nas aluka rizqa_ nahnu narzuquk wal 'a_qibatu lit taqwa_
Wa qa_lu_ laula_ ya'tina_ bi a_yatin mir rab bih awalam ta'ti him bay yinatu ma_ fis shuhufil u_la_
Wa lau an na- ahlakna_hum bi'adza_ bim min qablihi laqa_lu_ rab bana_ laula_ arsalta ilaina_ rasu_lan fanattabi'a a_ya_tika min qabli an nadzil la wa nakhza_
Qul kul lum mutarab bishun fatarab bashu_ fasata'lamu_na man ashsha_bush shira_this sawiy yi wa manih tada_
Iqtaraba lin na_si hisa_buhum wa hum fi gaflatim muridu_n
Ma_ yatihim min zikrim mir rab bihim muhdasin il las tamau_hu wa hum yalabu_n
La_hiyatan qulu_buhum wa asar run najwal lazina zalamu_ hal ha_za_ il la_ basarum afatatu_nas sihra wa antum tubsiru_n
Qa_la rab bi yalamul qaula fis sama_i wal ard wa huwas samiul alim
Bal qa_lu_ adga_su ahla_ mim balit tara_hu bal huwa sa_iru falya tina_ bi a_ya_tin kama_ ursilal aw walu_n
Ma_ a_mant qablahum min qaryatin ahlakna_ha_ afahum yuminu_n
Wa ma_ arsalna_ qablaka il la_ rija_lan nu_hi ilaihim fas alu_ ahlaz zikri in kuntum la_ talamu_n
Wa ma_ ja'alna_hum jasadal la_ yakulu_nat taa_ma wa ma_ ka_nu_ ha_lidin
Sum ma sadaqna_humul wada faanjaina_hum wa man nasa_u wa ahlaknal musrifin
Laqad anzalna_ ilaikum kita_ban fihi zikrukum afala_ taqilu_n
Wa kam qasamna_ min qaryatin ka_nat za_limataw wa ansana_ badaha_ qauman a_harin
Falam ma_ ahas su_ basana_ iza_ hum minha_ yarkudu_n
La_ tarkudu_ war ji u_ ila_ ma_ utriftum fihi wa masa_kinikum la'al lakum tus alu_n
Qa_lu_ ya_ wailana_ in na_ kun na_ za_limin
Fama_ za_lat tilka dawa_hum hat ta_ ja'alna_hum hasidan ha_midin
Wa ma_ halaqnas sama_a wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ la_ibin
Lau aradna_ an nat tahiza lahwal lat tahazna_hu mil ladun na_ in kun na_ fa_ilin
Bal naqzifu bil haq qi alal ba_tili fayadmauhu_ fa iza_ huwa za_hiq wa lakumul wailu mim ma_ tasifu_n
Wa la_hu_ manfis sama_wa_ti wal ard waman indahu_ la_ yastakbiru_na an iba_datihi wala_ yastahsiru_n
Yusab bihu_nal laila wan naha_ra la_ yafturu_n
Amit tahazu_ a_lihatam minal ardi hum yunsiru_n
Lau ka_na fihima_a_lihatun il lal la_hu lafasadata_ fasubha_nal la_hi rab bil arsi am ma_ yasifu_n
La_ yus alu am ma_ yafalu wa hum yus alu_n
Amit tahazu_ min du_nihi a_lihah qul ha_tu_ burha_nakum ha_za_ zikru mam maiya wa zikru man qahli bal aksaruhum la_ yalamu_nal haqa fahum muridu_n
Wa ma_ arsalna_ min qablika mir rasu_lin il la_ nu_hi ilaihi an nahu_ la_ ila_ha il la_ ana fabudu_n
Wa qa_lu tahazar rahma_nu waladan subha_nah bal iba_dum mukramu_n
La_ yasbiqu_nahu_ bil qauli wa hum bi amrihi yamalu_n
Yalamu ma_ baina aidihim wa ma_ halfahum wa la_ yasfau_na il la_ limanir tada_ wa hum min hasyatihi musfiqu_n
Wa may yaqul minhum in ni ila_hum min du_nihi faza_lika najzihi jahan nam kaza_lika najziz za_limin
Awalam yaral lazina kafaru_ an nas sama_wa_ti wal arda ka_nata_ ratqan fafataqna_huma_ wa ja'alna_ minal ma_i kul la sai in hay afala_ yuminu_n
Wa ja'alna_ fil ardi rawa_siya an tamida bihim wa ja'alna_ fiha_ fija_jan subulal la'al lahum yahtadu_n
Wa ja'alnas sama_a saqfam mahfu_zaw wa hum an a_ya_tiha_ muridu_n
Wa huwal lazi halaqal laila wan naha_ra was samsa wal qamar kul lun fi falakiy yasbahu_n
Wa ma_ ja'alna_ libasarim min qablikal huld afa im mit ta fahumul ha_lidu_n
Kul lu nafsin za_ iqatul maut wa nablu_kum bis sar ri wal hairi fitnah wa ilaina_ turjau_n
Wa iza_ ra a_kal lazina kafaru_ iy yat tahizu_naka il la_ huzu wa_ aha_zal lazi yazkuru a_lihatakum wa hum bizikrir rahma_ni hum ka_firu_n
Huliqal insa_nu min ajal sa urikum a_ya_ti fala_ tastajilu_n
Wa yaqu_lu_na mata_ ha_zal wadu in kuntum sa_diqin
Lau yalamul lazina kafaru_ hina la_ yakuf fu_na aw wuju_hihimun na_ra wa la_ an zuhu_rihim wa la_ hum yunsaru_n
Bal tatihim bagtatan fatabhatuhum fala_ yastatiu_na rad daha_ wa la_hum yunzaru_n
Wa laqadis tuhzi a birusulim min qablika faba_qa bil lazina sahiru_ minhum ma_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
Qul may yakla ukum bil laili wan naha_ri minar rahma_n bal hum an zikri rab bihim muridu_n
Am lahum a_lihatun tamnauhum min du_nina_ la_ yastatiu_na nasra anfusihim wa la_ hum min na_ yushabu_n
Bal mat tana_ ha_ ula_i wa a_ba_ ahum hat ta_ ta_la alaihimul umur afala_ yarauna an na_ natil arda nanqusuha_ min atra_fiha_ afahumul ga_libu_n
Qul in nama_ unzirukum bil wahyi wa la_ yasmaus sum mud dua_ a iza_ ma_ yunzaru_n
Wa la im mas sat hum nafhatum min aza_bi rab bika layaqu_lun na ya_ wailana_ in na_ kun na_ za_limin
Wa nadaul mawa_zinal qista liyaumil qiya_mati fala_ tuzlamu nafsun sai an wa in ka_na misqa_la hab batim min hardalin ataina_ biha_ wa kafa_ bina_ ha_sibin
Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sa_ wa ha_ru_nal furqa_na wa diya_ aw wa zikral lilmut taqin
Al lazina yahsauna rab bahum bil gaibi wa hum minas sa_ati musfiqu_n
Wa ha_za_ zikrum muba_rakun anzalna_h afa antum lahu_ munkiru_n
Wa laqad a_taina_ ibra_hima rusdahu_ min qablu wa kun na_ bihi a_limin
Iz qa_la li abihi wa qaumihi ma_ ha_zihit tama_silul lati antum laha_ a_kifu_n
Qa_lu_ wajadna_ a_ba_ ana laha_ a_bidin
Qa_la laqad kuntum antum wa a_ba_ ukum fi dala_lim mubin
Qa_lu_ ajitana_ bil haq qi am anta minal la_ibin
Qa_la bar rab bukum rab bus sama_wa_ti wal ardil lazi fatarahun na wa ama ala_ za_likum minas sa_hidin
Wa tal la_hi la akidan na asna_makum bada an tuwal lu_ mudbirin
Faja'alahum juza_zan il la_ kabiral lahum la'al lahum ilaihi yarjiu_n
Qa_lu_ man fa'ala ha_za_a bi a_lihatina_ in nahu_ laminaz za_limin
Qa_lu_ samina fatay yazkuru hum yuqa_lu lahu_ ibra_him
Qa_lu_ fatu_ bihi ala_ ayunin na_si la'al lahum yashadu_n
Qa_lu_ a anta fa'alta ha_za_ bi a_lihatina_ ya_ ibra_him
Qa_la bal fa'alahu_ kabiruhum ha_za_ fas aluhum in ka_nu_ yantiqu_n
Farajau_ ila_ anfusihim faqa_lu_ inakum antumuz za_limu_n
Sum ma nukisu_ ala ru u_sihim laqad alimta ma_ ha_ ula_i yantiqu_n
Qa_la afatabudu_na min du_nil la_hi ma_ la_ yanfaukum sai aw wa la_ yadur rukum
Uf fil lakum wa lima_ tabudu_na min du_nil la_h afala_ taqilu_n
Qa_lu_ har riqu_hu wan suru_ a_lihatakum in kuntum fa_ilin
Qulna_ ya_ na_ru ku_ni bardaw wa sala_man ala_ ibra_him
Wa ara_du bihi kaidan faja'alna_ humul ahsarin
Wa naj jaina_hu wa lu_tan ilal ardil lati ba_rakna_ fiha_ lila_lamin
Wa wahabna_ lahu_ is ha_q wa yaqu_ba na_filah wa kul lan ja'alna_ sa_lihin
Wa ja'alna_hum a im matay yahdu_na bi amrina_ wa auhaina_ ilaihim filal haira_ti wa iqa_mas sala_ti wa ita_ az zaka_h wa ka_nu_ lana_ a_bidin
Wa lu_tan a_taina_hu hukmaw wa ilmaw wa naj jaina_hu minal qaryatil lati ka_nat tamalul haba_ is in nahum ka_nu_ qauma sau in fa_siqin
Wa adhalna_hu fi rahmatina_ in nahu_ minas sa_lihin
Wa nu_han iz na_da_ min qablu fas tajabna_ lahu_ fanaj jaina_hu wa ah lahu_ minal karbil azim
Wa nasarna_hu minal qaumil lazina kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_tina_ in nahum ka_nu_ qauma sau in fa agraqna_hum ajmain
Wa da_wu_da wa sulaima_na iz yahkuma_ni fil harsi iz nafasat fihi ganamul qaum wa kun na_ lihukmihim sa_hidin
Fatah hamna_ha_ sulaima_n wa kul lan a_taina_ hukmaw wa ilmaw wasah harna_ ma'a da_wu_dal hiba_la yusab bihna wat tair wa kuna_ fa_ilin
Wa al lamna_hu sanata labu_sil lakum lituhsinakum min basikum fahal antum sa_kiru_n
Wa lisulaima_nar riha a_sifatan tajri bi amrihi ilal ardhil lati ba_rakna_ fiha_ wa kun na_ bikul li sai in a_li min
Wa minas saya_tini may yaghu_shu_na lahu_ wa ya'malu_na amalan du_na za_lik wa kun na_ lahum ha_fizin
Wa ay yu_ba iz na_da_ rab bahu_ an ni mas saniyad dur ru wa anta arhamur ra_himin
Fas tajabna_ lahu_ fakasyafna_ ma_ bihi min dur riw wa a_taina_hu ah lahu_ wa mitslahum ma'ahum rahmatam min 'indina_ wa zikra_ lil a_bidin
Wa isma_ila wa idrisa wa zal kifl kul lum minas sa_birin
Wa adkhalna_hum fi rahmatina_ in nahum minas sa_lihin
Wa zan nu_ni iz zahaba mugha_dhiban fazhan na al lan naqdira alaihi fana_da_ fiz zuluma_ti al la_ ila_ha il la_ anta subha_naka in ni kuntu minaz za_limin
Fas tajabna_ lahu_ wa naj jaina_hu minal gham wa kaza_lika nunjil mu'minin
Wa zakariy ya_ iz na_da_ rab bahu_ rab bi la_ tadzarni fardaw wa anta hairul wa_risin
Fas tajabna_ lah wa wahabna_ lahu_ yahya_ wa aslahna_ lahu_ zaujah in nahum ka_nu_ yusa_riu_na fil haira_ti wa yadu_nana_ raghabaw wa rahaba_ wa ka_nu_ lana_ ha_si'in
Wal lati ahsanat farjaha_ fanafakna_ fiha_ mir ru_hina_ wa ja'alna_ha_ wab naha_ a_yatal lil'a_lamin
In na ha_zihi um matukum um mataw wa_hidataw wa ana rab bukum fa'budu_n
Wa taqat ta'u_ amrahum bainahum kul lun ilaina_ ra_ji'u_n
Famay ya'mal minas sa_liha_ti wa huwa mu'minun fala_ kufra_na lisa'yih wa in na_ lahu_ ka_tibu_n
Wa hara_mun 'ala_ qaryatin ahlakna_ha_ an nahum la_ yarji'u_n
Hat ta_ iza_ futihat ya'ju_ju wa ma ju_ju wa hum min kul li badabiy yansilu_n
Waq tarabal wa'dul haq qu fa iza_ hiya sa_khishatun absa_rul lazina kafaru_ ya_wailana_ qad kun na_ fi ghaflatim min ha_za_ bal kun na_ za_limin
In nakum wa ma_ ta'budu_na min du_nil la_hi hashabu jahan nam antum laha_ wa_ridu_n
Lau ka_na ha_ ula_i a_lihatam ma_ waradu_ha_ wa kul lun fiha_ kha_lidu_n
Lahum fiha_ zafiruw wa hum fiha_ la_ yasma'u_n
In nal lazina sabaqat lahum min nal husna_ ula_ ika 'anha_ mub'adu_n
La_ yasma'u_na hasisaha_ wa hum fi mas tahat anfusuhum kha_lidu_n
La_ yahzunuhumul faza'ul akbaru wa tatalaq qa_humul mala_ ikah ha_za_ yaumukumul lazi kuntum tu_'adu_n
Yauma nathwis sama_ a kathay yis sijil li lilkutub kama_ badana_ aw wala khalqin nu'iduh wa dan 'alaina_ in na_ kun na_ fa_'ilin
Wa laqad katabna_ fiz zabu_ri mim ba'diz zikri an nal arda yaritsuha_ iba_diyas sa_lihu_n
In na fi ha_za_ labala_ghal liqaumin 'a_bidin
Wa ma_ arsalna_ka il la_ rahmatal lil'a_lamin
Qul in nama_ yu_ha_ ilay ya an nama_ ila_hukum ila_huw wa_hid fahal antum muslimu_n
Fa in tawal lau faqul a_zantukum 'ala_ sawa_ in wa in adri aqaribun am ba'idum ma_ tu_'adu_n
In nahu_ ya'lamul jahra minal qauli wa ya'lamu ma_ taktumu_n
Wa in adri la'al lahu_ fitnatul lakum wa mata_'un ila_ hin
Qa_la rab bih kum bil haq wa rab bunar rahma_nul musta'a_nu 'ala_ ma_ tashifu_n
Ya_ ay yuhan na_sut taqu_ rab bakum in na zal zalatas sa_'ati sai un azim
Yauma taraunaha_ tadzhalu kul lu murdi'atin am ma_ arda'at wa ta da'u kul lu za_ti hamlin hamlaha_ wa taran na_sa suka_ra_ wa ma_ hum bisuka_ra_ wa la-kin na 'aza_bal la_hi sadid
Wa minan na_si may yuja_dilu fil la_hi bighairi ilmiw wa yat tabi'u kul la saita_nim marid
Kutiba alaihi an nahu_ man tawal la_hu fa an nahu_ yudhil luhu_ wa yahdihi ila_ aza_bis sa'ir
Ya_ ay yuhan na_su in kuntum fi raibihim minal ba'tsi fa in na_ khalaqna_kum min tura_bin sum ma min nutfatin sum ma min alaqatin sum ma min mudghatim mukhal laqatiw wa gairi mukhal laqatil linubay yina lakum wa nuqir ru fil arha_mi ma_ nasya_ u ila_ ajalim musam man sum ma nukhrijukum thiflan sum ma litablughu_ asyud dakum wa minkum may yutawaf fa_ wa minkum may yurad du ila_ arzalil umuri likaila_ ya'lama min ba'di ilmin sai a_ wa taral arda ha_midatan fa iza_ anzalna_ alaihal ma_ ah taz zat wa rabat wa ambatat min kul li zaujin bahij
Za_lika bi an nal la_ha huwal haq qu wa an nahu_ yuhyil mauta_ wa an nahu_ 'ala_ kul li sai in qadir
Wa an nas sa_'ata a_tiyatul la_ raiba fiha_ wa an nal la_ha yab'atsu man fil qubu_r
Wa minan na_si may yuja_dilu la_hi bigairi ilmiw wa la_ hudaw wa la_ kita_bim munir
Sa_niya 'ithfihi liyudhil la an sabilil la_h lahu_ fid dun ya_ khizyuw wa nudziquhu_ yaumal qiya_mati aza_bal hariq
Za_lika bima_ qad damat yada_ka wa an nal la_ha laisa bizhalla_mil lil'abid
Wa minan na_si may ya'budul la_ha 'ala_ harf fa in asha_bahu_ khairunit ma an na bih wa in asha_bat hu fitnatunin qalaba 'ala_ wajhih khasirad dun ya_ wal a_khirah za_lika huwal khusra_nul mubin
Yad'u_ min du_nil la_hi ma_ la_ yadur ruhu_ wa ma_ la_ yanfa'uh, za_lika huwad dala_lul ba'id
Yad'u_ laman dar ruhu_ aqrabu min naf'ih labi'sal maula_ wa labi'sal asir
In nal la_ha yudkhilul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_r in nal la_ha yaf'alu ma_ yurid
Man ka_na yazhun nu al lay yanshurahul la_hu fid dun ya_ wal a_khirati fal yamdud bisababin ilas sama_i sum mal yaqta falyanzur hal yuz hiban na kaiduhu_ ma_ yaghiz
Wa kaza_lika anzalna_hu a_ya_tim bay yina_tiw wa an nal la_ha yahdil may yurid
In nal lazina a_manu_ wal lazina ha_du_ was sa_bi ina wan nasha_ra_ wal maju_sa wal lazina asraku_ in nal la_ha yafshilu bainahum yaumal qiya_mah in nal la_ha 'ala_ kul li sai in sahid
Alam tara an nal la_ha yasjudu lahu_ man fis sama_wa_ti wa man fil ardi was samsu wal qamaru wan nuju_ mu wal jiba_lu was sajaru wad dawa_b bu wa kasirum minan na_s wa kasirun haq qa 'alaihil aza_b wa may yuhinil la_hu fama_ lahu_ mim mukrim in nal la_ha yaf'alu ma_ yasya_
Ha_za_ni hasma_nikh tashamu_ fi rab bihim fal lazina kafaru_ qut ti'at lahum siya_bum mina_riy yushab bu min fauqi ru u_sihimul hamim
Yusharu bihi ma_ fi buthu_nihim wal julu_d
Wa lahum maqa_mi'u min hadid
Kul lama_ ara_du_ ay yakhruju_ minha_ min gham min u'idu_ fiha_ wa zu_qu_ aza_bal hariq
In nal la_ha yudkhilul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru yuhal launa fiha_ min asa_wira min zahabiw wa lu lu'a_ wa liba_suhum fiha_ harir
Wa hudu_ ilat tay yibi minal qaul wa hudu_ ila_ sira_til hamid
In nal lazina kafaru_ wa yashudu_na an sabilil la_hi wal masjidil hara_mil lazi ja'alna_hu lin na_si sawa_ anil 'a_kifu fihi wal ba_d wa may yurid fihi bi ilha_dim bizhulmin nudziqhu min 'aza_bin alim
Wa iz baw wa'na_ li ibra_hima maka_nal baiti al la_ tusrik bi sai aw wa tah hir baitiya lit ta_ ifina wal qa_ imina war ruk ka'is suju_d
Wa az zin fin na_si bil haj ji ya'tu_ka rija_law wa 'ala_ kul li da_miriy ya'tina min kul li faj jin amiq
Liyasnadu_ mana_fi'a lahum wayazkurus mal la_hi fi ay ya_mim ma'lu_ma_tim 'ala_ ma_ razaqahum mimbahimatil an'a_mi fakulu_ minha_ wa at'imul ba_ isal faqir
Sum mal yaqdu_ tafatsahum wal yu_fu_ nudzu_rahum walyat taw wafu_ bil baitil atiq
Za_lika, wa may yu'az zhim huruma_til la_hi fahuwa hairul lahu_ indarab bihi wa uhil lat lakumul an'a_mi il la_ ma_ yutla_ alaikum fajtanibur rijsa minal autsa_ni wajtanibu_ qaulaz zu_r
Hunafa_ a lil la_hi ghaira musrikina bihi wa may yusrik bil la_hi faka_an nama_ khar ra minas sama_i fatakhthafuhuth thairu au tahwi bihir rihu fi maka_nin sahiq
Za_lika wa may yu'az zhim sa'a_iral la_hi fa in naha_ min taqwal qulu_b
Lakum fiha_ mana_fi'u ila_ ajalim musam man sum ma mahil luha_ ilal baitil 'atiq
Wa likul li um matin ja'alna_ mansakal liyazkurus mal la_hi 'ala_ ma_ razaqahum mim bahimatil an'a_m fa ila_ hukum ila_huw wa_hidun falahu_ aslimu_ wa bas siril mukhbitin
Alazina iza_ zukiral la_hu wajilat qulu_buhum was sa_birina 'ala_ ma_ asha_bahum wal muqimis sala_ti wa mim ma_ razaqna_hum yunfiqu_n
Wal budna ja'alna_ha_ lakum min sa'a_ril la_hi lakum fiha_ khairun fazkurus mal la_hi 'alaiha_ sawa_f fa iza_ wajabat junu_buha_ fakulu_ minha_ wa at'imul qa_ni'a wal mu'tar kaza_lika sakh kharna_ha_ lakum la'al lakum taskurun
Lay yana_lal la_ha luhu_muha_ wa la_ dima_ uha_ wa la_kiy yana_luhut taqwa_ minkum kaza_lika sakh  kharaha_ lakum litukab birul la_ha 'ala_ ma_ hada_kum wa bas siril muhsinin
In nal la_ha yuda_fi'u anil lazina a_manu_ in nal la_ha la_ yuhib bukul la khaw wa_nin kafu_r
Uzina lil lazina yuqa_talu_na bi an nahum zulimu_ wa in nal la_ha 'ala_ nasrihim laqadir
Nil lazina ukhriju_ min diya_rihim bigairi haq qin il la_ ay yaqu_lu_ rab bunal la_h wa laula_ daf'ul la_hin na_sa ba'dahum biba'dil lahud dimat sawa_mi'u wa biya'uw wa salawa_tuw wa masa_jidu yuzkaru fihas mul la_hi katsira_ wa layanshuran nal la_hu may yansuruh in nal la_ha laqawiy yun 'aziz
Al lazina im mak kan na_hum fil ardi aqa_mus sala_ta wa a_tuz zaka_ta wa amaru_ bil ma'ru_fi wa nahau anil munkar wa lil la_hi 'a_qibatul umu_r
Wa iy yukaz zibu_ka faqad kadzabat qablahum qaumu nu_hiw wa 'a_duw wa samu_d
Wa qaumu ibra_hima wa qaumu lu_t
Wa asha_bu mad yan wa kuz ziba mu_sa_ fa amlaitu lilka_firina sum ma akhaztuhum fakaifa ka_na nakir
Faka ay yim min qaryatin ahlakna_ha_ wa hiya za_limatun fahiya kha_wiyatun 'ala_ uru_syiha_ wa bi'rim mu'at talatiw wa qasrim masyid
Afalam yasiru_ fil ardi fataku_na lahum qulu_buy ya'qilu_na biha_ au a_za_nuy yasma'u_na biha_ fa in naha_ la_ ta'mal absa_ru wa la_kin ta'mal qulu_bul lati fis sudu_r
Wa yasta'julu_naka bil'aza_bi wa lay yukhifal la_hu wa'dahu_ wa in na yauman 'inda rab bika ka alfi sanatim mim ma_ ta'ud du_n
Wa ka ay yim min qaryatin amlaitu laha_ wa hiya za_limatun sum ma akhadztuha_ wa ilay yal masir
Qul ya_ ay yuhan na_su in nama_ ana_ lakum nadzirum mubin
Fal lazina a_manu_ wa 'amilus sa_liha_ti lahum magfiratuw wa rizqun karim
Wal lazina sa'aufi a_ya_tina_ mu'a_jizina ula_ ika asha_bul jahim
Wa ma_ arsalna_ min qablika mir rasu_liw wa la_ nabiy yin il la_ iza_ taman na_ alqas saitha_nu fi umniy yatih fayansakul la_hu ma_ yulqis saita_nu sum ma yukhkimul lahu a_ya_tih wal la_hu 'alimun hakim
Liyaj'ala ma_ yulqis saita_nu fit natal lil lazina fi qulu_bihim maraduw wal qa_siyati qulu_buhum wa in naz za_limina lafi siqa_qim ba'id
Wa liya lamal lazina u_tul 'ilma an nahul haq qu mir rab bika fayu'minu_ bihi fatukbita lahu_ qulu_buhum wa in nal la_ha laha_dil lazina a_manu_ ila_ sira_tim mustaqim
Wa la_ yaza_hul lazina kafaru_ fi miryatim minhu hat ta_ ta'tiyahumus sa_'atu bagtatan au ya'tiyahum 'aza_bu yaumin 'aqim
Almulku yauma izil lil la_h yahkumu bainahum fal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti fi jan na_tin naim
Wal lazina kafaru_ wa kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_tina_ fa ula_ ika lahum aza_bum muhin
Wal lazina ha_jaru_ fi sabilil la_hi sum ma qutilu_ au ma_tu_ layarzuqan nahumul la_hu rizqan hasana_ wa in nal la_ha lahuwa hairur ra_ziqin
Layudhilan nahum mudhalay yardaunahu_ wa in nal la_ha la'alimun halim
Za_lika wa man 'a_qaba bimitsli ma_ 'u_qiba bihi sum ma bugiya 'alaihi layansuran nahul la_h in nal la_ha la'afuw wun gafu_r
Za_lika bi an nal la_ha yu_lijul laila fin naha_ri wa yu_lijun naha_ra fil laili wa an nal la_ha sami'um basir
Za_lika bi an nal la_ha huwal haq qu wa an na ma_ yad'u_na min du_nihi huwal ba_tilu wa an nal la_ha huwal 'aliy yul kabir
Alam tara an nal la_ha abzala minas sama_i ma_ an fatusbihul ardu mukhdar rah in nal la_ha latifun habir
Lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard wa in nal la_ha lahuwal ganiy yul hamid
Alam tara an nal la_ha sak kara lakum ma_ fil ardi wal fulka tajri fil bahri bi amrihi wa yumsikus sama_ a an taqa'a 'alal ardi il la_ bi iznih in nal la_ha bin na_si lara u_fur rahim
Wa huwal lazi ahya_kum sum ma yumitukum sum ma yuhyikum in nal insa_na lakafu_r
Likul li um matin ja'alna_ mansakan hum na_siku_hu fala_ yuna_zi un naka fil amri wad'u ila_ rab bik in naka la ala_ hudam mustaqim
Wa in ja_dalu_ka faqulil la_hu a'lamu bima_ ta'malu_n
Al la_hu yahkumu bainakum yaumal qiya_mati fima_ kuntum fihi tahtalifu_n
Alam ta'lam an nal la_ha ya'lamu ma_ fis sama_i wal ardi in na za_lika fi kita_b in na za_lika 'alal la_hi yasir
Wa ya'budu_na min du_nil la_hi ma_ lam yunaz zil bihi sulta_naw wa ma_ laisa lahum bihi 'ilm wa ma_ liz za_limina min nasir
Wa iza_ tutla_ 'alaihim a_ya_tuna_ bay yina_tin ta'rifu fi wuju_hil lazina kafarul munkar yaka_du_na yastu_na bil lazina yatlu_na alaihim a_ya_tina_ qul afa unab bi ukum bisar rim min za_likum ana_r wa adahal la_hul lazina kafaru_ wa bisal masir
Ya_ ay yuhan na_su duriba matsalun fastami'u_ lah in nal lazina tad'u_na min du_nil la_hi lay yahluqu_ zuba_baw wa lawij tama'u_ lah wa iy yaslubhumuz zuba_bu sai al la_ yastanqizu_hu min da'ufat ta_libu wal matlu_b
Ma_ qadarul la_ha haq qa qadrih in nal la_ha laqawiy yun aziz
Al la_hu yastafi minal mala_ ikati rusuluw wa minan na_s in nal la_ha sami'um basir
Ya'lamu ma_ baina aidihim wa ma_ halfahum wa ilal la_hi turja'ul umu_r
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ ka'u_ was judu_ wa budu_ rab bakum waf 'alul haira la'al lakum tuflihu_n
Wa ja_hidu_ fil la_hi haq qa jiha_dih huwaj taba_kum wa ma_ ja'ala 'alikum fid dini min haraj mil lata abikum ibra_him huwa sam ma_kumul muslimina min qablu wa fi ha_za_ liyaku_nar rasu_lu sahidan 'alaikum wa taku_nu_ suhada_ a 'alan na_s fa aqimus sala_ta wa a_tuz zaka_ta wa tasimu_ bil la_h huwa maula_kum fani'mal maula_ wa ni'man nasir
Qad aflahal muminu_n
Al lazinahum fi sala_tihim ha_siu_n
Wal lazinahum anil lagwi muridu_n
Wal lazinahum liz zaka_ti fa_ilu_n
Wal lazinahum lifuru_jihim ha_fizu_n
Il la_ ala_ azwa_jihim au ma_ malakat aima_nuhum fa in nahum gairu malu_min
Famanib taga_ wara_ a za_lika fa ula_ ika humul a_du_n
Wal lazinahum li ama_na_tihim wa ahdihim ra_u_n
Wal lazinahum ala_ salawa_tihim yuha_fizu_n
Ula_ ika humul wa_risu_n
Al lazina yarisu_nal firdaus hum fiha_ ha_lidu_n
Wa laqad halaqnal insa_na min sula_latim min tin
Sum ma jaalna_hu nutfaran fi qara_rim makin
Sum ma halaqnan nutfata alaqatan fahalaqnal alaqata mudgatan fahalaqnal mudgata iza_man fa kasaunal iza_ma lahma_ sum ma ansana_hu halqan a_har fataba_rakal la_hu ahsanul ha_liqin
Sum ma in nakum bada za_lika lamay yitu_n
Sum ma in nakum yaumal qiya_mati tubasu_n
Wa laqad halaqna_ fauqakum saba tara_iq wa ma_ kun na_ anil halqi ga_filin
Wa anzalna_ minas sama_i ma_ am biqadarin fa askan na_hu fil ard wa in na_ ala_ zaha_bin bihi laqa_diru_n
Fa ansana_ lakum bihi jan na_tim min nakhiliw wa ana_b lakum fiha_ fawa_kihu katsiratuw wa minha_ takulu_n
Wa sajaratan tahruju min tu_ri saina_a tan butu bid duhni wa sibgil lil a_kilin
Wa in na lakum fil ana_mi laibrah nusqikum mim ma_ fi butu_niha_ walakum fiha_ mana_fiu katsiratuw wa minha_ takulu_n
Wa alaiha wa alal fulki tuhmalu_n
Wa laqad arsalna_ nu_han il la_ qaumihi faqa_la ya_qaumi budul la_ha ma_ lakum min ila_hin gairuh afala_ tataqu_n
Faqa_lal mala ul lazina kafaru_ min qaumihi ma_ ha_za_ il la_ basarum mitslukum yuridu ay yatafad dala alaikum walau sa_ al la_hu la anzala mala_ ikatam ma_ samina_ biha_za_ fi a_ba_ inal aw walin
In huwa il la_ rajulum bihi jin natun fatarab basu_ bihi hat ta_ hin
Qa_la rab bin surni bima_ kaz zabu_n
Fa auhaina_ ilaihi anis naif fulka biayunina_ wa wahyina_ fa iza_ ja_a amruna_ wa fa_rat tan nu_ru fasluk fiha_ min kul lin zaujanis naini wa ahlaka il la_ man sabaqa alaihil qaulu minhum wa la_ tuha_tibni fil lazina zalamu_in nahum mugraqu_n
Fa izas tawaita anta wa mam maaka alal fulki faqulil hamdu lil la_hil lazi naj ja_na_ minal qaumiz za_limin
Wa qur rab bi anzilni munzalam muba_rakaw wa anta hairul munzilin
In na fi za_lika la a_ya_tiw wa in kun na_ lamubtalin
Sum ma ansana_ min badihim qar nan a_kharin
Fa arsalna_ fihim rasu_lam minhum anibudul laha ma_ lakum min ila_hin gairuh afala_ tat taqu_n
Wa qa_lal mala u min qaumihi lazina kafaru_ wa kaz zabu_ biliqa_ il a_khirati wa atrafna_hum fil haya_tid dun ya_ ma_ ha_za_ il la_ basarum mitslukum yakulu mim ma_ takulu_na minhu wa yasrabu mim ma_ tasrabu_n
Wa la in atatum basaram mitslakum in nakum izal laka_siru_n
Ayaidukum an nakum iza_ mit tum wa kuntum tura_baw wa iza_man an nakum mukhraju_n
Haiha_ta haiha_ta lima_ tu_adu_n
In hiya il la_ haya_tunad dun ya_ namu_tu wa nahya_ wa ma_ nahnu bimabu_sin
In huwa il la_ rajulunif tara_ alal la_hi kazibaw wa ma_ nahnu lahu_ bi muminin
Qa_la rab bin surni bima_ kaz zabu_n
Qa_la  am ma_ qalilil layusbinun na na_dimin
Fa akhazatumus saihatu bil haq qi faja'alna_hum gutsa_ a fabudal lil qaumiz za_limin
Sum ma ansana_ min badihim quru_nan a_kharin
Ma_ tasbiqu min um matin ajalaha_ wa ma_ yastahiru_n
Sum ma arsalna_ rusulana_ tatra_ kul lama_ ja_a um matar rasu_luha_ kaz zabu_hu fa atbana_ badahum badaw wa ja'alna_ hum aha_dis fa budal liqaumil la_ yuminu_n
Sum ma_ arsalna_ mu_sa_ wa akha_hu ha_ru_na bi a_ya_tina_ wa sulta_nim mubin
Ila_ firauna wa mala ihi fas takbaru_ wa ka_nu_ qauman a_lin
Faqa_lu_ anuminu libasaraini mitslina_ wa qaumuhuma_ lana_ a_bidu_n
Fakaz zabu_huma_ faka_nu_ minal muhlakin
Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sal kita_ba la'al lahum yahtadu_n
Wa ja'alnab na maryama wa um mahu_ a_yataw wa a_waina_huma_ ila_ rabwatin za_ti qara_riw wa main
Ya_ ay yuhar rasulu kulu_ minat tay yiba_ti wa malu_ sa_liha_ in ni bima_ tamalu_na alim
Wa in na ha_zihi um matukum um mataw wa_hidataw wa ana_ rab bukum fat taqu_n
Faqat tau_ amrahum bainahum zubura_ kul lu hizbin bima_ ladaihim farihu_n
Fazarhum fi gamratihim hat ta_ hin
Ayahsabu_na an nama_ numid du hum bihi mim ma_liw wa banin
Nusa_ri'u lahum fil haira_t bal la_ yasuru_n
In nal lazina hum min has yati rab bihim musfiqu_n
Wal lazina hum bi a_ya_ti rab bihim yuminu_n
Wal lazina hum birab bihim la_ yusriku_n
Wal lazina yutu_na ma_ a_tauw wa qulu_buhum wajilatun an nahum ila_ rab bihim ra_jiu_n
Ula_ ika yusa_riu_na fil haira_ti wa hum laha_ sa_biqu_n
Wa la_ nukal lifu nafsan il la_ wusaha_ wa ladaina_ kita_buy yantiqu bil haq qi wa hum la_ yuzlamu_n
Bal qulu_buhum fi gamratim min ha_za_ wa lahum ama_lum min du_ni za_lika hum laha_ a_milu_n
Hat ta_ iza_ akhazna_ mutrafihim bil aza_bi iza_ hum yaj aru_n
La_ taj arul yaum in nakum min na_ la_ tunsaru_n
Qad ka_nat a_ya_ti tutla_ alaikum fakuntum ala_ aqa_bikum tankisu_n
Mustakbirin bihi sa_miran tahjuru_n
Afalam yad dab barul qaula am ja_ ahum ma_ lam yati a_ba_ ahumul aw walin
Am lam yarifu_ rasu_lahum fahum lahu_ munkiru_n
Am yaqu_lu_na bihi jin nah bal ja_ ahum bil haq qi wa aksaruhum lilhaq qi ka_rihu_n
Wa lawit taba'al haq qu ahwa_ ahum lafasadatis sama_wa_tu wal ardu wa man fihin bal ataina_hum bizikrihim fahum an zikrihim muridu_n
Am tas aluhum harjan fakhara_ju rab bika hairuw wa huwa hairur ra_ziqin
Wa in naka latadu_hum ila_ sira_tim mustaqim
Wa in nal lazina la_ yuminu_na bil a_khirati anis sira_ti lana_kibu_n
Wa lau rahimna_hum wa kasafna_ ma_ bihim min dur ril lalaj ju_ fi tugya_nihim yamahu_n
Wa laqad akhazna_hum bil aza_bi famas taka_nu_ lirab bihim wa ma_ yatadar rau_n
Hat ta_ iza_ fatahna_ alaihim ba_ban za_ aza_bin sadidin iza_ hum fihi mublisu_n
Wa huwal lazi ansa a lakumus sama wal absa_ra wal af idah qalilam ma_ taskuru_n
Wa huwal lazi zara akum fil ardi wa ilaihi tuhsaru_n
Wa huwal lazi yuhyi wa yumitu wa lahuh tila_ful laili wan naha_r afala_ taqilu_n
Bal qa_lu_ mitsla ma_ qa_lal aw walu_n
Qa_lu_ a iza_ mitna_ wa kun na_ tura_baw wa iza_man a in na_ lamabu_su_n
Laqad wuidna_ nahnu wa a_ba_ una_ ha_za_ min qablu in ha_za_ il la_ asa_tirul aw walin
Qul limanil ardu wa man fiha_ in kuntum talamu_n
Sayaqu_lu_na lil la_h qul afala_ tazak karu_n
Qul mar rab bus sama_wa_tis sabi wa rab bul arsil azim
Sayaqu_lu_na lil la_h qul afala_ tataqu_n
Qul man biyadihi malaku_tu kul li sai iw wa huwa yujiru wa la_ yuja_ru alaihi in kuntum talamu_n
Sayaqu_lu_na lil la_h qul fa an na_ tus haru_n
Bal ataina_hum bil haq qi wa in nahum laka_zibu_n
Mat tahazal la_hu miw waladiw wa ma_ ka_na maahu_ min ila_hin izal lazahaba kul lu ila_hin bima_ halaqa wa la'ala_ baduhum ala_ bad subha_nal la_hi am ma_ yasifu_n
A_limil gaibi was saha_dati fataa_ la_ am ma_ yusriku_n
Qur rab bi ma_ turiyan ni ma_ yu_adu_n
Rab bi fala_ tajalni fil qaumiz za_limin
Wa in na_ ala_ an nuriyaka ma_ naiduhum laqa_diru_n
Idfa bil lati hiya ahsanus say yi ah nahnu alamu bima_ yasifu_n
Wa qur rab bi au_zu bika min ha maza_tis saya_tin
Wa au_zu bika rab bi ay yahduru_n
Hat ta_ iza_ja_ a ahada humul mautu qa_la rab birjiu_n
La'al li amalu sa_lihan fima_ taraktu kal la_ in naha_ kalimatun huwa qa_ iluha_ wa miw wara_ ihim barzahun ila_ yaumi yubasu_n
Fa iza_ nufiha fisisu_ri fala_ ansa_ba bainahum yauma iziw wa la_ yatasa_ alu_n
Faman saqulat mawa_zinuhu_ fa ula_ ika humul muflihu_n
Wa man haf fat mawa_zinuhu_ fa ula_ikal lazina hasiru_ anfusahum fi jahan nama ha_lidu_n
Talfahu wuju_hahumun na_ru wa hum fiha_ ka_lihu_n
Alam takun a_ya_ti tutla_ alaikum fakuntum biha_ tukaz zibu_n
Qa_lu_ rab bana_ galabat alaina_ siqwatuna_ wa kun na_ qauman da_l lin
Rab bana_ ahrijna_ minha_ fa in udna_ fa in na_ za_limu_n
Qa_lah sa u_ fiha_ wa la_ tukal limu_n
In nahu_ ka_na fariqum min iba_di yaqu_lu_na rab bana_ a_man na_ fagfir lana_ war hamna_ wa anta hairur ra_himin
Fat tahaztumu_hum sihriy yan hat ta_ ansaukum zikri wa kuntum minhum tadhaku_n
In ni jazaituhumul yauma bima_ sabaru_ an nahum humul fa_ izu_n
Qa_la kam labistum fil ardi adadasinin
Qa_lu_ labisna_ yauman au bada yaumin fas alil a_d din
Qa_la il labistum il la_ qalilal lau an nakum kuntum talamu_n
Afahasibtum an nama_ halaqna_kum abasaw wa an nakum ilaina_ la_ turjau_n
Fataa_lal la_hul malikul haq la_ ila_ha il la_ hu rab bul arsil karim
Wa may yadu maal la_hi ila_han a_hara la_ burha_na lahu_ bihi fa in nama_ hisa_buhu_ inda rab bih in nahu_ la_ yuflihul ka_firu_n
Wa qur rab big fir war ham wa anta hairur ra_himin
Su_ratun anzalna_ha_ wa faradna_ha_ wa anzalna_ fiha_ a_ya_tin bay yina_til la'al lakum tazak karu_n
Az za_niyatu waz za_ni faj lidu_ kul la wa_hidim minhuma_ miata jaldatiw wa la_ tahuzkum bihima_ rafatun fi dinil la_hi in kuntum tuminu_na bil la_hi wal yaumil a_khir wal yashad aza_bahuma_ ta_ ifatum minal muminin
Az za_ni la_ yankihu il la_ za_niyatan au musrikataw waz za_niyatu la_ yankihuha_ il la_ za_nin au musrik wa hur rima za_lika alal muminin
Wal lazina yarmu_nal muhsana_ti sum ma lam yatu_ bi arba'ati suhada_ a faj lidu_hum sama_nina jaldataw wa la_ taqbalu_ lahum saha_datan abada_ wa ula_ ika humul fa_siqu_n
Il lal lazina ta_bu_ mim badi za_lika wa aslahu_ fa in nal la_ha gafu_rur rahim
Wal lazina yarmu_na azwa_jahum wa lam yakul lahum suhada_ u il la_ a usuhum fasaha_datu ahadihim arbau saha_da_tim bil la_hi in nahu_ laminas sa_diqin
Wal ha_misatu an na lanatal la_hi alaihi in ka_na minal ka_zibin
Wa yadra u anhal aza_ba an tashada arba'a saha_da_tim bil la_hi in nahu_ laminal ka_zibin
Wal ha_misata an na gadabal la_hi alaiha_ in ka_na minas sa_diqin
Wa lau la_ fadlul la_hi alaikum wa rahmatuhu_ wa an nal la_ha taw wa_bun hakim
In nal lazina ja_u_ bil ifki usbatum minkum la_ tahsabu_hu sar ral lakum bal huwa hairul lakum likul lim ri im minhum mak tasaba minal ismi wal lazi tawal la_ kibrahu_ minhum lahu_ aza_bun azim
Lau la_ iz samitumu_hu zan nal muminu_na wal mumina_tu bi anfusihim hairaw wa qa_lu_ ha_za_ ifkum mubin
Lau la_ ja_ u_ alaihi bi arbaati suhada_ fa iz lam yatu_ bis suhada_i fa ula_ ika indal la_hi humul ka_zibu_n
Wa lau la_ fadlul la_hi alaikum wa rahmatuhu_ fid dun ya_ wal a_hirati lamas sakum fi ma_ afadtum fihi aza_bun azim
Iz talaq qaunahu_ bi alsinatikum wa taqu_lu_na bi afwa_hikum ma_ laisa lakum bihi ilmuw wa tahsabu_nahu_ hay yinaw wa huwa indal la_hi azim
Wa lau la_ iz samitumu_hu qultum ma_ yaku_nu lana_ an natakal lama biha_za_ subha_naka ha_za_ buhta_nun azim
Yaizhukumul la_hu an tau_du_ limislihi abadan in kuntum muminin
Wa yubay yinul la_hu lakumul a_ya_ti wal la_hu alimun hakim
In nal lazina yuhib bu_na an tasyial fa_hisatu fi lazina a_manu_ lahum aza_bun alimun fid dun ya_ wal a_khirah wal la_hu yalamu wa antum la_ talamu_n
Wa lau la_ fadlul la_hi alaikum wa rahmatuhu_ wa an nal la_ha ra u_fur rahim
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ tat tabiu_ hutuwa_tis saita_n wa may yat tabi hutuwa_tis saita_ni fa in nahu_ yamuru bil fahsa_i wal munkar wa lau la_ fadlul la_hi alaikum wa rahmatuhu_ ma_ zaka_ minkum min ahadin abadaw wa la_kin nal la_ha yuzak ki may yasya_ wal la_hu samiun alim
Wa la_ yatali ulul fadli minkum was sa'ati ay yu tu_ ulul qurba_ wal masa_kina wal muha_jirina fi sabilil la_hi wal yafu_ wal yasfahu_ ala_ tuhibu_na ay yagfiral la_hu lakum wal la_hu gafu_rur rahim
In nal lazina yarmu_nal muhsana_til ga_fila_til mumina_ti luinu_ fid dun ya_ wal a_hirah wa lahum aza_bun azim
Yauma tashadu alaihim alsinatahum wa aidihim wa arjuluhum bima_ ka_nu_ yamalu_n
Yauma iziy yuwaf fihimul la_hu dinahumul haq qa wa yalamu_na an nal la_ha huwal haq qul mubin
Alhabisa_tu lilhabisina wal habisu_na lil habisa_t wat tay yiba_tu lit tay yibina wat tay yibu_na lit tay yiba_t ula_ ika mubara u_na mim ma_ yaqu_lu_n lahum magfiratuw wa rizqun karim
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ tadhulu_ buyu_tan gaira buyu_tikum hat ta_ tastanisu_ wa tusal limu_ ala_ ahliha_ za_likum hairul lakum la'al lakum tazak karu_n
Lakum wa in qila lakumu_r jiu_ fa_r jiu_ huwa azka_ lakum wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na alim
Fa il lam tajidu_ fiha_ ahadan fala_ tadhulu_ha_ hat ta_ yuzana laisa alaikum juna_hun an tadhulu_ buyu_tan gaira masku_natin fiha_ mata_ul lakum wal la_hu yalamu ma_ tubdu_na wa ma_ taktumu_n
Qul lilmuminina yagud du_ min absa_rihim wa yahfazu_ furu_jahum za_lika azka_ lahum in nal la_ha habirum bima_ yasnau_n
Wa qul lilmumina_ti yagdudna min absa_rihin na wa yahfazna furu_jahun na wa la_ yubdina zinatahun na il la_ ma_ zahara minha_ wal yadribna bikumurihin na fala_ juyu_bihin na wa la_ yubdina zinatahun na il la_ libuu_latihin na au a_ba_ ihin na au a_ba_i buu_latihin na au abna_ ihin na au abna_i buu_latihin na au ihwa_nihin na au bani ihwa_nihin na au bani ahwa_tihin na au nisa_ ihin na au ma_ malakat aima_nuhun na awit ta_ bi ina gairil ulil irbati minar rija_li awit tiflil lazina lamyaz haru_ ala_ aura_tin nisa_i wala_ yadrib na biarjulihin na liyulama ma_ yuhfina min zinatihin na wa tu_bu_ ilal la_hi jamian ay yuhal muminu_na la'al lakum tuflihu_n
Wa ankihul aya_ma_ minkum was sa_lihina min iba_dikum wa ima_ikum iy yaku_nu_ fuqara_ a yugnihimul la_hu min fadlih wal la_hu wa_siun alim
Wal yastafifil lazina la_ yajidu_na nika_han hat ta_ yugniyahumul la_hu min fadlih wal lazina yabtagu_nal kita_ba mim ma_ malakat aima_nukum faka_tibu_hum in alimtum fihim hairaw wa a_tu_hum min ma_lil la_hil lazi a_ta_kum wa la_ tukrihu_ fataya_tikum alal biga_i in aradna tahas sunal litabtagu_ aradal haya_tid dun ya_ wa may yukrih huna fa in nal la_ha mim badi ikra_hin na gafu_rur rahim
Wa laqad anzalna_ ilaikum a_ya_tim mubay yina_tiw  wa masalam minal lazina halau min qablikum wa mauizatal lilmut taqin
Al la_hu nu_rus sama_wa_ti wal ard masalu nu_rihi kamiska_tin fiha_ misba_h almisba_hu fi zuja_jah az zuja_jatu ka an naha_ kaukabun dur riy yuy yu_qadu min sajaratim muha_rakatin zaitu_natil la_ sarqiy yatiw wa la_ garbiy yatiy yaka_du zaituha_ yudi u wa lau lam tamsasuna_r ru_run ala_ nu_r yahdil la_hu linu_rihi may yasa_ wa yadibul la_hul amsa_la lin na_s wal la_hu bikul li sai in alim
Fi buyu_tin azinal la_hu an turfa'a wa yuzkara fihas muhu_ yusab bihu lahu_ fiha_ bil guduw wi wal a_sa_l
Rija_lul la_ tulhihim tija_ratuw wa la_ baiun an zikril la_hi wa iqa_mis sala_ti wa ita_ iz zaka_ti yaha_fu_na yauman tataqal labu fihil qulu_bu wal absa_r
Liyajziyahumul la_hu absana ma_ amilu_ wa yazidahum min fadlih wal la_hu yarzuqu may yasya_ u bigairi hisa_b
Wal lazina kafaru_ ama_luhum kasara_bin biqiatiy yahsabuhuz zama_nu ma_ hat ta_ iza_ ja_ ahu_ lam yajid hu sai aw wa wajadal la_ha indahu_ fawaf fa_hu hisa_bah wal la_hu sariul hisa_b
Au kazuluma_tin fi bahril luj jiy yiy  yagsa_hu maujum min fauqihi maujum min faiqihi saha_b zuluma_tun baduha_ fauqa bad iza_ ahraja yadahu_ lam yakad yara_ha_ wa mal lam yajalil la_hu lahu_ nu_rar fama_ lahu_ min nu_r
Alam tara an nal la_ha yusab bihu lahu_ man fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wat tairu sa_f fa_t kul lun qad alima sala_tahu_ wa tasbihah wal la_hu alimun bima_ yafalu_n
Wa lil la_hi mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ard wa ilal la_hil masir
Alam tara an nal la_ha yuzji saha_ban sum ma yu al lifu bainahu_ sum ma yajaluhu_ ruka_man fataral wadqa yahruju min hila_lih wa yunaz zilu minas sama_i min jiba_lin fiha_ mim baradin fayusibu bihi may yasya_ u wa yasrifuhu_ am may yasya_ yaka_du sana_ barqihi yadzabu bil absa_r
Yuqal libul la_hul laila wan naha_r in na fi za_lika laibratal li ulil absa_r
Al la_hu halaqa kul la da_b batim mim ma_ fa minhum may yamsi ala_ batnih wa minhum may yamsi ala_ rijlaini wa minhum may yamsi ala_ arbain yahluqul la_hu ma_ yasya_  in nal la_ha ala_ kul li sai in qadir
Laqad anzalna_ a_ya_tim mubay yina_t wal la_hu yahdi may yasya_ u ila_ sira_tim mustaqim
Wa yaqu_lu_na a_man na_ bil la_hi wa bir rasu_li wa atana_ sum ma yatawal la_ fariqum minhum mim badi za_lika wa ma_ ula_ ika bil muminin
Wa iza_ duu_ ilal la_hi wa rasu_lihi liyahkuma bainahum iza_ fariqum minhum muridu_n
Wa iy yakul lahumul haq qu yatu_ ilaihi muzinin
Afi qulu_bihim maradun amir ta_bu_ am yakha_fu_na ay yahifal la_hu alaihim wa rasu_luh bal ula_ ika humuz za_limu_n
In nama_ ka_na qaulal muminina iza_ duu_ ilal la_hi wa rasu_lihi liyahkuma bainahum ay yaqu_lu_ samina_ wa atana_ wa ula_ ika humul muflihu_n
Wa may yutiil la_ha wa rasu_lahu_ wa yahsal la_ha wa yat taqi fa ula_ ika humul fa_ izu_n
Wa aqsamu_ bil la_hi jahda aima_nihim la in amartahum layahrujun qul la_ tuqsimu_ ta_atum maru_fah in nal la_ha habirun bima_ tamalu_n
Qul atiul la_ha wa atiur rasu_l fa in tawal lau fa in nama alaihi ma_ hum mila wa alaikum ma_ hum miltum wa in tutiu_hu tahtadu_ wa ma_ alar rasu_li il lal bala_gul mubin
Wa adal la_hul lazina a_manu_ minkum wa amilus sa_liha_ti layastahlifan nahum fil ardi kamas tahlafal lazina min qablihim wa layumak kinan na lahum dinahumul lazir tada_ lahum wa layubad dilan nahum min badi haufihim am na_ yabudu_nani la_ yusriku_na bi sai a_ wa man kafara bada za_lika fa ula_ ika humul fa_siqu_n
Wa aqimus sala_ta wa a_tuz zaka_ta wa atiur rasu_la la'al lakum turhamu_n
La_ tahsaban nal lazina kafaru_ mujizina fil ardi wa mawa_humuna_r wa labisal masir
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ liyasta zinkumul lazina malakat aima_nukum wal lazina lam yablugul huluma minkum sala_sa mar ra_tin min qabli sala_til fajri wa hina tadau_na siya_bakum minaz zahirati wa mim badi sala_til isa_i sala_su aura_til lakum laisa alaikum wa la_ alaihim juna_hun badahun na tawa_fu_na alaikum badukum ala_ badin kaza_lika yubay yinul la_hu lakumul a_yat wal la_hu alimun hakim
Wa iza_ balagal atfa_lu minkumul huluma falyastazinu_ kamastazanal lazina min qablihim kaza_lika yubay yinul la_hu lakum a_ya_tihi wal la_hu alimun hakim
Wal qawa_idu minan nisa_ il la_ti la_ yarju_na nika_han falaisa alaihin na juna_hun ay yadana siya_bahun na gaira mutabar rija_tin bizinatin wa ay yastafifna hairul lahun na wal la_hu samiun alim
Laisa alal ama_ harajuw wa la_ alal araji harajuw wa la_ alal maridi harajuw wa la_ ala_ anfusikum an takulu_ min buyu_tikum au buyu_ti a_ba_ ikum au buyu_ti um maha_tikum au buyu_ti ihwa_nikum au buyu_ti ahwa_tikum au buyu_ti ama_mikum au buyu_ti am ma_tikum au buyu_ti ahwa_likum au buyu_ti ha_la_tikum au ma_ malaktum mafa_tihahu_ au sadiqikum laisa alaikum juna_hun an takulu jamian au asta_ta_ fa iza_ dahaltum buyu_tan fasal limu_ ala_ anfusikum tahiy yatam min indil la_hi muba_rakatan tay yibah ka_zalika yubay yinul la_hu lakumul a_ya_ti la'al lakum taqilu_n
In namal muminu_nal lazina a_manu_ bil la_hi wa rasu_lihi wa iza_ ka_nu_ ma'ahu_ ala_ amrin ja_miil lam yazhabu_ hat ta_ yastazinu_h in nal lazina yastazinu_naka ula_ ikal lazina yuminu_na bil la_hi wa rasu_lih fa izas tazanu_ka libadi sanihim fazal liman sita minhum was tagfir lahumul la_ha in nal la_ha gafu_rur rahim
La_ tajalu_ dua_ ar rasu_li bainakum kadua_ ibadikum bada_ qad yalamul la_hul lazina yatasal lalu_na minkum liwa_za_ falyahzaril lazina yuha_lifu_na an amrihi an tusibahum fitnatun au yusibahum aza_bun alim
Ala_ in na lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wal ard qad yalamu ma_ antum alaih wa yauma yurjau_na ilaihi fayunab bi uhum bima_ amilu_ wal la_hu bikul li sai in alim
Taba_rakal lazi naz zalal furqa_na ala_ abdihi liyaku_na lila_lamina nazira_
Nil lazi lahu_ mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa lam yat tahiz waladaw wa lam yakul lahu_ sarikun fil mulki wa halaqa kul la sai in faqad darahu_ taqdira_
Wat tahazu_ min du_nihi a_lihatal la_ yahluqu_na sai aw wa hum yuhlaqu_na wa la_ yamliku_na li anfusihim dar raw wa la_ nafaw wa la_ yamliku_na mautaw wa la_ haya_taw wa la_ nusu_ra_
Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ in ha_za_ il la_ ifkunif tara_hu wa aa_nahu_ alaihi qaumun a_haru_n faqad ja_u_ zulmaw wa zu_ra_
Wa qa_lu_ asa_tirul aw walinak tatabaha_ fahiya tumla_ alaihi bukrataw wa asila_
Qul anzalahul lazi yalamus sir ra fis sama_wa_ti wal ard in nahu_ ka_na gafu_rar rahima_
Wa qa_lu_ ma_li ha_zar rasu_li yakulut taa_ma wa yamsi fil aswa_q lau la_ unzila ilaihi malakun fayaku_na ma'ahu_ nazira_
Au yulqa_ ilaihi kanzun au taku_nu lahu_ jan natuy yakulu minha_ wa qa_laz za_limu_na in tar tabiu_na il la_ rajulam mas hu_ra_
Unzur kaifa darabu_ lakal amsa_la fadal lu_ fala_ yastatiu_na sabila_
Taba_rakal lazi in sa_a ja'ala laka hairam min za_lika jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru wa yajal laka qusu_ra_
Bal kaz zabu_ bis sa_ah wa atadna_ liman kaz zaba bis sa_ati saira_
Iza_ ra at hum mim maka_nim baidin samiu_ laha_ tagay yuzaw wa zafira_

La_ tadul yauma subu_raw wa_hidaw wadu_ subu_ran kasira_

Lahum fiha_ ma_ yasya_ u_na ha_lidina ka_na ala_ rab bika wadam mas ula_
Wa yauma yahsuruhum wa ma_ yabudu_na min du_nil la_hi fayaqu_lu a antum adlaltum iba_di ha_ ula_i am hum dal lus sabil
Qa_lu_ subha_naka ma_ ka_na yan bagi lana_ an nat tahiza_ min du_nika min auliya_ a wa la_kim mat tatahum wa a_ba_ ahum hat ta_ nasuz zikir wa ka_nu_ qauman bu_ra_
Faqad kaz zabu_kum bima_ taqu_lu_na fama_ tastatiu_na sarfaw wala_ nasra_ wa may yazlim minkum nuziqu aza_ban kabira_

Wa yauma tasyaq qaqus sama_u bil gama_mi wa nuz zilal mala_ ikatu tanzila_
Almulku yauma izinil haq qu lir rahma_n wa ka_na yauman alal ka_firina asira_
Wa yauma yaad duz za_limu ala_ yadaihi yaqu_lu ya_laitanit takhaztu ma'ar rasu_li sabila_
Ya_ wailata_ laitani lam at takhiz fula_nan halila_
Laqad adal lani aniz zikri bada iz ja_ ani wa ka_nas saita_nu lil insa_ni hazu_la_
Wa qa_lar rasu_lu ya_ rab bi in na qaumit tahazu_ ha_zal qur a_na mahju_ra_
Wa kaza_lika ja'alna_ likul li nabiy yin aduw wam minal mujrimin wa kafa_ birab bika ha_diyaw wa nasira_

Wa a_daw wa samu_da wa asha_bar ras si wa quru_nan baina za_lika kasira_
Wa kul lan darabna_ lahul amsa_l wa kul lan tab barna_ tatbira_
Wa laqad atau alal qaryatil lati umtirat mataras sau afalam yaku_nu_ yaraunaha_ bal ka_nu_ la_ yarju_na nusu_ra_

In ka_da layudil luna_ an a_lihatina_ lau la_ an sabarna_ alaiha_ wa saufa yalamu_na hina yaraunal aza_ba man adal lu sabila_
Ara aita manit kataza ila_hahu_ hawa_h afa anta taku_nu alaihi wakila_
Am tahsabu an na aksarahum yasmau_na au yaqilu_n in hum il la_ kal ana_mi bal hum adal lu sabila_

Sum ma qabadna_hu ilaina_ qabday yasira_
Wa huwal lazi ja'ala lakumul laila liba_saw wan nauma suba_taw wa ja'alan naha_ra nusu_ra_
Wa huwal lazi arsalar riya_ha busram baina yadai rahmatih wa anzalna_ minas sama_i ma_ an tahu_ra_
Linuhyiya bihi baldatam mai taw wa nusqiyahu_ mim ma_ halaqna_ an a_maw wa ana_siy ya kasira_

Wa lau sina_ labaasna_ fi kul li qaryatin nazira_

Wa huwal lazi ja'alal laila wan naha_ra hilfatal liman ara_da ay yaz zak kara au ara_da suku_ra_

Yuda_al lahul aza_bu yaumal qiya_mati wa yahkud fihi muha_na_

Wa man ta_na wa amila sa_lihan fa in nahu_ yatu_bu ilal la_hi mata_ba_

Wa iz na_da_ rab buka mu_sa_ anitil qaumaz za_limin
Qauma firaun ala_ yat taqu_n
Qa_la rab bi in ni akha_fu ay yukaz zibu_n
Wa yadiqu sadri wa la_ yantaliqu lisa_ni fa arsil ila_ ha_ru_n
Wa lahum alay ya zambun fa akha_fu ay yaqtulu_n

Fatiya_ firauna faqu_la_ in na_ rasu_lu rab bil a_lamin
An arsil ma'ana_ bani isra_il
Qa_la alam nurab bika fina_ walidaw wa labista fina_ min umurika sinin
Wa fa'alta falatakal lati fa'alta wa anta minal ka_firin

Wa tilka nimatun tamun nuha_ alay ya an ab bat ta bani isra_il
Qa_la firaunu wa ma_ rab bul a_lamin

Qa_la liman haulahu_ ala_ tastamiu_n
Qa_la rab bukum wa rab bu a_ba_i kumul aw walin

Fa alqa_ asa_hu fa iza_ hiya suba_num mubin

Yuridu ay yuhrijakum min ardikum bisihrih fama_za_ tamuru_n
