Qa_la lahum mu_sa_ alqu_ ma_ antum mulqu_n
Fa alqau hiba_lahum wa ishiy yahum wa qa_lu_ biiz zati firauna in na_ lanahnul ga_libu_n
Fa alqa_ mu_sa_ asa_hu fa iza_ hiya talqafu ma_ yafiku_n
Fa ulqiyas saharatu sa_jidin
Qa_lu_ a_man na_ birab bil a_lamin
Rab bi mu_sa_ wa ha_ru_n
Qa_la a_mantum lahu_ qabla an a_zana lakum in nahu_ lakabirukumul lazi al lamakumus sihr falasaufa talamu_n la uqat ti an na aidiyakum wa arjulakum min hila_liw wa la usal liban nakum ajmain
Qa_lu_ la_ daira in na_ ila_ rab bina_ munqalibu_n
In na_ natmau ay yagfira lana_ rab buna_ hata_ya_na_ an kun na_ aw walal muminin
Wa auhaina_ ila_ mu_sa_ an asri bi iba_di in nakum mut tabau_n
Fa arsala firaunu fil mada_ ini ha_sirin
In na ha_ ula_i lasyirzimatun qalilu_n
Wa in nahum lana_ laga_ izu_n
Wa in na_ lajamiun ha_ziru_n
Fa akrajna_hum min jan na_tiw wauyu_n
Wa kunu_ziw wa maqa_min karim
Kaza_lik wa auratna_ha_ bani isra_il
Fa atbau_hum musriqin
Falam ma_ tara_ al jama_ni qa_la asha_bu mu_sa_ in na_ lamudraku_n
Qa_la kal la_ in na maiya rab bi sayahdin
Fa auhaina_ ila_ mu_sa_ anidrib biasa_kal bar fanfalaqa fa ka_na kul lu firwin kat taudil azim
Wa azlafna_ sam mal a_harin
Wa anjaina_ mu_sa_ wa mam maahu_ ajmain
Sum ma agraqnal a_harin
In na fi za_lika la a_yah wa ma_ ka_na aksarahum muminin
Wa in na rab baka lahuwal azizur rahim
Watlu alaihim naba a ibra_him
Iz qa_la li abihi wa qaumihi ma_ tabudu_n
Qa_lu_ nabudu asna_man fanazalu laha_ a_kifin
Qa_la hal yasmau_nakum iz tadu_n
Au yanfau_nakum au yadur ru_n
Qa_lu_ bal wajadna_ a_ba_ ana kaza_lika yafalu_n
Qa_la afara aitum ma_ kuntum tabudu_n
Antum wa a_ba_ ukumul aqdamu_n
Fa in nahum aduw wul li il la_ rab bal a_lamin
Al lazi halaqani fahuwa yahdin
Wal lazi huwa yutimuni wa yasqin
Wa iza_ maridtu fahuwa yasfin
Wal lazi yumituni sum ma yuhyin
Wal lazi atmau ay yagfira li hati ati yaumad din
Rab bi hab li hukmaw wa alhiqni bis sa_lihin
Wajal li lisa_na sidqin fil a_khirin
Wajalni miw warasati jan natin naim
Wagfir li abi in nahu_ ka_na minad da_l lin
Wa la_ tuhzini yauma yubasu_n
Yauma la_ yanfau ma_luw wa la_ banu_n
Il la_ man atal la_ha biqalbin salim
Wa uzlifatil jan natu lilmut taqin
Wa bur rizatil jahimu lilga_win
Wa qila lahum ainama_ kuntum tabudu_n
Min du_nil la_h hal yansuru_nakum au yantasiru_n
Fakubkibu fiha_ hum wal ga_wu_n
Wa junu_du iblisa ajmau_n
Qa_lu_ wa hum fiha_ yahtasimu_n
Tal la_hi in kun na_ lafi dala_lim mubin
Iz nusaw wikum birab bil a_lamin
Wa ma_ adal lana_ il lal mujrimu_n
Fama_ lana_ min sa_fiin
Wa la_ sadiqin hamim
Falau an na lana_ kar ratan fanaku_na minal muminin
In na fi za_lika la a_yah wa ma_ ka_na aksaruhum muminin
Wa in na rab baka lahuwal azizur rahim
Kaz zabat qaumu nu_hinil mursalin
Iz qa_la lahum akhu_hum nu_hun ala_ tat taqu_n
In ni lakum rasu_lun amin
Fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
Wa ma_ as alukum alaihi min ajr in ajriya il la_ ala_ rab bil a_lamin
Fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
Qa_lu_ anuminu laka wat tabaakal arzalu_n
Qa_la wa ma_ ilmi bima_ ka_nu_ yamalu_n
In hisa_buhum il la_ ala_ rab bi lau tasuru_n
Wa ma_ ana bitha_ridil muminin
In ana il la_ nazirum mubin
Qa_lu_ la il lam tantahi ya_nu_hu la taku_nan na minal marju_min
Qa_la rab bi in na qaumi kaz zabu_n
Faftah baini wa bainahum fat hawa naj jini wa mam maiya minal muminin
Fa anjaina_hu wa mam maahu_ fil fulkil masu_n
Sum ma agraqna_ badul ba_qin
In na fi za_lika la a_yah wa ma_ ka_na aksaruhum muminin
Wa in na rab baka lahuwal azizur rahim
Kaz zabat a_dunil mursalin
Iz qa_la lahum ahu_hum hu_dun ala_ tat taqu_n
In ni lakum rasu_lun amin
Fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
Wa ma_ as alukum alaihi min ajr in ajriya ila_ ala_ rab bil a_lamin
Atabnu_na bikul li riin a_yatan tabasu_n
Wa tat tahizu_na masa_nia la'al lakum tahludu_n
Wa iza_ batastum batastum jaba_rin
Fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
Wat taqul lazi amad dakum bima_ tamalu_n
Amad dakum bi an a_miw wa banin
Wa jan na_tiw wa uyu_n
In ni akha_fu alaikum aza_ba yaumin azim
Qa_lu_ sawa_ un alaina_ awa azta am lam takum minal wa_izin
In ha_za_ il la_ huluqul aw walin
Wa ma_ nahnu bimuaz zabin
Fakaz zabu_hu fa ahlakna_hum in na fi za_lika la a_yah wa ma_ ka_na aksaruhum muminin
Wa in na rab baka lahuwal azizur rahim
Kaz zabat samu_dul mursalin
Iz qa_la lahum ahu_hum sa_lihun ala_ tat taqu_n
In ni lakum rasu_lun amin
Fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
Wa ma_ as alukum alaihi min ajr in ajriya il la_ ala_ rab bil a_lamin
Atutraku_na fi ma_ ha_huna_ a_minin
Fi jan na_tiw wa uyu_n
Wa zuru_iw wa nahlin taluha_ hadim
Wa tanhitu_na minal jiba_li buyu_tan fa_rihin
Fat taqul la_ha wa qtiu_n
Wa la_ tutiu_ amral musrifin
Al lazina yufsidu_na fil ardi wa la_ yuslihu_n
Qa_lu_ in nama_ anta minal musaharin
Ma_ anta il la_ basarum mitluna_ fati bi a_ya_tin in kunta minas sa_diqin
Qa_la ha_zihi na_qatul la_ha sirbuw wa lakum sirbu yaumim malu_m
Wa la_ tamas su_ha bisu_ in fayahuzakum aza_bu yaumin azim
Fa'aqaru_ha_ fa asbahu_ na_dimin
Fa akhazahumul aza_b in na fi za_lika la a_yah wa ma_ ka_na aksaruhum muminin
Wa in na rab baka lahuwal azizur rahim
Kaz zabat qaumu lu_tinil mursalin
Iz qa_la lahum ahu_hum lu_tun ala_ tat taqu_n
In ni lakum rasu_lun amin
Fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
Wa ma_ as alukum alaihi min ajr in ajriya il la_ ala_ rab bil a_lamin
Atatu_naz zukra_na minal a_lamin
Wa tazaru_na ma_ halaqa lakum rab bukum min azwa_jikum bal antum qaumun a_du_n
Qa_lu_ la il lam tantahi ya_lu_tu lataku_nan na minal muhrajin
Qa_la in ni liamalikum minal qa_lin
Rab bi naj jini wa ahli mim ma_ yamalu_n
Fanaj jaina_hu wa ahlahu_ ajmain
Il la_ aju_zan fil ga_birin
Sum ma dam mamal a_harin
Wa mtama_ alaihim matara_ fasa_ a matarul munzarin
In na fi za_lika la a_yah wa ma_ ka_na aksaruhum muminin
Wa in na rab baka lahuwal azizur rahim
Kaz zaba asha_bul aikatil mursalin
Iz qa_la lahum suaibun ala_ tat taqu_n
In ni lakum rasu_lun amin
Fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
Wa ma_ as alukum alaihi min ajr in ajriya il la_ ala_ rab bil a_lamin
Auful kaila wa la_ taku_nu_ minal muhsirin
Wa zinu_ bil qista_sil mustaqim
Wa la_ tabhasun na_sa asya_ ahum wa la_ tasau fi ardi mufsidin
Wat taqul lazi halaqakum wal jibilatal aw walin
Qa_lu_ in nama_ anta minal musaharin
Wa ma_ anta il la_ basarum mitsluna_ wa in nazun nuka laminal ka_zibin
Fa asqit alaina_ kisalam minas sama_i in kunta minas sa_diqin
Qa_la rab bi alamu bima_ tamalu_n
Fakaz zabu_hu fa ahazahum aza_bu yaumiz zul lah in nahu ka_na aza_ba yaumin azim
In na fi za_lika la a_yatan wa ma_ ka_na aksaruhum muminin
Wa in na rab baka lahuwal azizur rahim
Wa in nahu_ latanzilu rab bil a_lamin
Nazala bihir ru_hul amin
Ala_ qalbika litaku_na minal munzirin
Bilisa_nin arabiy yim mubin
Wa in nahu_ lafi zuburil aw walin
Awalam yakul lahum a_yatan ay yalamahu_ ulama_ u bani isra_il
Wa lau naz zalna_hu ala_ badil ajamin
Faqara ahu_ alaihim ma_ ka_nu_ bihi muminin
Kaza_lika salakna_hu fi qulu_bil mujrimin
La_ yuminu_na bihi hat ta_ yarawul aza_bal alim
Fayatiyahum bagtataw wa hum la_ yasuru_n
Fayaqu_lu_ hal nahnu munzaru_n
Afabiaza_bina_ yastajilu_n
Afara aita im mat tana_hum sinin
Sum ma ja_ ahum ma_ ka_nu_ yu_adu_n
Ma_ agna_ anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yumat tau_n
Wa ma_ ahlakna_ min qaryatin il la_ laha_ munziru_n
Zikra_ wa ma_ kun na_ za_limin
Wa ma_ tanaz zalat bihis saya_tin
Wa ma_ yan bagi lahum wa ma_ yastatiu_n
In nahum anis sami lamazu_lu_n
Fala_ tadu maal la_hi ila_han a_khra fataku_na minal muaz zabin
Wa anzir asiratakal aqrabin
Wahfid jana_haka limanit tabaaka minal muminin
Fa in ashauka faqul in ni bari um mim ma_ tamalu_n
Wa tawak kal alal azizir rahim
Al lazi yara_ka hina taqu_m
Wa taqal lubaka fis sa_jidin
In nahu_ huwas samiul alim
Hal unab bi ukum ala_ man tanaz zalus saya_tin
Tanaz zalu ala_ kuli af fa_kin asim
Yulqu_nas sama wa aksaruhum ka_zibu_n
Was suara_u yat tabi uhumul ga_wu_n
Alam tara an nahum fi kul li wa_diy yahimu_n
Wa an nahum yaqu_lu_na ma_ la_ yafalu_n
Il lal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti wa zakarul la_ha katsiraw wantasaru_ min badi ma_ zulimu_ wa sayalamul lazina zalamu_ ay ya mun qalabiy yanqalibu_n
Ta_ sin tilka a_ya_tul qur a_ni wa kita_bim mubin
Hudaw wa busra- lilmuminin
Al lazina yuqimu_nas sala_ta wa yutu_naz zaka_ta wa hum bil a_hirati hum yu_qinu_n
In nal lazina la_ yuminu_na bil a_hirati zay yan na_ lahum ama_lahum fahum yamahu_n
Ula_ ikal lazina lahum su_ ul aza_bi wa hum fil a_hirati humul ahsaru_n
Wa in naka latulaq qal qur a_na mil lasun hakimin alim
Iz qa_la mu_sa_ li ahlihi in ni a_nastu na_ra_ sa a_tikum minha_ bihabarin au a_tikum bisha_bin qabasil la'al lakum tastalu_n
Falam ma_ ja_ aha_ nu_diya ambu_rika man fin na_ri wa man haulaha_ was subha_nal la_hi rab bil a_lamin
Ya_ mu_sa_ in nahu_ anal la_hul azizul hakim
Wa alqi asha_k falam ma_ ra a_ha_ tahtaz zu ka an naha_ ja_n nuw wal la_ mudbiraw wa lam yuaq qib ya_ mu_sa_ la_ takhaf in ni la_ yakha_fu laday yal mursalu_n
Il la_ man zalama sum ma bad dala husnan bada su_ in fa in ni gafu_rur rahim
Wa adkil yadaka fi jaibika tahruj baida_ a min gairi su_ in fi tisi a_ya_tin ila_ firauna wa qaumih in nahum ka_nu_ qauman fa_siqin
Falam ma_ ja_ at hum a_ya_tuna_ mubsiratan qa_lu_ ha_za_ sihrum mubin
Wa jahadu_ biha_ wastaiqanat ha_ anfusuhum zulmaw wa uluw wa_ fanzur kaifa ka_na a_qibatul mufsidin
Wa laqad a_taina_ da_wu_da wa sulaima_na ilma_ wa qa_lal hamdu lil la_hil lazi fad dalana_ ala_ katsirim min iba_dihil muminin
Wa warisa sulaima_nu da_wuda wa qa_la ya_ ay yuhan na_su ul limna_ mantiqat tairi wa u_tina_ min kuli sai in na ha_za_ lahuwal fadlul mubin
Wa husira lisulaima_na junu_duhu_ minal jin ni wal insi wat tairi fahum yu_zau_n
Hat ta_ iza_ atau ala_ wa_din namli qa_lat namlatuy ya_ ay yuhan namlud hulu_ masa_kinakum la_ yahtimanakum sulaima_nu wa junu_duhu_ wa hum la_ yasuru_n
Fatabas sama da_hikam min qauliha_ wa qa_la rab bi auzini an askura nimatakal lati anamta alay ya wa ala_ wa_liday ya wa an amala sa_lihan tarda_hu wa adhilni birahmatika fi iba_dikas sa_lihin
Wa tafaq qadat taira faqa_la ma_ liya la_ aral hud hud am ka_na minal ga_ibin
La uaz ziban nahu_ aza_ban sadi dan au la azbahan nahu_ au layatiyan ni bisulta_nim mubin
Famakatsa gaira baidin faqa_la ahatu bima_ lam tuhit bihi wa jituka min saba in binabaiy yaqin
In ni wajadtum ra atan tamlikuhum wa u_tiyat min kul li sai iw wa laha_ arsun azim
Wa jadtuha_ wa qaumaha_ yasjudu_na lis samsi min du_nil la_hi wa zay yana lahumus saita_nu ama_ lahum fasad dahum anis sabili fahum la_ yahtadu_n
Al la_ yasjudu_ lil la_hil lazi yuhrijul kitaba fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa yalamu ma_ tuhfu_na wa ma_ tulisu_n
Al la_hu la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa rab bul arsil azim
Qa_la sananzuru ashadaqta am kunta minal ka_zibin
Iz hab bikita_bi ha_za_ fa alqih ilaihim sum ma tawal la anhum fanzur ma_za_ yarjiu_n
Qa_lat ya_ ay yuhal mala u in ni ulqiya ilay ya kita_bun karim
In nahu_ min sulaima_na wa in nahu_ bismil la_hir rahma_nir rahim
Al la_ talu_ alay ya watu_ni muslimin
Qa_lat ya_ ay yuhal mala u aftu_ni fi amri ma_ kuntu qa_tiatan amran hat ta_ tashadu_n
Qa_lu_ nahnu ulu_ quw watiw wa ulu_ ba;sin sadidiw wal amru ilaika fanzuri ma_za_ tamurin
Qa_lat in nal mulu_ka iza_ dakhalu_ qaryatan afsadu_ha_ wa ja'alu_ aiz zata ahliha_ azil lah wa kaza_lika yafalu_n
Wa in ni mursilatun ilaihim bi hadiy yatin fana_diratun bima yarjiul mursalu_n
Falam ma_ ja_ a sulaima_na qa_la atumid du_nani bima_l fama_ a_ta_niyal la_hu hairum mim ma_ a_ta_kum bal antum bihadiy yatikum tafrahu_n
Irji ilaihim falanatiyan nahum bijunu_dil la_ qibala lahum biha_ wa lanuhrijan nahum minha_ azil lataw wa hum sa_giru_n
Qa_la ya_ ay yuhal mala u ay yukum yatini biarsiha_ qabla ay yatu_ni muslimin
Qa_la ifritum minal jin ni ana a_tika bihi qabla an taqu_ma mim maqa_mik wa in ni alaihi laqawiy yun amin
Qa_lal lazi indahu_ ilmum minal kita_bi ana a_tika bihi qabla ay yartad da ilaika tarfuk falam ma_ ra a_hu mustaqir ran indahu_ qa_la ha_za_ min fadli rab bi liyabluwani a askuru am akfur wa man sakara fa in nama_ yaskuru linafsih wa man kafara fa in na rab bi ganiy yun karim
Qa_la nak kiru_ laha_ arsaha_ nanzur atahtadi am taku_nu minal lazina la_ yahtadu_n
Falam ma_ ja_ at qila aha_kaza_ arsuk qa_lat ka an nahu_ huw wa u_tinal ilma min qabliha_ wa kun na_ muslimin
Wa sad daha_ ma_ ka_nat tabudu min du_nil la_h in naha_ ka_nat min qaumin ka_firin
Qila lahad hulis sar falam ma_ ra at hu hasibat hu luj jataw wa kasyafat an sa_qaiha_ qa_la in nahu_ sarhum mumar radum min qawa_rir qa_lat rab bi in ni zalamtu nafsi wa aslamtu ma'a sulaima_na lil la_hi rab bil a_lamin
Wa laqad arsalna_ ila_ samu_da aha_hum sa_lihan ani budul la_ha fa iza_ hum fariqa_ni yahtasimu_n
Qa_la ya_ qaumi lima tastajilu_na bis say yi ati qablal hasanati lau la_ tastagfiru_nal la_ha la'al lakum turhamu_n
Qa_lut tay yama_ bika wa bimam ma'ak qa_la ta_irukum indal la_hi bal antum qaumun tuftanu_n
Wa ka_na fi madinati tisatu rahtiy yufsidu_na fil ardi wa la_ yuslihu_n
Qa_lu_ taqa_samu_ bil la_hi lanubay yitan nahu_ wa ahlahu_ sum ma lanaqu_lan na liwaliy yihi ma_ sahidna_ mahlika ahlihi wa in na_ lasa_diqu_n
Wa makaru_ makraw wa makarna_ makraw wa hum la_ yasuru_n
Fanzur kaifa ka_na a_qibatu makrihim an na_ dam marna_hum wa qaumahum ajmain
Fatilka buyu_tuhum ha_wiyatam bima_ zalamu_ in na fi za_lika la a_yatal liqaumiy yalamu_n
Wa anjainal lazina a_manu_ wa ka_nu_ yat taqu_n
Wa lutan iz qa_la liqaumihi atatu_nal fa_hisyata wa antum tubsiru_n
A in nakum latatu_nar rija_la sahwatam min du_nin nisa_ bal antum qaumun tajhalu_n
Fama_ ka_na jawa_ba qaumihi il la_ an qa_lu_ ahriju_ a_ la lu_tim min qaryatikum in nahum una_suy yatatah haru_n
Fa anjaina_hu wa ahlahu_ il lam ra atahu_ qad darna_ha_ minal ga_birin
Wa amtarna_ alaihim matara_ fasa_ a matarul munzarin
Qulil hamdu lil la_hi wa sala_mun ala_ iba_dihil lazinas tafa_ a_l la_hu hairun am ma_ yusriku_n
Am man halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa anzala lakum minas sama_i ma_ fa an batna_ bihi hada_ iqa za_ta bahjah ma_ ka_na lakum an tumbitu_ sajaraha_ a ila_hum ma'al la_h bal hum qaumuy yadilu_n
Am man ya'alal arda qara_raw wa ja'ala hila_laha_ anha_raw wa ja'ala la_ha rawa_siya wa ja'ala bainal bahraini ha_jiza_ a ila_hum ma'al la_hi bal aksaruhum la_ yalamu_n
Am may yujibul mudtar ra iza_ daa_hu wa yaksifus su_a wa yajalukum hulafa_ al ard a ila_hum ma'al la_h qalilam ma_ tazak karu_n
Am may yahdikum fi zuluma_til bar ri wal bahri wa may yursilur riya_ha busram baina yadai rahmatih a ila_hum ma'al la_h taa_lal la_hu am ma_ yusriku_n
Am may yabda ul hakqa sum ma yuiduhu_ wa may yarzuqukum minas sama_i wal ard a ila_hum maal la_h qul ha_tu_ burha_nakum in kuntum sa_diqin
Qul la_ yalamu man fis sama_wa_ti wal ardil gaiba il lal la_h wa ma_ yasuru_na ay ya_na yubasu_n
Balid da_raka ilmuhum fil a_hirah bal hum fi sak kim minha_ bal hum minha_ amu_n
Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ a iza_ kuna_ tura_baw wa a_ba_ una_ a in na_ lamuhraju_n
Laqad wuidna_ ha_za_ nahnu wa a_ba_ una_ min qablu in ha_za_ il la_ asa_tirul aw walin
Qul siru_ fil ardi fanzuru_ kaifa ka_na a_qibatul mujrimin
Wa la_ tahzan alaihim wa la_ takun fi daiqim mim ma_ yamkuru_n
Wa yaqu_lu_na mata_ ha_zal wadu in kuntum sa_diqin
Qul asa_ ay yaku_na radifa lakum badul lazi tastajilu_n
Wa in na rab baka lazu_ fadlin aln na_si wa la_kin na aksarahum la_ yaskuru_n
Wa in na rab baka layalamu ma_ tukin nu sudu_ruhum wa ma_ yulinu_n
Wa ma_ min ga_ibatin fis sama_i wal ardi il la_ fi kita_bim mubin
In na ha_zal qur a_na yaqus su ala_ bani isra_ ila aksaral lazi hum fihi yahtalifu_n
Wa in nahu_ lahudaw wa rahmatul lilmuminin
In na rab baka yaqdi bainahum bihukmihi wahuwal azizul alim
Fatawak kal alal la_h in naka alal haq qil mubin
In naka la_ tusmiul mauta_ wa la_ tusmi us sum mad du a_ a iza_ wal lau mudbirin
Wa ma_ anta biha_dil umyi an dala_latihim in tusmiu il la_ may yuminu bi a_ya_tina_ fahum muslimu_n
Wa iza_ waqa'al qaulu alaihim ahrajna_ lahum da_b batam minal ardi tukal limuhum an nan na_sa ka_nu_ bi a_ya_tina_ la_ yu_qinu_n
Wa yauma masuru min kul li um matin faujam mim may yukaz zibu bi a_ya_tina_ fahum yu_zau_n
Hatta_ iza_ ja_ u_ qa_la akaz zabtum bi a_ya_ti wa lam tuhitu_ biha_ ilman am ma_ za_ kuntum tamalu_n
Wa waqa'al qaulu alaihim bima_ za_lamu_ fahum la_ yantiqu_n
Alam yarau an na_ ja'alnal laila liyaskunu_ fihi wan naha_ra mubisira_ in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy yuminu_n
Wa yauma yunfaku fis su_ri fafazia man fis sama_wa_ti wa man fil ardi il la_ man sa_al la_hu wa kulun atauhu da_hirin
Wa taral jiba_la tahsabuha_ ja_midataw wa hiya tamur ru mar ras saha_b sunal la_hil lazi atqana kul la sai in nahu_ habirun bima_ tafalu_n
Man ja_ a bil hasanati falahu_ hairum minha_ wa hum min fazain yauma izin a_minu_n
Wa man ja_ a bis say yi ati fakub bat wuju_huhum fin na_r hal tujzauna il la_ ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
In nama_ umirtu an abuda rab ba ha_zihil baldatil lazi har ramaha_ wa lahu_ kul lu sai iw wa umirtu an ku_na minal muslimin
Wa an atluwal qura_n famanih tada_ fa in nama_ yahtadil linafsih wa man dal la faqul in nama_ ana minal munzirin
Wa qulil hamdu lil la_hi sayurikum a_ya_tihi fatarifu_naha_ wa ma_ rab buka biga_filin am ma_ tamalu_n
Ta_ sim mim
Tilka a_ya_tul kita_bil mubin
Natlu_ alaika min nabai mu_sa_ wa firauna bil haq qi laqaumiy yuminu_n
In na firauna ala_ fil ardi wa ja'ala ahlaha_ siya ay yastadifu ta_ ifafatam minhum yuzab bihu abna_ ahum wa yastahyi nisa_ ahum in nahu_ ka_na minal mufsidin
Wa nuridu an namun na alal lazinas tadifu_ fil ardi wa najalahum a im mataw wa najalahumul wa_risin
Wa numak kina lahum fil ardi wa nuriya fia'auna wa ha_ma_na wa junu_dahuma_ minhum ma_ ka_nu_ yahzaru_n
Wa auhaina_ ila_ um mi mu_sa_ an ardiih fa iza_ hifti alaihi fa alqihi fil yam mi wa la_ taha_fi wa la_ tahzani in na_ ra_d du_hu ilaiki wa ja_ilu_hu minal mursalin
Fal taqatahu_ a_lu firauna liyaku_na lahum aduw waw wa hazana_ in na firauna wa ha_ma_na wa junu_dahuma_ ka_nu_ ha_ti in
Wa qa_latim ra atu firauna qur ratu ainil li wa lak la_ taqtulu_h asa_ ay yanfaana_ au nat tahizahu_ waladaw wa hum la_ yasuru_n
Wa asbaha fu a_du um mi mu_sa_ fa_riga_ in ka_dat latubdi bihi lau la_ ar rabatna_ ala_ qalbiha_ litaku_na minal muminin
Wa qa_lat li uhtihi qus sih fabasurat bihi an junubiw wa hum la_ yasuru_n
Wa har ramna_ alaihil mara_dia min qablu faqa_lat hal adul lukum ala_ ahli baitiy yakfulu_nahu_ lakum wa hum lahu_ na_sihu_n
Faradadna_hu ila_ um mihi kaitaqara ainuha_ wa la_ tahzana wa litalama an na wadal la_hi haq quw wa la_kina aksarahum la_ yalamu_n
Wa lam ma_ balaga asud dahu_ was tawa_ a_taina_hu hukmaw wa ilma_ wa kaza_lika najzil muhsinin
Wa dakalal madinata ala hini gaflatim min ahliha_ fawajada fiha_ rajulaini yaqtatila_ni ha_za_ min siatihi wa ha_za_ min aduw wihi fastaga_sahul lazi min siatihi alal lazi min aduw wihi fawakazahu_ mu_sa_ faqada_ alaihi qa_la ha_za_ min amalis saita_ni in nahu_ aduw wum mudil lum mubin
Qa_la rab bi ni zalamtu nafsi fagfirli fagafara lah in nahu_ huwal gafu_rur rahim
Qa_la rab bi bima_ anamta alay ya falan aku_na zahiral lilmujrimin
Fa asbaha fil madinati ka_ ifay yataraq qabu fa izal lazis tansarahu_ bil amsi yastasrikuh qa_la lahu_ mu_sa_ in naka lagawiy yum mubin
Falam ma_ an ara_da ay yabtisya bil lazi huwa aduw wul lahuma_ qa_la ya_ mu_sa_ aturidu an taqtulani kama_ qatalta nafsam bil amsi in turidu il la_ an taku_na jab ba_ran fil ardi wa ma_ turidu an taku_na minal muslihin
Wa ja_ a rajulum min aqsal madinati yasa_ qa_la ya_ mu_sa_ in nal mala a yatamiru_na bika liyaqtulu_ka fahruj in ni laka minan na_sihin
Fakharaja minha_ ha_ ifay yataraq qab qa_la rab bi naj jini minal qaumiz za_limin
Wa lam ma_ tawaj jaha tilqa_ a madyana qa_la asa_ rab bi ay yahdiyani sawa_ as sabil
Wa lam ma_ warada ma_ a mad yana waiada alaihi um matam minan na_si yasqu_na wawajada min du_nihimum ra ataini tazu_da_n qa_la ma_ hatbukuma_ qa_lata_ la_ nasqi hat ta_ yusdirar ri a_u wa abu_na_ saikun kabir
Fasaqa_ lahuma_ sum ma tawal la_ ilaz zil li faqa_la rab bi in ni lima_ anzalta ilay ya min hairin faqir
Faja_ at hu ihda_huma_ tamsi alas tihya_ qa_;at in na abi yadu_ka liyajziyaka ajra ma_ saqaita lana_ falam ma_ ja_ ahu_ wa qas sa alaihil qasasa qa_la la_ takhaf najauta minal qaumiz za_limin
Qa_lat ihda_huma_ ya_ abatis tajirhu in na haira manis tajartal qawiy yul amin
Qa_la in ni uridu an unkihaka ihdab natay ya ha_taini ala_ an tajurani sama_niya hijaj fa in atmamta asyran famin indik wa ma_ uridu an asyuqa alaik satajiduni in sa_ al la_hu minas sa_lihin
Qa_la za_lika baini wa bainak ay yamal ajalaini qadaitu fala_ udwa_na alay wal la_hu ala_ ma_ naqu_lu wakil
Falam ma_ qada_ mu_sal ajala wa sa_ra bi ahlihi a_nasa min ja_nibit tu_ri na_ra_ qa_la li ahlihim kutsu_ in ni a_nastu Na_ral la'al li a_tikum minha_ bikhabarin au jazwatim minan na_ri la'al lakum tastalu_n
Falam ma_ ata_ha_ nu_diya min sa_ti il wa_dil aimani fil buqatil muba_rakati minas sajarati ay ya_ mu_sa_ in ni anal la_hu rab bul a_lamin
Wa an alqi asha_k falam ma_ ra a_ha_ tahtaz zu ka an naha_ nuw wal la_ mudbiraw walam yuaq qib ya_ mu_sa_ aqbil wa la_ takhaf in naka minal a_minin
Usluk yadaka fi jaibika tahruj baida_ a min gairi su_ iw wadmum ilaika jana_haka minar rahbi faza_nika burha_na_ni mir rab bika ila_ firauna wa mala ih in nahum ka_nu_ qauman fa_siqin
Qa_la rab bi in ni qataltu minhum nafsan fa akha_fu ay yaqtulu_n
Wa aki ha_ru_nu huwa afsahu mini lisa_nan fa arsilhu maiya rid ay yusad diquni in ni akha_fu ay yukaz zibu_n
Qa_la sanasud du adudaka bi akhika wa najalu lakuma_ sulta_nan fala_ yasilu_na ilaikuma_ bi aya_tina_ antuma_ wa manit taba'akumal ga_libu_n
Falam ma_ ja_ ahum mu_sa_ bi a_ya_tina_ bay yina_tin qa_lu_ ma_ ha_za_ il la_ sihrum muftaraw wa ma_ samina_ biha_ za_ fi a_ba_ inal aw walin
Wa qa_la mu_sa_ rab bi alamu biman ja_ a bil huda_ min indihi wa man taku_nu lahu_ a_qibatud da_r in nahu_ la_ yuflihuz za_limu_n
Wa qa_la firaunu ya_ ay yuhal mala u ma_ alimatu lakum min ila_hin gairi fa auqid li ya_ ha_ma_nu alat tini fajal li sarhal la'al li at taliu ila_ ila_hi mu_sa_ wa in ni la azun nuhu_ minal ka_zibin
Was takbara huwa wa junu_duhu_ fil ardi biga ril haq qi wa zan nu_ anahum ilaina_ la_ yurjau_n
Fa akazna_hu wa junu_dahu_ fanabazna_hum fil yam fan zur kaifa ka_na a_qibatuz za_limin
Wa ja'alna_hum a im matay yadu_na ilan na_ri wa yaumal qiya_mati la_ yunsaru_n
Wa atbana_hum fi ha_zihid dun ya_ lanah wa yaumal qiya_mati hum minal maqbu_hin
Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sal kita_ba mim badi ma_ ahlaknal quru_nal u_la_ basa_ ira lin na_si wa hudaw wa rahmatal la al lahum yatazak karu_n
Wa ma_ kunta bija_nibil garbiy yi iz qada_ina_ ila_ mu_sal amra wa ma_ kunta minas sa_hidin
Wa la_kin na_ ansana_ quru_nan fa tata_wala alaihimul umur wama_ kunta sa_wiyan fi ahli mad dana tatlu_ alaihim a_ya_tina_ wa la_kin na_ kun na_ mursilin
Wa ma_ kunta bija_nibit tu_ri iz na_daina_ wa la_kir rahmatam mir rab bika litunzira qaumam ma_ a_ta_hum min nazirim min qablika la al lahum yatazak karu_n
Wa lau la_ an tusibahum musibatun bima_ qad damat aidihim faya qu_lu_ rab bana_ laula_ arsalta ilaina_ rasu_lan fanat tabia a_ya_tika wa naku_na minal muminin
Falam ma_ ja_ ahumul haq qu min indina_ qa_lu_ laula_ u_tiya mitsla ma_ u_tiya mu_sa_ awalam yakfuru_ bima_ u_tiya mu_sa_ min qabl qa_lu_ sihra_ni taza_hara_ wa qa_lu_ in na_ bikul lin ka_firu_n
Qul fatu_ bikita_bim min indil la_hi huwa ahda_ minhuma_ at tabihu in kuntum sa_diqin
Fa il lam yastajibu_ laka falam an nama_ yat tabiu_na ahwa_ ahum wa man adal lu_ mim manit tabaa hawa_hu bagairi hudam minal la_h in nal la_ha la_ yahdil qaumaz za_limin
Wa laqad was salna_ lahumul qaula la'al lahum yatazak karu_n
Al lazina a_tainahumul kita_ba min qabihi humabihi yuminu_n
Wa iza_ yutla_ alaihim qa_lu_ a_man na_ bihi in nahul haq qu mir rab bi na_ in na_ kun na_ min qablihi muslimin
Ula_ ika yutauna ajrahum mar rataini bima_ sabaru_ wa yadra u_na bil hasanatis say yi ata wa mim ma_ razaqna_hum yunfiqu_n
Wa iza_ samiul lagwa aradu_ anhu wa qa_lu_ lana_ ama_luna_ wa lakum ama_lukum sala_mun alaikum la_ nabtagil ja_hilin
In naka la_ tahdi man ahbabta wa la_kin nal la_ha yahdi may yasya_ wa huwa alamu bil muhtadin
Wa qa_lu_ in nat tabiil huda_ ma'aka nutakat taf min ardina_ awalam numak kil lahum haraman a_minay yujba_ ilaihi samara_tu kul li sai ir rizqam mil ladun na_ wa la_kin na aksarahum la_ yalamu_n
Wa kam ahlakna_ min qaryatim batirat maisyataha_ fatilka masa_kinuhum lam tuskam min badihim il la_ qalila_ wa kun na_ nahnul wa_risin
Wa ma_ ka_na rab buka muhlikal qura_ hat ta_ yabatsa fi um miha_ rasu_lay yatlu_ alaihim a_ya_tina_ wa ma_ kun na_ muhlikil qura_ il la_ wa ahluha_ za_limu_n
Wa ma_ u_titum min sai in famata_ul haya_tid dun ya_ wa zinatuha_ wa ma_ indal la_hi hairuw wa abqa_ afala_ taqilu_n
Afamaw wa'adna_hu wa dan hasanan fahuwa la_qihi kamam mat tana_hu mata_al haya_tid dun ya_ sum ma huwa yaumal qiya_mati minal muhdarin
Wa yauma yuna_dihim fayaqu_lu aina suraka_ iyal lazina kuntum tazumu_n
Qa_lal lazina haq qa alaihimul qaulu rab bana_ ha_ ula_ il lazina agwaina_ agwaina_hum kama_ gawaina_ tabar rana_ ilaikama_ ka_nu_ iy ya_na_ yabudu_n
Wa qiladu_ suraka_ akum fada'auhum falam yastajibu_ lahum wa ra_wul aza_b lau an nahum ka_nu_ yahtadu_n
Wa yauma yuna_dihim fayaqu_lu ma_za_ ajabtumul mursalin
Fa'amiyat alaihumul an ba_ u yauma izin fahum la_ yatasa_ alu_n
Fa am ma_ man ta_ba wa a_mana wa amila sa_lihan fa'asa_ ay yku_na minal muflihin
Wa rab buka yahluqu ma_ yasya_u wa yahta_r ma_ ka_na lahumul hiyarah subha_nal la_hi wa taa_la_ am ma_ yusriku_n
Wa rab buka yalamu ma_ tukin nu sudu_ruhum wa ma_ yulinu_n
Wa huwal la_hu la ila_ha il la_ hu lahul hamdu fil u_la_ wal a_khira_ti wa lahul hukmu wa ilaihi turjau_n
Qul ara aitum in ja'alal la_hu alaikumul laila sarmadan ila_ yaumil qiya_mati man ila_hun gairul la_hi yatikum bidiya_ afala_ tasmau_n
Qul ara aitum in ja'alal la_hu alaikumun naha_ra sarmadan ila_ yaumil qiya_mati man ila_hun gairul la_hi yatikum bilailin taskunu_na fih afala_ tubsiru_n
Wa mir rahmatihi ja'ala lakumul laila wan naha_ra litaskunu_ fihi wa litabtagu_ min fadlihi wa la'al lakum taskuru_n
Wa yauma yuna_dihim fayaqu_lu aina suraka_ iyal lazina kuntum tazumu_n
Wa nazana_ min kul li um matin sahidan faqulna_ ha_tu_ burha_nakum fa'alimu_ an nal haq qa lil la_hi wa dal la anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yaftaru_n
In na qa_ru_na ka_na min qaumi mu_sa_ fabaga_ alaihim wa a_taina_hu minal kunu_zi ma_ in na mafa_tihahu_ latanu_ u bil usbati ulil quw wati iz qa_la lahu_ qaumuhu_ la_ tafrah in nal la_ha_ la_ yuhib bul fari hin
Wabtagi fi ma_ a_ta_kal la_hud da_ral a_khirata wa la_ tansa nasibaka minad dun ya_ wa ahsin kama_ ahsanal la_hu ilaika wa la_ tabgil fasa_da fil ard in nal la_ha la_ yuhib bul mutsidin
Qa_la in nama_ u_tituhu_ ala_ ilmin indi awalam yalam an nal la_ha qad ahlaka min qablihi minal quru_ni man huwa asyad du minhu quw wataw wa aksaru jama_ wa la_ yus alu an zunu_bihimul mujrimu_n
Fahraja ala_ qaumihi fi zinatih qa_lal lazina yuridu_nal haya_tad dun ya_ ya_ laita lana_ mitsla ma_ u_tiya qa_ru_nu in nahu_ lazu_ haz zin azim
Wa qa_lal lazina u_tul ilma wailakum sawa_bul la_hi hairul liman a_mana wa amila sa_liha_ wa la_ yulaq qa_ha_ il las sa_biru_n
Fahasafna_ bihi wa bida_rihil ard fama_ ka_na lahu_ minfi atiy yansuru_nahu_ min du_nil la_hi wa ma_ ka_na minal muntasirin
Wa asbahal lazina taman nau maka_nahu_ bil amsi yaqu_lu_na waika an nal la_ha yabsutur rizqa limay yasya_ u min iba_dihi wa yaqdir lau la_ am man nal la_hu alaina_ lahasafa bina_ waika an nahu_ la_ yuflihul ka_firu_n
Tilkad da_rul a_khiratu najaluha_ lil lazina la_ yuridu_na uluw wan fil ardi wa la_ fasa_dan wal a_qibatu lilmut taqin
Man ja_ a bil hasanati falahu_ hairum minha_ wa man ja_ a bis say yi ati fala_ yujzal lazina amilus say yi a_ti il la_ ma_ ka_nu_ yamalu_n
In nal lazi farada alaikal qur a_na larad duka ila_ maa_d qur rab bi alamu man ja_ a bil huda_ wa man huwa fi dala_lin mubin
Wa ma_ kunta tarju_ ay yulqa_ ilaikal kita_bu il la_ rahmatam mir rab bika fala_ taku_nan na zahiral lilka_firin
Wa la_ yashud dun naka an a_ya_til la_hi bada_ iz unzilat ilaika wadu ila_ rab bika wa la_ taku_nan na minal musrikin
Wa la_ tadu ma'al la_hi ila_han a_khar la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa kul lu sai in ha_likun il la_ wajhah lahul hukmu wa ilaihi turjau_n
Alif la_m mim
Ahasiban na_su ay yutraku_ ay yaqu_lu_ a_man na_ wa hum la_ yuftanu_n
Wa laqad fatan nal lazina min qablihim falayalaman nal la_hul lazina sadaqu_ wa layalaman nal ka_zibin
Am hasibal lazina yamalu_nas say yi a_ti yasbiqu_na_ sa_ a ma_ yahkumu_n
Man ka_na yarju_ liqa_ al la_hi fa in na ajalal la_hi la a_t wa huwas samiul a_lamin
Wa man ja_hada fa in nama_ yuja_hidu linafsihi in nal la_ha la ganiy yun anil a_lamin
Wal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti lanukaf firan na anhum say yi a_tihim wa lanajziyan nahum ahsanal lazi ka_nu_ yamalu_n
Wa was sainal insa_na biwa_lidaihi husna_ wa in ja_hada_ka litusrika bima_ laisa laka bihi ilmun fala_ tutihuma_ ilay ya marjiukum fa unab bi ukum bima_ kuntum tamalu_n
Wal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti lanudhilan nahum fis sa_lihin
Wa minan na_si may yaqu_lu a_man na_ bil la_hi fa iza_ u_ziya fil la_hi ja'ala fitnatan na_si kaaza_bil la_h wa la in ja_ a nasrum mir rab bika layaqu_lun na in na_ kun na_ ma'akum awalaisal la_hu bi alama bima_ fi suduril a_lamin
Wa layalaman nal la_hul lazina a_manu_ wa layalaman nal muna_fiqin
Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ lil lazina a_manut tabiu_ sabilana_ walnahmil hata_ya_kum wa ma_ hum biha_milina min hata_ya_hum min sai in nahum laka_zibu_n
Wa layahmilun na asqa_lahum wa asqa_lam ma'a asqa_lihim wa layusalun na yaumal qiya_mati am ma_ ka_nu_ yaftaru_n
Wa laqad arsalna_ nu_han ila_ qaumihi falabitsa fihim alfa sanatin il la_ hamsina a_ma_ fa ahazahumut tu_fa_nu wa hum za_limu_n
Fa anjalna_hu asha_bas safinati wa ja'alna_ha_ a_ya_tal lil a_lamin
Wa ibra_hima iz qa_la liqaumihi budul la_ha wat taqu_h za_likum hairul lakum in kuntum talamu_n
In nama_ tabudu_na min du_nil la_hi ausa_naw wa tahluqu_na ifka_ inal lazina tabudu_na min du_nil la_hi la_ yamliku_na lakum rizqan fabtagu_ indal la_hir rizqa wa budu_hu waskuru_ lah ilaihi turjau_n
Wa in tukaz zibu_ faqad kaz zaba umamum min qablikum wa ma_ alar rasu_li il lal bala_gul mubin
Awalam yarau kaifa yubdiul la_hul halqa sum ma yuiduh in na za_lika alal la_hi yasir
Qul siru_ fil ardi fanzuru_ kaifa bada al halqa sum mal la_hu yunsi un nas atal a_hirah in nal la_ha ala_ kul li sai in qadir
Yuaz zibu may yasya_u wa yarhamu may yasya_u wa ilaihi tuqlabu_n
Wa ma_ antum bimujizina fil ardi wa la_ fis sama_i wa ma_ lakum min du_nil la_hi miw waliy yiw wa la_ nasir
Wal lazina kafaru_ bi a_ya_til la_hi wa liqa_ ihi ula_ ika ya isu_ mir rahmati wa ula_ ika lahum aza_bun alim
Fama_ ka_na jawa_ba qaumihi il la_ an qa_luq tulu_hu au har riqu_hu fa anja_hul la_hu minan na_r in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy yuminu_n
Wa qa_la in namat takaztum min du_nil la_hi ausa_nam mawad data bainikum fil haya_tid dun ya_ sum ma yaumal qiya_mati yakfuru badukum bibadiw wa yalanu badukum badaw wa mawa_kumun na_ru wa ma_ lakum min na_sirin
Fa a_mana_ lahu_ lu_tun wa qa_la in ni muha_jirun ila_ rab bi in nahu_ huwal azizul hakim
Wa wahabna_ lahu_ is ha_qa wa yaqu_ba wa ja'alna_ fi zur riy yatihin nubuw wata wal kita_ba wa a_taina_hu ajrahu_ fid dun ya_ wa in nahu_ fil a_khirati laminas sa_lihin
Wa lu_tan iz qa_la liqaumihi in nakum latatu_nal fa_hisah ma_ sabaqakum biha_ min ahadim minal a_lamin
A in nakum latatu_nar rija_la wa taqtau_nas sabila wa tatu_na fi na_dikumul munkara fama_ ka_na jawa_ba qaumihi il la_ an qa_lu tina_ biaza_bil la_hi in kunta minas sa_diqin
Qa_la rab bin surni alal qaumil mufsidin
Wa lam ma_ ja_ at rusuluna_ ibra_hima bil busra_ qa_lu_ in na_ muhliku_ ahli ha_zihil qaryah in na ahlaha_ ka_nu_ za_limin
Qa_la in na fiha_ lu_ta_ qa_lu_ nahnu alamu biman fiha_ lanunaj jiyan nahu_ wa ahlahu_ il lam ra atah ka_nat minal ga_birin
Wa lam ma_ an ja_ at rusuluna_ lu_tan si a bihim wa da_qa bihim zaraw wa qa_lu_ la_ takaf wa la_ tahzan in na_ munaj ju_ka wa ahlaka il lam ra ataka ka_nat minal ga_birin
In na_ munzilu_na ala_ ahli ha_zihil qaryati rijzam minas sama_i bima_ ka_nu_ yafsuqu_n
Wa laqad tarakna_ minha_ a_yatam bay yinatal liqaumiy yaqilu_n
Wa ila_ mad yana aha_hum suaiban faqa_la ya_ qaumi budul la_ha war jul yaumal a_khira wa la_ tasau fil ardi mufsidin
Fakaz zabu_hu fa akhazat humur rajfatu fa asbahu_ fi da_rihim ja_simin
Wa a_daw wa samu_da wa qad tabay yana lakum mim masa_kinihim wa zay yana lahumus saita_nu ama_lahum fasad dahum anis sabili wa ka_nu_ mustabsirin
Wa qa_ru_na wa firauna wa ha_ma_n wa laqad ja_ ahum mu_sa_ bil bay yina_ti fastakbaru_ fil ardi wa ma_ ka_nu_ sa_biqin
Fakul lan akhazna_ bizam bih faminhum man arsalna_ alaihi ha_siba_ wa minhum man akhazat hus saihah wa minhum man hasafna_ bihil ard wa minhum man agraqna_ wa ma_ ka_nal la_hu liyazlimahum wa la_kin ka_nu_ anfusahum yazlimu_n
Matsalul lazinat takhazu_ min du_nil la_hi auliya_ a kamatsalil ankabu_t it takhazat baita_ wa in na auhanal buyu_ti labaitul ankabu_ti lauka_nu_ yalamu_n
In nal la_ha yalamu ma_ yadu_na min du_nihi min sai in wa huwal azizul hakim
Wa tilkal amsa_lu nadribuha_ lina_si wa ma_ yaqilu ha_ il lal a_limu_n
Khalaqal la_hus sama_wa_ti wal arda bil haq in na fi za_lika ka a_yatal lil muminin
Utlu ma_ u_hiya ilaika minal kita_bi wa aqimis sala_h in nas sala_ta tanha_ anil fahsa_i wal munkar wa lazikrul la_hi akbar wal la_hu yalamu ma_ tasnau_n
Wa la_ tuja_dilu_ ahlal kita_bi il la_ bil lati hiya ahsan il lal lazina zalamu_ minhum wa qu_lu_ a_man na_ bil lazi unzila ilaina_ wa unzila ilaikum wa ila_huna_ wa ila_hukum wa_hiduw wa nahnu lahu_ muslimu_n
Wa kaza_ lika anzalna_ ilaikal kita_b fal lazina a_taina_humul kita_ba yuminu_na bih wa min ha_ ula_i may yuminu bih wa ma_ yajhadu bi a_ya_tina_ il lal ka_firu_n
Wa ma_ kunta tatlu_ min qablihi min kita_biw wa la_ tahut tuhu_ biyaminika izal lar ta_bal mubtilu_n
Bal huwa a_ya_tun bay yina_tun fi sudu_ril lazina u_tul ilm wa ma_ yajhadu bi a_ya_tina il laz za_limu_n
Wa qa_lu_ lau la_ unzila alaihi a_ya_tum mir rab bihi qul in namala_ya_tu indal la_h wa in nama_ ana nazirum mubin
Awalam yakfihim an na_ anzalna_ alaikal kita_ba yutla_ alaihim in na fi za_lika larahmataw wa zikra_ laqaumiy yuminu_n
Qul kafa_ bil la_hi baini wa bainakum sahida_ yalamu ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wal ard wal lazina a_manu_ bil ba_tili wa kafaru_ bil la_hi ula_ ika humul ha_siru_n
Wa yastajilu_naka bil aza_b wa lau la_ ajalum musam mal laja_ ahumul aza_b wa layatiyan nahum bagtataw wa hum la_ yasuru_n
Yastajilu_naka bil aza_b wa in na jahan nama lamuhitatum bil ka_firin
Yauma yagsa_humul aza_bu min fauqihim wa min tahti arjulihim wa yaqu_lu zu_qu_ ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
Ya_ iba_diyal lazina a_manu_ in na ardi wa_siatun fa iy ya_ya fabudu_n
Kul lu nafsin za_ iqatul maut sum ma ilaina_ turjau_n
Wal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti lanubaw wi an nahum minal jan nati gurafan tajri min tahtihal anha_ru ha_lidina fiha_ nima ajrul a_milin
Al lazina sabaru_ wa ala_ rab bihim yatawak kalu_n
Wa ka ay yim min da_b batil la_ tahmilu rizqaha_ al la_hu yarzuquha_ wa iy ya_kum wa huwas samiul alim
Wa la in sa altahum man halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa sah haras samsa wal qamara layaqu_lun nal la_h fa an na_ yufaku_n
Al la_hu yabsutur rizqa limay yasa_u min iba_dihi wa yaqdiru lah in nal la_ha bikul li sai in alim
Wa la in sa altahum man naz zala minas sama_i ma_ an fa ahya_ bihil arda min badi mautiha_ layaqu_lun nal la_h qulil hamdu lil la_h bal aksarahum la_ yaqilu_n
Wa ma_ ha_zihil haya_tud dun ya_ il la_ lahwuw wa laib wa in nad da_ral a_hirata lahiyal hayawa_n lau ka_nu_ yalamu_n
Fa iza_ rakibu_ fil fulki daawul la_ha muhlisina lahud din falam ma_ naj ja_hum il al bar ri iza_ hum yusriku_n
Liyakfuru_ bima_ a_taina_hum wa liyamat tau_ fasaufa yalamu_n
Awalam yarau an na_  ja'alna_ haraman a_minaw wa yutakhat tafun na_su min haulihim afabil ba_tili yuminu_na wa binimatil la_hi yakfuru_n
Wa man azlamu mim manif tara_ alal la_hi kaziban au kaz zaba bil haq qi lam ma ja_ah alaisa fi jahan nama maswal lil ka_firin
Wal lazina ja_hadu_ fina_ lanahdiyan nahum subulana_ wa in nal la_ha lama'al muhsinin
Alif la_m mim
Gulibati ru_m
Fi adnal ardi wa hum min badi galabihim sayaglibu_n
Fi bidi sinin lil la_hil amru min qablu wa min bad wa yauma iziy yafrahul muminu_n
Binasril la_h yansuru may yasya_ wa huwal azizur rahim
Wadal la_h la_ yuhliful la_hu wadahu_ wa la_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yalamu_n
Yalamu_na za_hiram minal haya_tid dun ya_ wa hum anil a_hirati hum ga_filu_n
Awalam yatafak karu_ fi anfusihim ma_ halaqal la_hus sama_wa_ti wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ il la_ bil haq qi wa ajalim musam ma_ wa in na kasiram minan na_si biliqa_i rab bihim laka_firu_n
Awalam yasi ru_ fil ardi fayanzuru_ kaifa ka_na a_qibatul lazina min qablihim ka_nu_ asyad da minhum quw wataw wa asa_rul arda wa amaru_ha_ aksara mim ma_ amaru_ha_ wa ja_ at hum rusuluhum bil bay yinati fama_ka_nal la_hu liyazlimahum wa la_kin ka_nu_ anfusahum yazlimu_n
Sum ma ka_na a_qibatal lazina asa_ us su_ a_ an kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_til la_hi wa ka_nu_ biha_ yastahzi u_n
Al la_hu yabda ul halqa sum ma yuiduhu_ sum ma ilaihi turjau_n
Wa yauma taqu_mus sa_atu yublisul mujrimu_n
Wa lam yakul lahum min suraka_ ihim sufaa_ u wa ka_nu_ bisuraka_him ka_firin
Wa yauma taqu_mus sa_atu yaumaiziy yatafar raqu_n
Fa am mal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti fahum fi raudatiy yuhbaru_n
Wa am mal lazina kafaru_ wa kaz zabu_ bi a_yatina_ wa liqa_ il a_hirati fa ula_ ika fil aza_bi muhdaru_n
Fasubha_nal la_hi hina tumsu_na wa hina tusbihu_n
Wa lahul hamdu fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa asiy yaw wa hina tuzhiru_n
Yuhrijul hay ya minal may yiti wa yuhrijul may yita minal hay yi wa yuhyil arda bada mautiha_ wa kaza_lika tuhraju_n
Wa min a_ya_tihi an halaqakum min tura_bin sum ma iza_ antum basyarun tantasiru_n
Wa min a_ya_tihi an halaqalakum min anfusikum azwa_jal litaskunu_ ilaiha_ wa ja'ala bainakum mawad dataw wa rahmah in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til laqaumiy yatafak karu_n
Wa min a_ya_tihi halqus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wahtila_fu alsinatikum wa alwa_nikum in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til lila_lamin
Wa min a_ya_tihi mana_mukum bil laili wan naha_ri wabtiga_ ukum min fadlih in na fi za_lika la_ a_ya_til liqaumiy yasmau_n
Wa min a_ya_tihi yurikumul barqa haufaw wa tama'aw wa yunaz zilu minas sama_i ma_ an fayuhyi bihil arda bada mautiha_ in na fi za_lika la a_yatil liqaumiy yaqilu_n
Wa min a_ya_tihi an taqu_mas sama_ u wal ardu bi amrihi sum ma iza_ daa_kum dawatam minal ardi iza_ antum tahruju_n
Wa lahu_ man fis sama_wa_ti wal ard kul lul lahu_ qa_nitu_n
Wa huwal lazi yabdaul halqa sum ma yuiduhu_ wa huwa ahwanu alaih wa lahul matsalul ala_ fis sama_wa_ti wal ard wa huwal azizul hakim
Daraba lakum masalam min anfusikum hal lakum mim ma_ malakat aima_nukum min suraka_a fi ma_ razaqna_kum fa antum fihi sawa_ un taha_fu_nahum kakifatikum anfusakum kaza_lika nufas silul a_ya_ti liqaumiy yaqilu_n
Balit taba'al lazina zalamu_ ahwa_ ahum bigairi ilm famay yahdi man adal lal la_h wa ma_ lahum min na_sirin
Fa aqim wajhaka lid dini hanifa_ fitratal la_hil lati fataran na_sa alaiha_ la_ tabdila lihalqil la_h za_likad dinul qay yimu wa la_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yalamu_n
Munibina ilaihi wat taqu_hu wa aqimus sala_ta wa la_ taku_nu_ minal musrikin
Minal lazina far raqu_ dinahum wa ka_nu_ siyaa_ kul lu hizbin bima_ ladaihim farihu_n
Wa iza_ mas san na_sa dur run daau rab bahum munibina ilaihi sum ma iza_ aza_qahum minhu rahmatan iza_ fariqum minhum birab bihim yusriku_n
Liyakfuru_ bima_ a_taina_hum fatamat tau_ fasaufa talamu_n
Am anzalna_ alaihim sulta_nan fahuwa yatakal lamu bima_ ka_nu_ bihi yusriku_n
Wa iza_ adzaqnan na_sa rahmatan farihu_ biha_ wa in tushibhum say yi atun bima_ qad damat aidihim iza_ hum yaqnatu_n
Awalam yarau an nal la_ha yabsutur rizqa limay yasya_ u wa yaqdir in nafi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy yuminu_n
Fa a_ti zal qurba_ haq qahu_ wal miskina wabnas sabil za_lika hairul lil lazina yuridu_na wajhal la_hi wa ula_ika humul muflihu_n
Wa ma_ a_taitum mir ribal liyar buwa_fi amwa_lin na_si fala_ yarbu_ indal la_h wa ma_ a_taitum min zaka_tin turidu_na wajhal la_hi fa ula_ ika humul mudifu_n
Al la_hul lazi halaqakum sum ma razaqakum sum ma yumitukum sum ma yuhyikum hal min suraka_ ikum may yafalu min za_likum min sai subha_nahu_ wa taa_la_ am ma_ yusriku_n
Zaharal fasa_du fil bar ri wal bahri bima_ kasabat aidin na_si liyuziqahum badal lazi amilu_ la'al lahum yarjiu_n
Qul siru_ fil ardi fanzuru_ kaifa ka_na a_qibatul lazina min qabl ka_na aksaruhum musrikin
Fa aqim wajhaka lid dinil qay yimi min qabli ay yatiya yaumul la_ marad da lahu_ minal la_hi yauma iziy yasad dau_n
Man kafara fa'alaihi kufruh wa man amila sa_lihan fali anfusihim yamhadu_n
Liyajziyal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti min fadlih in nahu_ la_ yuhib bul ka_firin
Wa min a_ya_tihi ay yursilar riya_ha mubas sira_tiw wa liyuzqakum mir rahmatihi wa litajriyal fulku bi amrihi wa litabtagu_ min fadlihi wa la'al lakum taskuru_n
Wa laqad arsalna_ min qablika rusulan ila_ qaumihim faja_ u_hum bil bay yina_ti fantaqamna_ minal lazina ajramu_ wa ka_na haq qan alaina_ nasrul muminin
Al la_hul lazi yursilur riya_ha fatutsiru saha_ban fayabsutuhu_ fis sama_i kaifa yasya_u wa yajaluhu_ kisafan fataral waqda yahruju min hila_lih fa iza_ asha_ba bihi may yasya_ u min iba_dihi iza_ hum yastabsiru_n
Wa in ka_nu_ min qabli ay yunaz zala alaihim min qablihi lamublisin
Fanzur ila_ a_sa_ri rahmatil la_hi kaifa yuhyil arda bada mautiha_ in na za_lika lamuhyil mauta_ wa huwa ala_ kul li sai in qadir
Wa la in arsalna_ rihan fara auhu musfar ral lazal lu_ min badihi yakfuru_n
Fa in naka la_ tusmiul mauta_ wa la_ tusmius sum mad dua_ a iza_ wal lau mudbirin
Wa ma_ anta biha_dil umyi an dala_tihim in tusmiu il la_ may yuminu bi a_ya_tina_ fahum muslimu_n
Ala_hul lazi halaqakum min dufin sum ma ja'ala min badi dafin quw watan sum ma jaala min badi quw watin dafan wasai batan yahluku ma_ yasya_ u wahuwal alimul qadir
Wa yauma taqu_mus sa_atu yuqmisul mujrimu_na ma_ labisu_ gaira sa_a_h kaza_lika ka_nu_ yufaku_n
Wa qa_lal lazina u_tul ilma wal ima_na laqad labistum fi kita_bil la_hi ila_ yaumil basi faha_za_ yaumul basi wa la_kin nakum kuntum la_ talamu_n
Fayauma izil la_ yanfaul lazina zalamu_ maziratuhum wa la_ hum yustatabu_n

Kaza_lika yatbaul la_hu ala_ qulu_bil lazina la_ yalamu_n

Alif la_m mim
Tilka a_ya_tul kita_bil hakim
Hudaw wa rahmatal lilmuhsinin
Al lazina yuqimu_nas sala_ta wayutu_naz zaka_ta wahum bil a_hiratihum yu_qinu_n
Ula_ ika ala_ hudam mir rabihim wa ula_ ika humul muflihu_n
Wa minan na_si may yastari lahwal hadisi liyudil la an sabilil la_hi bigairi ilmiw wa yat tahizaha_ huzuwa_ ula_ ika lahum aza_bum muhin
Wa iza_ tutla_ alaihi a_ya_tuna_ wal la_ mustakbiran ka ak kam yasmaha_ ka a na fi uzunaihi waqra_ fabas sirhu biaza_bin alim
In nal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti lahum jan na_tun naim
Ha_lisina fiha_ wa dal la_hi haq qa_ wa huwal azizul hakim
Halaqas sama_wa_ti bigairi amadin taraunaha_ wa alqa_ fil ardi rawa_siya an tamida bikum wa bas sa fiha_ min kul li da_b bah wa anzalna_  minas sama_i ma_ an fa an batna_ fiha_ min kul li zaujin karim
Ha_za_ halqul la_hi fa aru_ni ma_za_ halaqal lazina min du_nih baliz za_limu_na fi dala_lim mubin
Wa laqad a_taina_ luma_nal hikmata aniskur lil la_h wa may yaskur fain nama_ yaskur linafsih wa man kafara fa in nal la_ha ganiy yun hamid
Wa iz qa_la luqma_nu libnihi wa huwa yaizuhu_ ya_bunay ya la_ tusrik bil la_h in nas sirka lazhulmun azim
Wa was sainal insa_na biwa_lidaih hamalat hu um muhu_ wahnan ala_ wahniw wa fisa_luhu_ fi a_maini aniskur li wa liwa_lidaik ilay yal masir
Wa in ja_hada_ka ala_ antusrika bi ma_ laisa laka bihi ilmun fala_ tuti huma_ wa sa_hibhuma_ fid dun ya_ maru_faw wat tabi sabila man ana_ba ilay ya sum ma ilay ya marjiukum fa unab bi ukum bima_ kuntum tamalu_n
Ya_ bunay ya in naha_ in taku misqa_la hab batim min hardalin fatakun fi sakratin au fis sama_wa_ti au fil ardi yati bihal la_h in nal la_ha latifun habir
Ya_ bunay ya aqimis sala_ta wamur bil maru_fi wanha anil munkari was bir ala_ ma_ asa_bak in na za_lika min azmil umu_r
Wa la_ tushair khad daka lin na_si wa la_ tamsi fil ardi maraha_ in nal la_ha la_ yuhib bu kul la muhta_lin faku_r
Waqsid fi masyika wagdud min sautik in na ankaral azwa_ti lashautul hamir
Alam tarau an nal la_ha sak kara lakum ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi wa asbaga alaikum niamahu_ za_hirataw wa ba_tinah wa minan na_si may yuja_dilu fil la_hi baigairi ilmiw wa la_ hudaw wa la_ kita_bim munir

Ma_ halqukum wa la_ basukum il la_ kanafsiw wa_hidah in nal la_ha samiun basir

Alif la_m mim
Tanzilul kita_bi la_ raiba fihi mir rab bil a_lamin

An nabiy yu aula_ bil muminina min anfusihim wa azwa_juhu_ um maha_tuhum wa ulul arha_mi baduhum aula_ bibadin fi kita_bil la_hi minal muminina wal muha_jirina il la_ an talalu_ ila_ auliya_ ikum maru_fa_ ka_na za_lika fil kita_bi masu_ra_

Liyas alassa_diqin an sidqihim wa a'ad da lilka_firina aza_ban alima_
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manuz kuru_ nimatal la_hi alaikum iz ja_ atkum junu_dun fa arsalna_ alaihim rihaw wa junu_dal lam tarauha_ wa ka_nal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na basira_

Huna_likab tuliyal muminu_na wa zul zilu_ zilza_la_n sadida_
Wa iz yaqu_lul muna_fiqu_na wal lazina fi qulu_bihim maradum ma_ wa'adanal la_hu wa rasu_luhu il la_ guru_ra_
Wa iz qa_lat ta_ ifatum minhum ya_ ahla yasriba la_ muqa_ma lakum farjiu_ wa yastazinu fariqum minhumun nabiy ya yaqu_lu_na in na buyu_tana_ aurah wa ma_ hiya biauratin iy yuridu_na il la_ fira_ra_

Iy yasya yuz hibkum wa yati bihalqin jadid
Wa ma_ za_lika alal la_hi bi aziz
Wa la_ taziru wa_ziratuw wizra uhra_ wa in tadu musqalatun ila_ himliha_ la_ yuhmal minhu sai uw wa lau ka_na za_qurba_ in nama_ tunzirul lazina yahsauna rab bahum bil gaibi wa aqa_mus sala_h wa man tazak ka_ fa in nama_ yatazak ka_ linafsih wa ilal la_hil masir
Wa ma_ yastawil ama_ wal basir
Wa laz zulu ma_tu wa lan nu_r
Wa laz zil lu wa lal haru_r
Wa ma_ yastawil ahya_u wa lal amwa_t in nal la_ha yusmiu may yasya_ wa ma_ anta bimusmiim man fil qubu_r
In anta il la_ nazir
In na_ arsalna_ka bil haq qi basiraw wa nazira_ wa in min um matin il la_ hala_ fiha_ nazir
Wa iy yukaz zibu_ka faqad kaz zabal lazina min qablihim ja_ athum rusuluhum bil bay yina_ti wa biz zuburi wa bil kita_bil munir
Sum ma ahaztul lazina kafaru_ fakaifa ka_na nakir
Alam tara an nal la_ha anzala minas sama_ ma_ fa ahrajna_ bihi samara_tim muhtalifan alwa_nuha_ wa minal jiba_li judadun biduw wa humrum muhtalifun alwa_nuha_ wa gara_bibu su_d
Wa minan na_si wa dawa_b bi wal ana_mi muhtalifun alwa_nuhu_ kaza_lik in nama_ yahsal la_ha min iba_dihil ulama_u in nal la_ha azizun gafu_r
In nal lazina yatlu_na kita_bal la_hi wa aqa_mus sala_ta wa anfaqu_ mim ma_ razaqna_hum sir raw wa ala_niyatay yarju_na tija_ratal lan tabu_r
Liyuwaf fiyahum uju_rahum wa yazidahum min fadlih in nahu_ gafu_run saku_r
Wal lazi auhaina_ ilaika minal kita_bi huwal haq qu musad diqal lima_ baina yadaih in nal la_ha bi iba_dihi lahabirun basir
Sum ma aurasnal lazinas tafaina_ min iba_dina_ faminhum za_limul linafsih wa minhum muqtasid wa minhum sa_biqun bil haira_ti bi iznil la_h za_lika huwal fadlul kabir
Jan na_tu adniy yadhulu_naha_ yuhal launa fiha_ min asa_wira min zahabiw wa luluan wa liba_suhum fiha_ harir
Wa qa_lul hamdu lil la_hil lazi azhaba an nal hazan in na rab bana_ lagfu_run saku_r
Al lazi ahal lana_ da_ral muqa_mati min fadlih la_ yamas suna_ fiha_ nasabuw wala_ yamas suna_ fiha_ lugu_b
Wal lazina kafaru_ lahum na_ru jahan nam la_ yuqda_ alaihim fayamu_tu_ wala_ yukaf fafu anhum min aza_biha_ kaza_lika najzi kul la kafu_r
Wa hum yastariku_na fiha_ rabana_ ahrijna_ namal sa_lihan gairal lazi kun na_ namal awalam nuam mirkum ma_ yatazak karu fihi man tazak kara wa ja_ akumun nazir fazu_qu_ fama_ liz za_limin na min nasir
In nal la_ha alimu gaibis sama_wa_ti wal ard in nahu_ alimun biza_tis sudu_r
Huwal lazi jaalakum hala_ ifa fil ard faman kafara fa'alaihi kufruh wa la_ yazidul ka_firina kufruhum inda rab bihim il la_ maqta_ wa la_ yazidul ka_firina kufruhum il la_ hasa_ra_
Qul ara aitum suraka_ akumul lazina tadu_na min du_nil la_h aru_ni ma_za_ halaqu_ minal ardi am lahum sirkun fis sama_wa_t am a_taina_hum kita_ban fahum ala_ bayinatim min bal iy yaiduz za_limu_na baduhum badan il la_ guru_ra_
In nal la_ha yumsikus sama_wa_ti wal arda an tazu_la_ wala in za_lata_ in amsakahuma_ min afadim min badih in nahu_ ka_na haliman gafu_ra_
Wa aqsamu_ bil la_hi jahda aima_nihim la in ja_ ahum nazirul layaku_nan na ahda_ min ihdal umam falama_ ja_ ahum nazirum ma_ za_dahum il la_ nufu_ra_
Istikba_ran fil ardi wa makras say yi wa la_ yahiqul makrus say yi u il la_ bi ahlil fahal yansuru_na il la_ sunatal aw walin falan tajida lisun natil la_hi tabdila_ walan tajida lisun natil la_hi tahwila_
Awalam yasiru_ fil ardi fayanzuru_ kaifa ka_na a_qibatul lazina min qablihim wa ka_nu_ asad da minhum quw wah wa ma_ ka_nal la_hu liyujizahu_ min sai in fis sama_wa_ti wa la_ fil ard in nahu_ ka_na aliman qadira_
Wa lau yu a_hizul la_hun na_sa bima_ kasabu_ ma_ taraka ala_ zahriha_ min da_b batiw wa la_kiy yu ahiruhum ila_ ajalim musam ma_ fa iza_ ja_ a aja luhum fa in nal la_ha ka_na biiba_dihi basira
Ya_ sin
Wal qur a_nil hakim
In naka laminal mursalin
Ala_ sira_tim mustaqim
Tanzilal azizir rahim
Litunzira qaumam ma_ unzira a_ba_ uhum fahum ga_filu_n
Laqad haq qal qaulu ala_ aksarihim fahum la_ yuminu_n
In na_ jaalna_ fi ana_qihim agla_lan fahiya ilal azqa_ni fahum muqmahu_n
Wa ja'alna_ min baini aidihim sad daw wa min halfihim sad dan fa agsaina_hum fahum la_ yubsiru_n
Wa sawa_ un alaihim a anzartahum am lam tunzirhum la_ yuminu_n
In nama_ tunziru manit taba'azikra wa hasyiyar rahma_na bil gaib fabas sirhu bimagfiratiw wa ajrin karim
In na nahnu nuhyil mauta wa naktubu ma_ qad damu_ wa a_sa_rahum wa kul la sai in ahsaina_hu fi ima_mim mubin
Wadrib lahum masalan asha_bal qaryah iz ja_ ahal mursalu_n
Iz arsalna_ ilaimus naini fakaz zabu_huma_ fa'az zazna_ bitsa_lisin faqa_lu_ in na_ ilaikum mursalu_n
Qa_lu_ ma_ antum il la_ basarum misluna_ wa ma_ anzalar rahma_nu min sai in in antum il la_ takzibu_n
Qa_lu_ rab buna_ yalamu in na_ ilaikum lamursalu_n
Wa ma_ alaina_ il lal bala_gul mubin
Qa_lu_ in na_ tatay yarna_ bikum la il lam tantahu_ lanarjuman nakum wa layamas san nakum min na_ aza_bun alim
Qa_lu_ ta_ irukum maakum a in zuk kirtum bal antum qaumum musrifu_n
Wa ja_ a min aqsal madinati rajuluy yasa_ qa_la ya_ qaumit tabiul mursalin
At tabiu_ mal la_ yas alukum ajraw wa hum muhtadu_n
Wa ma_ liya la_ abudul lazi fatarani wa ilaihi turjau_n
A at takhizu min du_nihi a_lihatan iy yuridnir rahma_nu bidur ril la_ tugni an ni syafa_atuhum sai aw wa la_ yunqizu_n
In ni izal lafi dala_lim mubin
In ni a_mantu birab bikum fasmau_n
Qiladkhulil jan nah qa_la ya_laita qaumi yalamu_n
Bima gafara li rab bi wa jaalani minal mukramin
Wa ma_ anzalna_ ala_ qaumihi mim badi min jundim minas sama_ I wama_ kun na_ munzilin
In ka_nat il la_ saihataw wa_hidatan fa iza_ hum kha_midu_n
Ya_ hasratan alal iba_d ma_ yatihim mir rasu_lin il la_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
Alam yarau kam ahlakna_ qablahum minal quru_ni an nahum ilaihim la_ yarjiu_n
Wa in kul lu lam ma_ jamiul ladaina_ muhdaru_n
Wa a_ya_tul lahumul ardhul maitah ahyaina_ha_ wa akhrajna_ minha_ haban faminhu yakulu_n
Wa ja'alna_ fiha_ jan ja_tim min nakhiliw wa ana_biw wa faj jarna_ fiha_ minal uyu_n
Liyakulu_ min samarihi wa ma_ amilat hu aidihim afala_ yaskuru_n
Subha_nal lazi khalaqal azwa_ja kul laha_ mim ma_ tun bitul ardu wa min anfusihim wa mim ma_ la_ yalamu_n
Wa a_yatul lahumul lail naslakhu minhun naha_ra fa iza_ hum muzlimu_n
Was samsu tajri limustaqar ril laha_ za_lika taqdirul azizil alim
Wal qamara qad darna_hu mana_zila hat ta_ a_da kal urju_nil qadim
Las samsu yan bagi laha_ an tudrikal qamara wa lal lailu sa_biqun naha_r wa kul lun fi falakiy yasbahu_n
Wa a_yatul lahum an na_ hamalna_ zur riy yatahum fil fulkil mashu_n
Wa khalaqna_ lahum mim mitslihi ma_ yarkabu_n
Wa in nasa nugriqhum fala_ sarika lahum wa la_ hum yunqazu_n
Il la_ rahmatam min na_ wa mata_an ila_ hin
Wa iza_ qila lahumut taqu_ ma_ baina aidikum wa ma_ khalfakum la'al lakum turhamu_n
Wa ma_ tatihim min a_ya_tim min a_ya_ti rab bihim il la_ ka_nu_ anha_ muridin
Wa iza_ qila lahum anfiqu_ mim ma_ razaqakumul la_hu qa_lal lazina kafaru_ lil lazina a_manu_ anutimu mal lau yasya_ ul la_hu atamahu_ in antum il la_ fi ala_lim mubin
Wa yaqu_lu_na mata_ ha_zal wadu in kuntum sa_diqin
Ma_ yanzuru_na il la_ saihataw wa_hidatan takhuzuhum wa hum yakhis simu_n
Fala_ yastatiu_na tausiyataw wa la_ ila_ ahlihim yarjiu_n
Wa nufikha fis su_ri fa iza_ hum minal ajda_tsi ila_ rab bihim yansilu_n
Qa_lu_ ya_ wailana_ man baatsana_ mim marqadina_ ha_za_ ma_ wa'adar rahma_nu wa sadaqal mursalu_n
In ka_nat il la_ saihataw wa_hidatan fa iza_ hum jamiul ladaina_ muhdaru_n
Fal yauma la_ tuzlamu nafsun sai aw wa la_ tujzauna il la_ ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
In na asha_bal jan natil yauma fi sugulin fa_kihu_n
Hum wa azwa_juhum fi zila_lin alal ara_ iki mut taki u_n
Lahum fiha_ fa_kihatuw wa lahum ma_ yad dau_n
Sala_mun qaulam mir rab bir rahim
Wamta_zul yauma ay yuhal mujrimu_n
Alam ahad ilaikum ya_ bani a_dama al la_ tabudus saita_n in nahu_ lakum aduw wum mubin
Wa ani budu_ni ha_za_sira_tum mustaqim
Wa laqad adhal la minkum jibil lan katsira_ afalam taku_nu_ taqilu_n
Ha_zihil jahan namul lati kuntum tu_adu_n
Islauhal yauma bima_ kuntum takfuru_n
Alyauma nakhtimu ala_ afwa_hihim wa tukal limuna_ aidihim wa tashadu arjuluhum bima_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
Wa lau nasya_u lathamasna_ ala_ ayunihim fastabaqus sira_ta fa an na_ yubsiru_n
Wa lau nasya_ u lama sakhna_hum ala_ maka_ natihim famas tata_u_ mudiy yaw wa la_ yarjiu_n
Wa man nuam mirhu nunak kis hu fil khalq afala_ yaqilu_n
Wa ma_ al lamna_hus sira wa ma_ yan bagil lah in huwa il la_ zikruw wa qur a_num mubin
Liyunzira man ka_na hay yaw wa yahiq qal qaulu alal ka_firin
Awalam yarau an na_ khalaqna_ lahum mim ma_ amilat aidina_ an a_man fahum laha_ ma_likum
Wa zal lalna_ha_ lahum faminha_ raku_buhum wa minha_ yakulum
Wa lahum fiha_ mana_fiu wa masya_rib afala_ yaskurun
Wat takahuzu_ min du_nil la_hi a_lihatal la'at lahum yunsaru_n
La_ yastatiu_na nasrahum wa hum lahum jundum muhdaru_n
Fala_ yahzunka qauluhum in na_ nalamu ma_ yusir ru_na wa ma_ yulinu_n
Awa lam yaral insa_nu an na_ khalaqna_hu min nutfatin fa iza_ huwa  khasimum mubin
Wa daraba lana_ matsalaw wa nasiya halqah qa_la may yuhyil iza_ma wahiya ramim
Qul yuhyi hal lazi an sa aha_ aw wala mar rah wa huwa bikul li khalqin alim
Nil lazi ja'ala lakum minas sajaril akhdari na_ran fa iza_ antum minhu tu_qidu_n
Awa laisal lazi khalaqnas sama_wa_ti wal arda biqa_dirin ala_ ay yakhluqa mitslahum bala_ wa huwal khal la_qul alim
In nama_ amruhu_ iza_ ara_da sai an ay yaqu_la lahu_ kun fayaku_n
Fasubha_nal lazi biyadihi malaku_tu kul li sai aw wa ilaihi turjau_n
