Aja alal a_lihata ila_haw wa_hida_ in na ha_za_ lasyai uja_b
Wantalaqal mala u minhum anim su_ wasbiru_ ala_ a_lihatikum in na ha_za_ lasyai uy yura_d
Ma_ samina_ biha_za_ fil mil latil a_khirah in ha_za_ il lak tila_q
A unzila alaihiz zikru min bainina_ bal hum fi sak kim min zikri bal lam ma_ yazu_qu_
Am indahum khaza_ inu rahmati rab bikal azizil wah hab
Am lahum mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ fal yartaqu_ fil asba_b
Jundum ma_ huna_lika mahzu_mum minal ahza_b
Kaz zabat qablahum qaumu nu_hiw wa a_duw wa firaunu zul auta_d
Wa samu_du wa qaumu lu_tiw wa asha_bul aikah ula_ ikal ahza_b
In kul lun il la_ kaz zabar rusula fahaq qa iqa_b
Wa ma_ yanzuru ha_ ula_ I il la_ saihataw wa_hidatam ma_ laha_ min fawa_q
Wa qa_lu_ rab bana_ aj jil lana_ qitana_ qabla yaumil hisa_b
Isbir ala_ ma_ yaqu_lu_na waz kur abdana_ da_wu_da zal aid in nahu_ aw wa_b
In na_ sak karna_l jiba_la ma'ahu_ yusab bihna bil asyiy yi wal isra_q
Wat taira mahsu_rah kul lul lahu_ aw wa_b
Wa sadadna_ mulkahu_ wa a_taina_hul hikmata wa faslal khita_b
Wa hal ata_ka naba ul hasmi iz ta saw warul mihra_b
Iz dakalu_ ala_ da_wu_da fafazia minhum qa_lu_ la_ takhal hasma_ni baga_ baduna_ ala_  badin fahkum bainana_ bil haq qi wa la_ tustit wahdina_ ila_ sawa_ is sira_t
In na ha_za_ akhi lahu_ tisuw wa tisu_na najataw waliya najatuw wa_ hidah fa qa_la akfilniha_ wa az zani fil khita_b
Qa_la laqad zalamaka bisu a_li najatika ila_ nia_jih wain na katsiram minal hulata_i layabgi baduhum ala_ badin il lal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti wa qalilum ma_ hum wa zan na da_wu_du an nama_ fatan na_hufastagfara rab bahu_ wa khar ra ra_ki aw wa ana_h
Faghafarna_ lahu_ za_lik wa in na lahu_ indana_ lazulfa_ wa husna_ ma a_b
Ya_ da_wu_du in na_ ja'alna_ka kalifatan fil ardi fahkum bainan na_si bil haq qi wa la_ tat tabi il hawa_ fayudil laka an sabilil la_h in nal lazina yadil lu_na an sabilil la_hi lahum aza_bun sadidun  bima_ na su_ yaumal hisa_b
Wa ma_ khalaqnas sama_ a wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ ba_tila_ za_lika zan nul lazina kafaru_ fawailul lil lazina kafaru_ minan na_r
Am najalul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti kal mufsidina fil ard am najalul mut taqina kal fuj ja_r
Kita_bun anzalna_hu ilaika muba_rakul liyad dab baru_ a_ya_tihi wa liyatazak kara ulul alba_b
Wa wahabna_ lida_wu_da sulaima_n nimal abd in nahu_ aw wa_b
Iz urida alaihi bil asyiy yis sa_fina_tul jiya_d
Faqa_la in ni ahbabtu hub bal khairi an zikri rab bi hat ta_ tawa_rat bil hija_b
Rud du_ha_ alay fatafiqa mas ham bis su_qi wal ana_q
Wa laqad fatan na_ sulaima_na wa al qaina_ ala_ kursiy yihi jasadan sum ma ana_b
Qa_la rab bigfir li wa hab li mulkal la_ yan bagi li ahadim min badi in naka antal wah ha_b
Fasak karna_ lahur riha tajri bi am rihi ruka_ an haitsu asha_b
Was saya_tina kul la ban na_ iw wa gaw wa_s
Wa a_khirina muqar ranina fil asfa_d
Ha_za_ ata_ una_ famnun au amsik bigairi hisa_b
Wa in na lahu_ indana_ lazulfa_ wa husna ma a_b
Wazkur abdana_ ay yu_b iz na_da_ rab bahu_ an ni mas saniyas saita_nu binusbiw wa aza_b
Urkud birijlik ha_za_ mugtasalun ba_riduw wa sara_b
Wa wahabna_ lahu_ ahlahu_ wa mitslahum maahum rahmatam min na_ wa zikra_ li ulil alba_b
Wa kuz biyadika digsan fadrib bihi wa la_ takhnats in na_ wajadna_hu sa_bira_ nimal abdu in nahu_ aw wa_b
Wazkur iba_dana_ ibra_hima wa isha_q wa yaqu_ba ulil aidi wal absa_r
In na_ akhlasna_hum bikha_lisatin zikrad da_r
Wa in nahum indana_ laminal mustafainal akhya_r
Wazkur isma_ila wal yasaa wa zal kif wa kul lum minal akhya_r
Ha_za_ zikr wa in na lilmut taqina lahusnu ma a_b
Jan na_ti adnim mufat tahatal lahumul abwa_b
Mut taki na fiha_ yadu_na fiha_ bifa_kihatin katsiratiw wa sara_b
Wa indahum qa_sira_tut tarfi atra_b
Ha_za_ ma_ tu_adu_na liyaumi hisa_b
In na ha_za_ larizquna_ ma_ lahu_ min nafa_d
Ha_za_ wa in na lit ta_ghina lasar ra ma a_b
Jahan nam yaslaunaha_ fabisal miha_d
Ha_za_ falyazu_qu_hu hamimuw wa gas sa_q
Wa a_kharu min saklihi azwa_j
Ha_za_ faijum muqtahimum maakum la_ marhaban bihim in nahum sa_lun na_r
Qa_lu_ bal antum la_ marhaban bikum antum qad damtumu_hu lana_ fabisal qara_r
Qa_lu_ rab bana_ man qad dama lana_ ha_za_ fazid hu aza_ban difan fin na_r
Wa qa_lu_ ma_ lana_ nara_ rija_lan kun na_ naud duhum minal asra_r
At takazna_hum sikriy yan am za_gat anhumul absa_r
In na za_lika lahaq qun taka_shumu ahlin na_r
Qul in nama_ ana munziruw wa ma_ min ila_hin il lal la_hul wa_hidul qaha_r
Rab bus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahumal azizul gaf fa_r
Qul huwa naba un azim
Antum anhu muridu_n
Ma_ ka_na liya min ilmin bil mala il ala_ iz yahtasimu_n
Iy yuha_ ilay ya il la_ an nama_ ana nazirum mubin
Iz qa_la rab buka lilmala_ ikati in ni kha_liqun basyaram min tin
Fa iza_ saw waituhu_ wa nafaktu fihi mir ru_hi faqau_ lahu_ sa_jidin
Fasajadal mala_ ikatu kul luhum ajmau_n
Il la_ iblis istakbara wa ka_na minal ka_firin
Qa_la ya_ iblisu ma_ manaaka an tasjuda lima_ khalaqtu biyaday ya astakbarta am kunta minal a_lin
Qa_la ana_ khairum minhu khalaqtani min na_riw wa khalaqtahu_ min tin
Qa_la fakruj minha fa in naka rajim
Wa in na alaika lanati ila_ yaumid din
Qa_la rab bi fa anirni ila_ yaumi yub atsu_n
Qa_la fa in naka minal munzarin
Ila_ yaumil waqtil malu_m
Qa_la fabiiz zatika la ugwiyan nahum ajmain
Il la_ iba_daka minhumul muklasin
Qa_la fal haq qu wal haq qa aqu_l
La amla an na jahan nama minka wa mim man tabiaka minhum ajmain
Qul ma_ as alukum alaihi min ajriw wa ma_ ana minal mutakal lifin
In huwa il la_ zikrul lil a_lamin
Wa latalamun na naba ahu_ bada hin
Tanzilul kita_bi minal la_hil azizil hakim
In na anzalna_ ilaikal kita_ba bil  haqi fa budil la_ha mukhlisal lahud din
Ala_ lil la_hid dinul ha_lis wal lazinat takhazu_ min du_nihi auliya_ a ma_ nabuduhum il la_ liyuqar ribu_na_ ilal la_hi zulfa_ in nal la_ha yahkumu bainahum fi ma_ hum fihi yahtalifu_n in nal la_ha la_ yahdi man huwa ka_zibun kaf fa_r
Lau ara_dal la_hu ay yat takhiza wa ladal lastafa_ mim ma_ yakhluqu ma_ yasya_ u subha_nah huwal la_hul wa_hidul qah ha_r
Halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda bil haq yukaw wirul laila Qalan naha_ri wa yukaw wirun naha_ra alal laili wa sah haras samsa wal qamar kul luy yajri li ajalim musam ma_ ala_ huwal azizul gaf fa_r
Halaqakum min nafsiw wa_hidatin sum ma ja'ala minha_ zaujaha_ wa anzala lakum minal ana_mi sama_niyata azwa_j yahlukuqum fi butu_ni ummaha_tikum halqam min badi halqin fi zuluma_tin sala_ts za_likumul la_hu rab bukum lahul mulku la_ ila_ha il la_ huw fa an na_ tusrafu_n
In takfuru_ fa in nal la_ha ganiy yun ankum wa la_ yarda_ liiba_dihil kufr wa in taskuru_ yardahu lakum wa la_ taziru wa_ziratuw wizra ukha_ sum ma ila_ rab bikum marjiukum fayunab bi ukum bima_ kuntum tamalu_na in nahu_ alimun biza_tis sudu_r
Wa iza_ masal insa_na dur run daa_ rab bahu_ muniban ilaihi sum ma iza_ haw wa lahu_ nimatam minhu nasiya ma_ ka_na yadu_ ilaihi min qablu wa ja'ala lil la_hi anda_dal liyudil la an sabilih qul tamat bikufrika qalilan in naka min as ha_bin na_r
Am man huwa qa_nitun a_na_ al laili sa_jidaw waqa_ imay yah zarul a_hirata wa yarju_ rahmata rab bih qul hal yastaw lazina yalamu_na wal lazina la yalamu_n in nama_ yatazak karu ulul alba_b
Qul ya_ iba_dil lazina a_manut taqu_ rab bakum lil lazina ahsanu_ fi ha_zihid dun ya_ hasanah wa ardul la_hi wa_siah in nama_ yuwaf fas sabiru_na ajrahum bigairi hisa_b
Qul in ni umirtu an abudal la_ha muhlisal lahud din
Wa umirtu li an aku_na aw walal muslimin
Qul in ni akha_fu in ashaitu rab bi aza_ba yaumin azim
Qulil la_hi abudu muhlisal lahu_ dini
Fabudu_ ma_ situm min du_nih qul in nal ha_sirinal lazina hasiru_ anfusahum wa ahlihim yaumal qiya_mah ala_ za_lika huwal husra_nul mubin
Lahum min fauqihim zulalum minan na_ri wa min tahtihim zulal za_lika yukaw wiful la_hu bihi iba_dah ya_ iba_di fat taqu_n
Wal lazinaj tanabut ta_gu_ta ay yabudu_ha_ wa ana_bu_ ilal la_hi la humul busra_ fabas sir iba_d
Al lazina yastamiu_nal qaula fayat tbiu_na ahsanah ula_ ikal lazina hada_humul la_hu wa ula_ ika hum ulul alba_b
Afaman haq qa alaihi kalimatul aza_b afa anta tunqizu man fin na_r
La_kinil lazinat rab bahum lahum gurafum min fauqiha_ gurafum mabniy yatun tajri min tahtihal anha_ru wadal la_h la_ yuhliful la_hul mia_d
Alam tara an nal la_ha anzala minas sama_ i ma_ an fasalakahu_ yana_bia fil ardi sum ma yuhriju bihi zaram muhtalifan alwa_nuhu_ sum ma yahiju fatara_hu musfar ran sum ma yajaluhu_ huta_man in na fi za_lika lazikra_ li ulil alba_b
Afaman sarahal la_hu sadrahu_ lil isla_mi fahuwa ala_ nu_rim mir rabih fawailul lilqa_siyati qulu_buhum min zikril la_h ula_ ika fi dala_lim mubin
Al la_hu naz zala ahsanal hadisi kita_bam mutasa_biham matsa_ niyataq sa ir ru minhu julu_dul lazina yahsauna rab bahum sum ma talinu julu_duhum wa qulu_buhum ila_ zikril la_h za_lika hudal la_hi yahdi bihi may yasya_ wa man yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ min ha_d
Afamay yat taqi biwajihi su_ al aza_bi yaumal qiya_mati wa qila liz za_limina zu_qu_ ma_ kuntum taksibu_n
Kaz zabal lazina min qablihim fa_ta_humul aza_bu min haitsu la_ yasuru_n
Fa aza_qahumul la_hul hizya fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa la'aza_bul a_hirati akbar lau ka_nu_ yalamu_n
Wa laqad darabna_ lin na_si fi haa_zal qur a_ni min kul li matsalil la al lahum yatazak karu_n
Qur a_nan arabiy yan gaira zi iwajil la'al lahum yat taqu_n
Darabal la_hu matsaral rajulan fihi suraka_ u mutasa_kisu_na wa rajulan salamal lirajulin hal yastawiya_ni matsalan alhamdu lil la_h bal aksaruhum la_ yalamu_n
In naka may yituw wa in nahum may yitu_n
Sum ma in nakum yaumal qiya_mati inda rab bikum taktasimu_n
Faman azhlamu mim man kazaba alal la_hi wa kaz zaba bis sidiq iz ja_ ah alaisa fi jahan nama matswal lilka_firin
Wal lazi ja_ a bis sidiq qa sad daqa bihi ula_ ika humul mut taqu_n
Lahum ma_ yasya_ u_na inda rab bihim za_lika jaza_ ul muhsinin
Liyukaf firal lahu anhum aswa al lazi amilu wa yajziyahum ajrahum bi ahsani lazi ka_nu_ yamalu_n
Alaisal la_hu bika_fin abdah wa yukaw wifu_naka bil lazina min du_nih wa may yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ min ha_d
Wa may yahdil la_hu lama_ lahu_ mim mudil alaisal la_hu biazizin zintiqa_m
Wa la in sa altahum man halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda layaqu_lun nal la_h qul afara aitum ma_ tadu_na min du_nil la_hi in ara_daniyal la_hu bidur rin hal hun na ka_sifa_tu dur rihi au ara_dani birahmatin hal hun na mumsika_turahmatih qul hasbiyal la_h alaihi yatakwak kalul mutawak kilu_n
Qul ya_ qaumimalu_ ala_ maka_natikum in ni a_milun fasaufa talamu_n
May yatihi aza_buy yukhzihi wa wa yahil lu alaihi aza_bun muqim
In na_ anzalna_ alaikal kita_ba lin na_ si bil haq famanih tada_ falinafsih wa man dal la fa in nama_ yadil lu alaiha_ wa ma_ anta alaihin biwakil
Al la_hu yatawaf fal anfusa hina mautiha_ wal lati lam tamut fi mana_miha_ fayumsikul lati qada_ alaihal mauta wa yursilul ukhra_ ila_ ajalin musam ma_ in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy yatafak karu_n
Amit takhazu_ min du_nil la_hi sufa a_ qul awalau ka_nu_ la_ yamiliku_na sai aw wa la_ yaqilu_n
Qul lil la_his safa_ atu jami a_ lahu_ mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ard sum ma ilaihi turja u_n
Wa iza_ zukiral la_hu wahsahus ma az zat qulu_bul lazina la_ yuminu_na bil a_khirah wa iza_ zukiral lazina min du_nihi iza_ hum yastabsiru_n
Qulil la_hum ma fa_tiras sama_wa_ti wal ard a_limal gaibi was saha_dati anta tahkumu baina fiba_dika fima_ ka_nu_ fihi yakhtalifu_n
Wa lau an na lil lazina zalamu_ ma_ fil ardi jamiaw mitslahu_ maahu_ laftadau bihi min su_il aza_bi yaumai qiya_mah wa bada_lahum minal la_hi ma_ lam yaku_nu_ yahtasibu_n
Wa bada_lahum say yi a_tu ma_ kasabu_ wa ha_qa bihim ma_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
Fa iza_ mas sam insa_na dur run daa_na_ sum ma iza_ khaw walna_hu nima_tam min na_ qa_la in nama_ u_tituhu_ ala_ ilm bal hiya fitnatuw wa la_kin na aksarahum la_ yalamu_n
Qad da_lahal lazina min qablihim fama_ agna_ anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
Fa asha_bahum say yi a_tu ma_ kasabu_ wal lazina zalamu_ min ha_ula_ I sayusibihim say yi a_tu ma_ kasabu_ wa ma_ hum bimujizin
Awalam yalamu_ an nal la_ha yabsuthur rijqa limay yasya_ u wa yaqdir in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til liqaumiy yuminu_n
Qul ya_ iba_diyal lazina asrafu_ ala_ anfusihim la_ taqnatu_ mir rahmatil la_h in nal la_h in nal la_ha yagfiruz zunu_ba jamia_ in nahu_ huwal gafu_rur rahim
Wa anibu_ ila_ rab bikum wa aslimu_ lahu_ min qabli ay yatiyakumul aza_bu sum ma la_ tunsaru_n
Wat tabiu_ ahsana ma_ unzila ilaikum mir rab bikum min qabli ay yatiyakumul aza_bu bagtataw wa antum la_ tasuru_n
An taqu_la nafsuy ya_ hasrata_ ala_ ma_ far rathu fi jan bil la_hi wa in kuntu laminas sa_hirin
An taqu_la lau an nal la_ha hada_ni lakuntu la_ minal mut taqin
Au taqu_la hina taral aza_ba lau an na li kar ratan fa aku_na minal muhsinin
Bala_ qad ja_ atka a_ya_ti fakaz zabta biha_ wastakbarta wa kunta minal ka_firin
Wa yaumal qiya_mati taral lazina kazabu_ alal la_hi wuju_huhum mus wad dah alaisa fi jahan nama matswal lil mutakab birin
Wa yunaj jil la_hul lazinat taqau bimafa_zatihim la_ yamas suhumus su_ u wa la_ hum yahzanu_n
Al la_hu kha_liqu kul li sai iw wa huwa ala_ kuli sai iw wakil
Lahu_ maqa_lidus sama_wa_ti wal ard wal lazina kafaru_ bi a_ya_til la_hi ula_ ika humul kha_siru_n
Qul afaghairal la_hi tamuru_n ni abudu ay yuhal ja_hilu_n
Wa laqad u_hiya ilaika wa ilal lazina min qablik la in asrakta layahbatana amaluka wa lataku_nan na minal kha_sirin
Balil la_ha fabud wa kum minas sa_kirin
Wa ma_ qadarul la_ha haq qa qadrihi wal ardu jamian qabdatuhu_ yaumal qiya_mati was sama_wa_tu matwiy ya_tun biyaminih subha_nahu wataa_la_ am ma_ yusriku_n
Wa nufikha fis su_ri fashaiqa man fis sama_wati wa man fil ardi il la_ man sa_ al la_h sum ma nufikha fihi ukhra_ fa iza_ hum qiya_muy yanzhuru_n
Wa asraqatil ardu binu_ri rab biha_ wa wudial kita_bu wa ji a bin nabiyina was suhada_ I wa qudiya bainahum bil haq qi wa hum la_ yuzlamu_n
Wa wuf fiyat kul lu nafsim ma_ amilat wa huwa alamu bima_ yafalu_n
Wa siqal lazina kafaru_ ila_ jahanama zumara_ hat ta_ iza_ ja_ u_ha_ futihat abwa_buha_ wa qa_la lahum khazanatuha_ alam yatikum rusulum minkum yatlu_na alaikum a_ya_ti rab bikum wa yunziru_nakum liqa_ a yaumikum ha_za_qa_lu_ bala_ wa la_kin haq qat kalimatul aza_bi alal ka_firin
Qilad khulu_ azwa_ba jahan nama kha_lidina fiha_ fabisa matswal mutakab birin
Wa siqal lazinat taqau rab bahum ilal jan nati zumara_ hat ta_ iza_ ja_ u_ha_ wa futihat abwa_buha_ wa qa_la lahum khazanatuha_ sala_mun alaikum tibtum fad khulu_ha_ kha_lidin
Wa qa_lul hamdu lil la_hil lazi sadaqana_ wadahu_ wa auratsanal arda natabaw wa u minal jan na_ti haitsu nasya_ u fanima ajrul a_milin
Wa taral mala_ikata ha_f fina min haulil arsi yusab bihu_na bihamdi rab bihim wa qudiya bainahum bil haq qi wa qilal hamdu lil la_hi rab bil a_lamin
Ha_ mim
Tanzilul kita_bi minal la_hil azizil alim
Gha_fariz zan bi wa qa_bilit taubi sadidil iqa_bi zit taul la_ il la_ha il la_ huw wlaihil masir
Ma_ yuja_dilu fi a_ya_til la_hi il lal lazina kafaru_ fala_ yagrurka taqalubuhum fil bila_d
Kaz zabat qablahum qaumu nu_hiw wal ahza_bu min badihim wa hamat kul lu um matin birasu_lihim liyakhuzu_hu wa ja_dalu_ bil ba_tili liyud hidu_ bihil haq qa fa akhaz tuhum fakaifa ka_na iqa_b
Wa kaza_lika haq qat kalimatu rab bika alal lazina kafaru_ an nahum asha_bun na_r
Al lazina yahmilu_nal arsa wa man haulahu_ yusab bihu_na bihamdi rabihim wa yuminu_na bihi wa yastagfiru_na lil lazina a_manu_ rabana_ wa sita kul la sai ir rahmataw wa ilman tagfir lil lazina ta_bu_wat tabau_ sabilaka waqihim aza_bal jahim
Rab bana_ wa adkhilhum jan na_ti adnil lati wa adtahum wa man salaha min a_ba ihim wa azwa_jihim wa zur riy ya_tihim in naka antal azizul hakim
Wa qihimus say yi a_t wa man taqis say yi a_ti yauma izin faqad rahimtah wa za_lika huwal fauzul azhim
In nal lazina kafaru_ yuna_da una lamaqtul la_hi akbaru mim maqtikum anfusakum iz tadauna ilal ima_ni fatakfuru_n
Qa_lu_ rab bana_ amat tanats nataini wa ahyaitanats nataini fatarafna_ bizunu_bina_ fahal ila_ khuru_jim min sabil
Za_likum bi an nahu_ iza_ duiyal lahu wahdahu_ kafartum wa iy yusy rak bihi tuminu_ falhukmu lil la_hil aliy yil kabir
Huwal lazi yurikum a_ya_tihi wa yunaz zilu lakum minas sama_i rizqa_ wa ma_ yatazak karu il la_ may yunib
Fadul la_ha muklisina lahud dina walau karihal ka_firu_n
Rafiud daraja_ti zul arsy yulqiru_ha min amrihi ala_ may yasya_ u min iba_dihi liyunzira yaumat tala_q
Yauma hum ba_rizu_na la yakta_ alal la_hi minhum sai limanil mulkul yaum lil la_hil wa_hidil qah ha_r
Alyauma tujza_ kul lu nafsin bima_ kasabat la_ zulmal yaum in nal la_ha sariul hisa_b
Wa anzirhum yaumal a_zifati izil qulu_bu ladal hana_jiri ka_zimin ma_ liz za_limina min hami miw wa la_ safiiy yuta_
Yalamu kha_ inatal ayuni wa ma_ tukhfis sudu_r
Wal la_hu yaqdi bil haq wal lazina yadu_na min du_nihi la_ yaqdu_na bisai in nal la_ha huwas samiul basir
Awalam yasuru_ fil ardi fayanzuru_ kaifa ka_na qa_qibatul lazina ka_nu_ min qablihim ka_nu_ hum asyad damin hum quw wataw wa a_tsaran fil ardi fa akazahumul la_hu bizunu_bihim wa ma_ ka_na lahum minal la_hi miw wa_q
Za_lika bi an nahum ka_nat tatihim rusuluhum bil bay yina_ti fakafaru_ fa akazahumul la_h in nahu_ qawiy yun sadidul iqa_b
Wa laqad arsalna_ mu_sa_ bi a_ya_tina_ wa sulta_nim mubin
Ila_ firauna wa ha_ma_na wa qa_ru_na taqa_lu_ sa_hirun kaz za_b
Falam ma_ ja_ ahum bil haq qi min indina_ qa_luqtulu_ abna_ al lazina a_manu_ maahu_ wastahyu_ nisa_ ahum wa ma_ kaidul ka_firina il la_ fi dala_l
Wa qa_la firaunu zaru_ni aqtul mu_sa walyadu rab bah in ni akha_fu ay yubad dila dinakum au ay yuzhira fil ardil fasa_d
Wa qa_la mu_sa_ in ni uztu birab bi wa rab bikum min kul li mutakab biril la_ yuminu biyaumil hisa_b
Wa qa_la rajulum muminum min a_li firauna yaktumu ima_nahu_ ataqtulu_na rajulan ay yaqu_la rab biyal la_hu wa qad ja_ akum bil bay yina_ti mir rab bikum wa iy yaku ka_ziban fa'alaihi kazibuh wa iy yaku sa_diquy yushibkum badul lazi yaidukum in nal la_ha la_ yahdi man huwa musrifun kaz za_b
Ya_ qaumi lakumul mulkul yauma za_hirina fil ardi famay yansuruna_ min basil la_hi in ja_ ana_ qa_la firauna ma_ urikum il la_ ma_ ara_ wa ma_ ahdikum il la_ sabilar rasya_d
Wa qa_lal lazi a_mana ya_ qaumi in ni akha_fu alaikum mitsla yaumil ahza_b
Mitsla dabi qaumi nu_hiw waa_diw wa samu_da wal lazina min badihim wa mal la_hu yuridu zulmal liliba_d
Wa ya_ qaumi in ni akha_fu alaikum yaumat tana_d
Yauma tuwal lu_na mudbirina ma_ lakum minal la_hi min asim wa may yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ min ha_d
Wa laqad ja_akum yu_sufu min qablu bil bay yina_ti fama_ ziltum fi sakim mim ma_ ja_ akum bih hat ta_ iza_ halaka qultum lay yab atsal la_hu min badihi rasu_la_ kaza_lika yudil lul la_hu man huwa musrifum murta_b
Al lazina yuja_dilu_na fi a_ya_til la_hi bigairi sulta_nin ata_hum kabura maqtan indal la_hi wa indal lazina a_manu_ kaza_lika yatbaul la_hu ala_ kul li qabli mutakab birin jab ba_r
Wa qa_la firaunu ya_ ha_ma_nubni li sarhal la al li ablugul asba_b
Asba_bas sama_wa_ti fa at talia ila_ ila_hi mu_sa_ wa in ni la azun nuhu_ kaziba_ wa kaza_lika zuy yina li firauna su_ u amalihi wa sud da anis sabil wa ma_ kaidu firauna il la_ fi taba_b
Wa qa_lal lazi a_mana ya_ qaumit tabiu_ni ahdikum sabilar rasya_d
Ya_ qaumi in nama_ ha_zihil haya_tud dun ya_ mata_uw wa in nal a_khirata hiya da_rul qara_r
Man amila say yi atan fala_ yujza_ il la_ mitslaha_ wa man amila sa_lihan min zakarin au unsa_ wa huwa muminun fa ula_ ika yadhulu_nal jan nata yurzaqu_na fiha_ bigairi hisa_b
Wa ya_ qaumi ma_li adu_kum ilan naja_ti wa tadu_nani ilan na_r
Tadu_nani li akfura bil la_hi wa usrika bihi ma_ laisa li bihi ilmuw wa ana_ adu_kum ilal azizil gaf fa_r
La_ jarama an nama_ tadu_nani ilaihi laisa lahu_ dawatun fid dun ya_ wa la_ fil a_khirati wa an na marad dana_ ilal la_hi wa an nal musrifina hum asha_bun na_r
Fasatazkuru_na ma_ aqu_lu lakum wa ufaw widu amri ilal la_h in nal la_ha basirun bil iba_d
Fawaqa_hul la_hu say yi a_ti ma_ makaru_ wa ha_qa bi a_li firauna su_ ul aza_b
An na_ru yuradu_na alaiha_ guduw waw wa asyiy ya_ wa yauma taqu_mus sa_atu adkhilu_ a_la firauna asyad dal aza_b
Wa iz yataha_j ju_na fin na_ri fayaqu_lud duafa_ u lil lazinas takbaru_ in na_ kun na_ lakum tabaan fahal antum mugnu_na an na_ nasibam minan na_r
Qa_lal lazina takbaru_ in na_ kul lun fiha_ in nal la_ha qad hakama bainal iba_d
Wa qa_lal lazina fin na_r likhazanati jahan namadu_ rab bakum yukhaf fif an na_ yaumam minal aza_b
Qa_lu_ awalam taku tatikum rusulukum bil bay yina_t qa_lu bala_ qa_lu_ fadu_ wa ma_ du'a_ ul ka_firina il la_ fi dala_l
Ina_lanansuru rusulana_ wal lazina a_manu_ fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa yauma yaqu_mul asha_d
Yauma la_ yanfauz za_limina maziratuhum wa lahumul lanatu wa lahum su_ ud da_r
Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sal huda_ wa  auratsna_ bani isra_ilal kita_b
Hudaw wa zikra li ulil lalba_b
Fasbir in na wadal la_hi haq quw was tagfir lizan bika wa sab bih bihamdi rab bika bil asiy yi wal ibka_r
In nal lazina yuja_dilu_na fi a_ya_til la_hi bigairi sulta_nin ata_hum in fi sudu_rihim il la_ kibrum ma_ hum bi ba_ligihi fastaiz bil la_h in nahu_ huwas samiul basir
Lakhalqus sama_wa_ti wal ardi akbaru min khalqin na_si wa la_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yalamu_n
Wa ma_ yastawil ama_ wal basiru wal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti wa lal musi qalilam ma_ tatazak karu_n
In nas sa_ata la a_tiyatul la_ raiba fiha_ wala_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yuminu_n
Wa qa_la rab bukumud u_ni astajib lakum in nal lazina yastakbiru_na an iba_dati sayadkhulu_na jahan na ma_ da_khirin
Al la_hul lazi jaala lakumul laila litas kunu_ fihi wan naha_ra mubsira_ in nala la_ha lazu_ fadlin alan na_si wa la_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yaskuru_n
Za_likumul la_hu rab bukum kha_liqukul li sai la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa fa ana_ tufaku_n
Kaza_lika yufakul lazina ka_nu_ bi a_ya_til la_hi yajhadu_n
Al la_hul lazi jaala lakumul arda qara_raw was sama_ abina_ aw wasaw warakum fa ahsana suwarakum wa razaqakum minat tay yiba_t za_likumul la_hu rab bukum fataba_rakal la_hu rab bul a_lamin
Huwal hay yu la_ ila_ha il la_ huwa fadu_hu muklisina lahud din alhamdu lil la_hi rab bil  a_lamin
Qul in ni an abudal lazina tadu_na min du_nil la_hi lam ma_ ja_ aniyal bay yina_tu mir rab bi wa umirtu an uslima li rab bil a_lamin
Huwal lazi khalaqakum min tura_bin sum ma min nutfatin sum ma min alaqatin sum ma yukhrijukum tiflan sum ma litablugu_ asyud dakum sum ma litaku_nu_ suyu_kha_ wa minkum may yutawaf fa_ min qablu wa litablugu_ ajalam musam ma_ wa la al lakum taqilu_n
Huwal lazi yuhyi wa yumitu faiza_ qadha_ amran fa in nama_ yaqu_lu lahu_ kun fayaku_n
Alam tara ilal lazina yuja_dilu_na fi a_ya_til la_h an na_ yusrafu_n
Al lazina kaz zabu_ bi kita_bi wa bima_ arsalna_ bihi rusulana_ fasaufa yalamu_n
Izil agla_lu fi ana_qihim was sala_sil yushabu_n
Fil hamimi sum ma fin na_ri yusjaru_n
Sum ma qila lahum ainama_ kuntum tusriku_n
Min du_nil la_h qa_lu_ dal lau_ ana_ bal lam nakun nadu_ min qablu sai a_ kaza_lika yudil lul la_hul ka_firin
Za_likum bima_ kuntum tafrahu_na fil ardi bigairil haq qi wa bima_ kuntum tamrahu_n
Udkhulu_ abwa_ba jahan nama kha_lidina fiha_ fa bisa matswal mutakabirin
Fasbir in na wadal la_hi haq qun faim ma_ nuriyan naka badal lazi naiduhum au natawaf fayan naka fa ilaina_ yurjau_n
Wa laqad arsalna_ rusula min qablika minhum man qasasna_ alaika wa minhum mal lam naq sus alaika wa ma_ ka_na lirasu_lin ay yatiya bi a_yatin il la_ bi iznil la_hi fa iza_ ja_ a amrul la_hi qudiya bil haq qi wakasira huna_ likal mubtilu_n
Al la_hul lazi ja'ala lakumul ana_ma litarkabu_ minha_ wa minha_ takulu_n
Wa lakum fiha_ mana_fiu wa litablugu_ alaiha_ ha_jatan fi sudu_rikum wa alaiha_ wa alal fulki tuh malu_n
Wa yurikum a_ya_tihi fa ay ya a_ya_til la_hi tunkiru_n
Afalam yasiru_ fil ardi fayanzuru_ kaifa ka_na a_qibatul lazina min qablihim ka_nu_ aksara min hum wa asyad da quw wataw wa a_tsa_ran fil ardi fama_ agna_ anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
Falam ma_ ja_ at hum rusuluhum bil bay yina_ti farihu_ bima_ indahum minal ilmi wa ha_qa_ bihim ma_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
Falam ma_ ra au basana_ qa_lu_ a_man na_ bil la_hi wahdahu_ wa kafarna_ bima_ kun na_ bihi musrikin
Falam yaku yanfauhum ima_nuhum lam ma_ ra au basana_ sun natal la_hil lati qad khalat fi iba_dihi wa khasira huna_likal ka_firu_n
Ha_ mim
Tanzilum minar rahma_nir rahim
Kita_bun fus silat a_ya_tuhu_ qur a_nan arabiy yal liqaumiy yalamu_n
Basiraw wa naziran fa arada aksaruhum fahum la_ yasmau_n
Wa qa_lu_ qulu_buna_ fi akin natim mim ma_ tadu_na_ ilaihi wa fi a_za_nina_ waqruw wa min bainina_ wa bainika hija_bun famal in nana_ a_milu_n
Qul in nama_ ana basarum mitslukum yu_ha_ ilay ya an nama_ ila_hukum ila_huw wa_hidun fastaqimu_ ilaihi was tagfiru_h wa wailul lil musrikin
Al lazina a_ yutu_naz zaka_ta wa hum bil a_khiratihum ka_firu_n
In nal lazina a_manu_ wa amilusa_liha_ti lahum ajrun gairu mamnu_n
Qul ain nakum latakfu_runa bil lazi khalaqal arda fi yaumaini wa tajalu_na lahu_ asda_da_ za_lika rab bul a_lamin
Wa ja'ala fiha_ rawa_siya min fauqiha_ wa ba_raka fiha_ wa qad dara fiha_ aqwa_taha_ fi arbaata ay ya_m sawa_ al lis sa_ ilin
Sum mas tawa_ ilas sama_i wa hiya duka_nun faqa_la laha_ wa lil arditiya_ tauan au karha_ qa_lata_ ataina_ ta_ i in
Faqada_hun na saba sama_wa_ti fi yaumaini wa auha_ fi kul li sama_ in amraha_ wa zay yan nas sama_ ad dun ya_ bi masa_biha wa hifza_ za_lika taqdirul azizil alim
Fa in aradu_ faqul anzartukum sa_iqatam mitsla sa_iqati a_diw wa samu_d
Iz ja_ at humur rusulu min baini aidihim wa min khalfihim al la_ tabudu_ ilal la_h qa_lu_ lau sa_ a rab buna_ la anzala mala_ikatan fa in na_ bima_ ursitum bihi ka_firu_n
Fa am ma_ a_dun fastakbaru_ fil ardi bigairil haq qi wa qa_lu_ ma_ asyadu min na_ quw wah awalam yarau an nal la_hal lazi khalaqahum huwa asyad du minhum quw wah wa ka_nu_ bi a_ya_tina_ yajhadu_n
Fa arsalna_ alaihim rihan sarsaran fi ay ya_min nahisa_til linuziqahum aza_bal khizyi fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa la'aza_bal a_khirati akhza_ wa hum la_ yunsaru_n
Wa am ma_ samu_du fahadaina_hum fastahab bul ama_ alal huda_ fa akhazat hum sa_iqatu aza_bil hu_ ni bima_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
Wanaj jainal lazina a_manu_ waka_nu_ yat taqu_n
Wa yauma yuhsaru ada_ ul la_hi ilan na_ri fahum yu_za u_n
Hat ta_ iza_ ma_ ja_ u_ha_ sahida alaihim samuhum wa absa_ruhum wa julu_duhum bima_ ka_nu_ yamalu_n
Wa qa_lu_ li julu_dihim lima sahidtum alaina_ qa_lu_ antaqanal la_hul lazi antaqa kul la sai iw wa huwa khalaqkum aw wala mar ratiw wa ilaihi turjau_n
Wa ma_ kuntum tastatiru_na ay yashada alaikum samukum wa la_ absa_rukum wa la_ julu_dukum wala_kin zanantum an nal la_ha la_ yalamu katsiram mim ma_ tamalu_n
Wa za_likum zan nukumul lazi zanantum birab bikum arda_kum fasbahtum minal kha_sirin
Fa iy yasbiru_ fan na_ru matswal lahum wa iy yastatibu_ fama_ hum minal mutabin
Wa qay yadna_ lahum qurana_ a fa zaay yanu_ lahum ma_ baina aidihim wa ma_ khalfahum wa haq qa alaihimul qaulu fi umamin qad khalat min qablihim minal jin ni wal insi inahum ka_nu_ kha_sirin
Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ la_ tasmau_ liha_zal qur a_ni wal gau fihi la'al lakum taglibu_n
Falanuziqan nal lazina kafaru_ aza_ban sadidaw wa lanajziyan nahum aswa al lazi ka_nu_ yamalu_n
Za_lika jaza_ u ada_ la_hin na_ru lahum fiha_ sa_rul khuld jaza_ an bima_ ka_nu_ bi a_ya_tina_ yajhadu_n
Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ rab bana_ arinal lazzini adal la_na_ minal jin ni wal insi najalhuma_ tahta aqda_mina_ liyaku_na_ minal azfalin
In nal lazina qa_lu_ rab bunal la_hu sum mas taqa_mu_ tatanaz zalu alaihimul mala_ ikatu al la_ takha_fu_ wa la_ tahzanu_ wa absyiru_ bil jan natil lati kuntum tu_adu_n
Nahnu auliya_ ukum fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa fil a_khirati wa lakum fiha_ ma_ tastahi anfusukum wa lakum fi ha_ ma_ tad dau_n
Nuzulam min gafu_rir rahim
Wa man ahsanu qaulam mim man daa_ ilal la_hi wa amila sa_lihaw wa qa_la in nani minal muslimin
Wa la_ tastawil hasanatu wa las say yi ah idfa bil lati hiya ahsanu fa izal lazi bainaka wa bainahu_ ada_watun ka an nahu_ waliy yun hamim
Wa ma_ yulaq qa_ha_ ilal lazina sabaru_ wa ma_ yulaq qa_ha_ il la_ zu_haz zin azim
Wa im ma_ yanzagan naka minas saita_ni nazgun fastaiz bil la_h in nahu_ huwas saul alim
Wa min a_ya_tihil lailu wan naha_ru was samsu wal qamar la_ tasjudu_ lis samsi wa la_ lilqamari was judu_ lil la_hil lazi khalaqahun na in kuntum iy ya_hu tabudu_n
Fa inis takbaru_ fal lazina inda rab bika yusab bihu_na lahu_ bil laili wan naha_ri wa hum la_ yas amu_n
Wa min a_ya_tihi an naka taral arda kha_siatan fa iza_ anzalna_ alaihal ma_ ajtaz zat wa rabat in nal lazi ahya_ha_  lamuhyil mauta_ in nahu_ ala_ kul li sai in qadir
In nal lazina yulhidu_na fi a_ya_tina_ la_ yakhfauna alaina_ afmay yulqa_ fin na_ri khairun am may yati a_minay yaumal qiya_mah imalu_ ma_ situm inahu_ bima_ tamalu_na basir
In nal lazina kafaru_ biz zikri lama_ ja_ ahum wa in nahu_ lakita_bun aziz
La_ yatihil ba_tilu mim baini yasaihi wa la_ min khalif tanzilum min hakimin hamid
Ma_ yuqa_lu laka il la_ ma_ qad qila lir rusuli min qablik in na rab baka lazu_ magfiratiw wa zu_ iqa_bin alim
Wa lau jaalna_hu qur a_nan ajamiy yal laqa_lu_ lau la_ fus silat a_ya_tuh a ajamiy a_manu_ hudaw wa sifa_ wal lazina la_ yuminu_na fi a_za_nihim waqruw wa huwa alaihim ama_ ula_ ika yuna_dauna mim maka_nin baid
Wa laqad a_taina_ mu_sal kita_ba fakhtulifa fih wa lau la_ kalimatun sabaqat mir rab bika laqudiya bainahum wa in nahum lafi sak sim minhu murib
Man amila sa_lihan falinafsihi wa man asa_ a fa'alaiha_ wa ma_ rab buka bi zal la_mil lil abid
Ilaihi yurad du ilmus sa_ah wa ma_ takhruju min samara_tin min akma_miha wa ma_ tahmilu min unsa_ wa la_ tadau il la_ bi ilmih wa yauma yuna_dihim aina suraka_ I qa_lu_ a_zan na_ka ma_ min na_ min sahid
Wa dal la anhum ma_ ka_nu_ yad u_na min qablu wa zan nu_ ma_ lahum mim mahis
La_ yas amul insa_nu min dua_il khair wa im mas sahus sar ru fayau_sun qanu_th
Wa la in adzaqna_hu rahmatam min na_ mim badi dar ra_ a mas sat hu layaqu_lan na ha_za_ li wa ma_ azhun nus sa_ ata qa_ imataw wa la ir rujitu ila_ rab bi in na li indahu_ lalhusna fa lanunab bi an nal lazina kafaru_ bima_ amilu_ wa lanuziqan nahum min aza_bin galiz
Wa iza_ anamna_ alal insa_ni arada wa na a_ bija_nibih wa iza_ mas sahus sar ru fazu_ dua_in arid
Qul ara aitum in ka_na min indil la_hi sum ma kafartum bihi man adhal lu mim man huwa fi siqa_qin baid
Sanurihim a_ya_tina_ fil a_fa_qi wa fi anfusihim hat ta_ yatabay yana lahum an nahul haq awalam yakfi birab bika an nahu_ ala_ kul li sai in sahid
Ala_ in nahum fi miryatim mil liqa_i rab bihim ala_ in nahu_ bikuli sai im muhit
Ha_ mim
Ain Sin Qa_f
Kaza_lika yu_hi ilaika wa ilal lazina min qablikal la_hul azizul hakim
Lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard wa huwal aliy yul azim
Taka_dus sama_wa_ti yatafat tarnamin faiqihin na wal mala_ikatu yusab bihu_na bihamdi rab bihim wa yastagfiru_na liman fil ard ala_ inal la_ha huwal gafu_rur rahim
Wal lazinat takazu_ min du_nihi auliya_ al la_hu hafizun alaihim wa ma_ anta alaihim biwakil
Wa kaza_lika auhaina_ ilaika qur a_nan arabiy yal lituzira um mal qu ra_ wa man haulaha_ wa tunzira yaumal jami la_ raiba fih fariqun fil jan nati wa fariqun fis sair
Wa lau sa_ al la_hu lajaalahum umataw wa_hidataw wa la_kiy yudkhilu may yasya_u fi rahmatih waz za_limu_na ma_ lahum miw waliy yiw wa la_ nasir
Amit takazu_ min du_nihi auliya_ fal la_hu huwal waliy yu wa huwa yuhyil mauta_ wa huwa ala_ kul li sai in qadir
Wa mak talaftum fihi min sai in fahukmuhu_ ilal la_h za_likumul la_hu rab bi alaihi tawak kaltu wa ilaihi unib
Fa_tirus sama_wa_ti wal ard jaala lakum min anfusikum azwa_jaw wa minal ana_mi aswa_ja_ yazra ukum fih laisa kamitlihi sai uw wa huwas samiul basir
Lahu_ maqa_lidus sama_wa_ti wal ard yabsutur rizqa limay yasya_u wa yaqdir in nahu_ bikul li sai in alim
Sara'a lakum minad dini ma_ wasa_ bihi nu_haw wal lazi auhaina_ ilaika wa ma_ was saina_ bihi ibra_hima wa mu_sa_ wa isa_ an aqimud dina wa la_ tatafar raqu_ fih kabura alal musrikina ma tadu_hum ilaih al la_hu yajtabi ilaihi may yasya_u wa yahdi ilaihi may yunib
Wa ma_ tafar raqu_ il la_ min badi ma_ ja_ ahumul ilmu bagyan bainahum wa lau la_ kalimatun sabaqat mir rab bika ila_ ajalim musam mal faqudiya bainahum wa in nal lazina u_ritsul kita_ba min badihim lati sakim imnu murib
Fa liza_lika fadu wastaqim kama_ umirta wa la_ tat tabi ahwa_ ahum wa qul a_mantu bima_ anzalal la_hu min kita_b wa umirtu li adila bainakum al la_hu rab buna_ wa rab bukum lana_ ama_luna_ wa lakum ama_lukum la_ huj jata bainana_ wa bainakum al la_hu yajmau bainana_ wa ilaihil masir
Wal lazina yuha_j ju_na fil la_hi mim badi mastujiba lahu_ huj jatuhum da_hidatun inda rab bihim wa alaihim gadabuw wa lahum aza_bun sadid
Al la_hul lazi anzalal kita_ba bil haqi wal miza_n wa ma_ yudrika la'alas sa_ata qarib
Yastajilu bihal lazina la_ yuminu_na biha_ wal lazina a_manu_ musfiqu_na minha_ wa yalamu_na an nahal haq ala_ in nal lazina yuma_ru_na fis sa_ati lafi sala_lin baid
Al la_hu latifun biiba_dihi yarzuqu may yasya_ wa huwal qawiy yul aziz
Man ka_na yuridu hartsal a_khirati nazid lahu_ fi hartsihi wa man ka_na yuridu harsad dun ya_ nutihi minha_ wa ma_ lahu_ fil a_khirati min nasib
Am lahum suraka_ u sarau_ lahum minad dini ma_ lam yazan bihil la_hu wa lau la_ kalimatul fasli la qudiya bainahum wa in naz za_limina lahum aza_bun alim
Taraz za_limina musfiqina mim ma_ kasabu_ wa huwa wa_qiun bihim wal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_lihati fi rauda_til jan na_t lahum ma_ yasya_ u_na inda rab bihim za_lika huwal fadul kabir
Za_likal lazi yubas sirul la_hu iba_dahul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_t qul la_ as alukum alihi ajran il lal mawad data fil qurba_ wa may yaqtarif hasanatan nazid lahu_ fiha_ hus na_ in nal la_ha gafu_run saku_r
Am yaqu_lu_naf tara_ alal lahi kazina_ fa iy yasya il la_hu yaktim ala_ qalbik wa yamhul la_hul ba_tila wa yuhiq qul haq qa bikalima_tih in nahu_ alimu_n biza_tis sudu_r
Wa huwal lazi yaqbalut taubata an iba_dihi wa yafu_ anis say yi a_ti wa yalamu ma_ tafalu_n
Wa yastajibul lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti wa yaziduhum min fadlih wal ka_firu_na lahum aza_bun sadid
Walau basatal la_hur razqa liiba_dihi labagau fil ardi wa la_kiy yunaz zilu biqadarim ma_ yasya_ in nahu_ bi iba_dihi kabirun basir
Wa huwal lazi yunaz zilul gaitsa mim badi ma_ qanathu_ wa yansyuru rahmatah wa huwal waliy yul hamid
Wa min a_ya_tihi halqus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bat sa fihima_ min da_b bah wa huwa ala_ jamihim iza_ yasya_ u qadir
Wa ma_ asha_bakum mim musibatin fa bima_ kasabat aidikum wa yafu_ an katsi
Wa ma_ antum bimujizina fil ardi wa ma_ lakum min du_nil la_hi miw waliy yiw wa la_ nasir
Wamin a_ya_tihil jawa_ri fil bahri kal ala_m
Iy yasya yuskinir riha fayazalna rawa_kida ala_ zahrir in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til likul li sab ba_rin saku_r
Au yu_bigun na bima_ kasabu_ wa yafu an katsir
Wa yalamal lazina yuja_dilu_na fi a_ya_tina_ ma_ lahum mim mahis
Fama_ u_titum min sai in famata_ul haya_tid dun ya_ wa ma_ indal la_hi khairuw wa abqa_ lil lazina a_manu_ wa ala_ rab bihim yatawak kalu_n
Wal lazina yajtanibu_na kaba_ iral ismi wal fawa_hisya wa iza_ ma_ gadibu_hum yagfiru_n
Wal lazinas taja_bu_ lirab bihim wa aqa_mus sala_h wa amruhum su_ra_ bainahum wa mim ma_ razaqna_hum yunfiqu_n
Wal lazina iza_ asha_bahumul bagyu hum yantasiru_n
Wa jaza_u say yi atin say yi atum mitsluha_ faman afa_ wa aslaha fa ajruhu_ alal la_h in nahu_ la_ yuhib buz za_limin
Wa lamanin tasara bada zulmihi fa ula_ ika ma_ alaihim min sabil
In namas sabilu alal lazina yazlimu_nan na_sa wa yabgu_na fil ardi bigairil haq ula_ ika lahum aza_bun alim
Wa laman sabara wa gafara in na za_lika lamin azmil umu_r
Wa may yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ miw waliy yim min badih wa taraz za_limina lam ma_ ra awul aza_ba yaqu_lu_na hal ila_ marad dim min sabil
Wa tara_hum yuradu_na alaiha_ ha_siina minaz zul li yanzuru_na min tarfin hafiy wa qa_lal lazina a_manu_ in nal ka_sirinal lazina kasiru_ anfusahum wa ahlihim yaumal qiya_mah ala_ in naz za_limina fi aza_bim muqim
Wa ma_ ka_na lahum min auliya_ a yansuru_nahum min du_nil la_h wa may yudlilil la_hu fama_ lahu_ min sabil
Istajibu_ lirab bikum min qabli ay yatiya yaumul la_ marad da lahu_ minal la_h ma_ lakum mim malja iy yauma iziw wa ma_ lakum min nakir
Fa in aradu_ fama_ arsalna_ka alaihim hafizan in alaika il lal bala_g wa in na_ iza_ adzaqnal insa_na min na_ rahmatan fariha biha_ wa in tusibum say yi atun bima_ qad damat aidihim fa in nal insa_na kafu_r
Lil la_hi mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ard yakluqu ma_ yasya u yahabu limay yasya_u ina_tsaw wa yahabu limay yasya_ uz zuku_r
Au yuzaw wijuhum zukra_naw wa ina_sa_ wa yajalu may yasya_ u aqima in nahu_ alimun qadir
Wa ma_ ka_na libasarin ay yukal limahul la_hu wahyan au miw wara_i hija_bin au yursila rasu_lan fayu_hiya bi iznihi ma_ yasya_ inahu_ aliy yun hakim
Wa kaza_lika auhaina_ ilaika ru_ham min amrina_ ma_ kunta tadri mal kita_bu wa lal ima_nu wa la_kin jaalna_hu nu_ran nahdi bihi man nasa_u min iba_dina_ wa in naka_ la tahdil ila_ sira_tim mustaqim
Sira_til la_hil lazi lahu_ ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ard ala_ ilal la_hi tasirul umu_r
Ha_ mim
Wal kita_bil mubin
In na_ ja'alna_hu qur a_nan arabiy yal la al lakum taqilu_n
Wa in nahu_ fi um mil kita_bi ladaina_ la'aliy yun hakim
Afanadribu ankumuz zikra safhan an kuntum qaumam musrifin
Wa kam arsalna_ min nabiy yin fil aw walin
Wa ma_ yatihim min nabiy yin il la_ ka_nu_ bihi yastahzi u_n
Fa ahlakna_ asyad da minhum batsaw wa mada_ matsalul aw walin
Wa la in sa altahum man halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda layaqu_lun na halaqahun nal azizul alim
Al lazi ja'ala lakumul arda mahdaw wa jaala lakum fiha_ subulal la al lakum tahtadu_n
Wal lazi naz zala minas sama_i ma_ an biqadar fa ansarna_ bihi baldatam maita_ kaza_lika tukraju_n
Wal lazi halaqal azwa_ja kul laha_ wa ja ala lakum minal fulki wal an a_mi ma_ tarkabu_n
Litastawu_ ala_ zuhu_rihi sum ma tazkuru_ nimata rab bikum izas tawaitum alaihi wa taqu_lu_ subna_nal lazi sak kara lana_ ha_za_ wa man kun na_ lahu_ muqrinin
Wa in na_ ila_ rab bina_ lamunqalibu_n
Wa ja'alu_ lahu_ min iba_dihi juz a_ in nal insana_ lakafu_rum mubin
Amit takaza mim ma_ yakluqu bana_tiw wa asfa_kum bil banin
Wa iza bus sira ahaduhum bima_ daraba lir rahma_ni matsalan zal la wajuhu_ muswad daw wa huwa kazim
Awa may yunas sa u fil hilyati wa huwa fil hisa_mi gairu mubin
Wa ja'alul mala_ ikatal lazina hum iba_dur rahma_ni ina_tsa_ asyahidu_ halqahum satuktabu saha_datuhum wa yus alu_n
Wa qa_lu_ lau sa_ ar rahma_nu ma_ abadna_hum ma_ lahum biza_lika min ilmin in hum il la_ yakrusu_n
Am a_taina_hum kita_bam min qablihi fahum bihi mustamsiku_n
Bal qa_lu_ in na_ wajadna_ a_ba_ ana_ ala_ um matiw wa in na_ ala_ a_tsa_rihim muhtadu_n
Wa kaza_lika ma_ arsalna_ min qablika fi qaryatim min nazirin il la_ qa_la mutrafu_ha_ in na_ wa jadna_ a_ba_ ana_ ala_ um matiw wa in na_ ala_ a_tsa_rihim muqtadu_n
Qa_la awalau jitukum bi ahda_ mim ma_ wajatum alihi a_ba_ akum qa_lu_ in na_ bima_ ursiltum bihi ka_firu_n
Fantaqamna_ minhum fanzur kaifa ka_na a_qibatul mukaz zibin
Wa iz qa_la ibra_himu li abihi wa qaumihi in nani bara_ um mim ma_ tabudu_n
Il lal lazi fatarani fa in nahu_ sayahdin
Wa jaalaha_ kalimatan ba_qiyatan fi aqibihi la al lahum yarjiu_n
Bal mat tatu ha_ ula_i wa a_ba_ ahum hat ta_ ja_ ahumul haq qu wa rasu_lum mibin
Wa lam ma_ ja_ ahumul haq qu qa_lu_ ha_za_ sihruw wa in na_ bihi ka_firu_n
Wa qa_lu_ lau la_ nuz zila ha_zal qur a_nu ala_ rajulim minal qaryataini azim
Ahum yaqsimu_na rahmata rab bika nahnu qasamna_ bainahum maisyatahum fil haya_tid dun ya_ wa rafana_ badahum fauqa badin daraja_til liyat takhiza baduhum badan sukriy ya_ wa rahmatu rab bika khairum mim ma_ yajmau_n
Wa lau la_ ay yaku_nan na_su umataw wa_hidatal laja'alna_ limay yakfuru bir rahma_ni libuyu_tihim suqufam min fid datiw wa maa_rija alaiha_ yazharu_n
Wa libuyu_tihim abwa_baw wa sururan alaiha_ yat taki u_n
Wa zukrufa_ wa in kul lu za_lika lam ma_ mata_ul haya_tid dun ya_ wal a_khiratu inda rab bika lilmut taqin
Wa may yasu an zikrir rahma_ni nuqay yid lahu_ saita_nan fahuwa lahu_ qarin
Wa in nahum layasud du_nahum anis sabili wa yahsabu_na an nahum muhtadu_n
Hat ta_ iza_ ja_ ana_ qa_la ya_laita baini wa bainaka budal masriqaini fabisal qarin
Wa lay yanfakumul yauma iz zalamtum an nakum fil aza_bi mustariku_n
Afa anta tusmius sum ma au tahdil umya wa man ka_na fi dala_lim mubin
Fa im ma_ nazaban na bika fa in na_ minhum muntaqimu_n
Au nuriyan nakal lazi wa adna_hum fa in na_ alaihim muqtadiru_n
Fastamsik bil lazi u_hiya ilaik in naka ala_ sira_tim mustaqim
Wa in nahu_ lazikrul laka wa laqaumika wa saufa tus alu_n
Was al man arsalna_ min qablika mir rusulina_ aja'alna min du_nir rahma_ni a_lihatay yubadu_n
Wa laqad arsalna_ mu_sa_ bi a_ya_tina_ ila_ firauna wamala_ ihi faqa_lain ni rasu_lu rab bil a_lamin
Falam ma_ ja_ ahum bi a_ya_tina_ iza_ hum minha_ yadhaku_n
Wa ma_ nurihim min a_yatin il la_ hiya akbaru min ukhtiha_ wa akhaz na_hum bil aza_bi la'al lahum yarjiu_n
Wa qa_lu_ ya_ ay yuhas sa_hirudu lana_ rab baka bima_ ahida indak in nana_ lamuhtadu_n
Falam ma_ kasyafna_ anhumul aza_ba iza_ hum yankutsu_n
Wa na_da_ firaunu fi qaumihi qa_la ya_ qaumi alaisa li mulku misra wa ha_zihil anha_ru tajri min tahti afala_ tubsiru_n
Am ana_khairum min ha_zal lazi huwa mahinuw wa la_ yaka_du yubin
Falau la_ ulqiya alaihi aswiratum min zahabin au ja_ a ma'ahul mala_ikatu muqtarinin
Fastakhaf fa qaumahu_ fa ata_u_h in nahum ka_nu_ qauman fa_siqin
Falam ma_ a_safu_nan taqamna_ minhum fa agraqna_hum ajmain
Faja'alna_hum salafaw wa matsalal lil a_khirina
Wa lam ma_ duribabnu maryama matsalan iza_ qaumuka minhu yasidu_n
Wa qa_lu_ a a_lihatuna_ khairun am hu ma_ darabu_hu laka il la_ jadala_ bal hum qaumun khasimu_n
In huwa il la_ abdun an amna_ alaihi wa jaalna_hu matsalal libani isra_il
Wa lau nasya_u lajaalna_ minkum mala_ikatan fil ardi yakhlufu_n
Wa in nahu_ la ilmul lis sa_ati fala_ tamtarun na biha wat tabiu_n ha_za_ sira_tum mustaqim
Wa la_ yasud dan nakumus saita_n in nahu_ lakum aduw wum mubin
Wa lam ma_ ja_ aisa_ bil bay yina_ti qa_la qad jitukum bilhikmati wa li ubay yina lakum badal lazi taktalifu_na fih fat taqul la_ha wa atiu_n
In nal la_ha huwa rab bi wa rab bukum fabudu_h ha_za_ sira_tum mustaqim
Faktalafal ahza_bu min bainihim fa wailul lil lazina zalamu_ min aza_bi yaumin alim
Hal yansuru_na il las sa_ata an tatiyahum bagtataw wa hum la_ yasuru_n
Al akhil la_ u yauma izim baduhum libadin aduw wun il lal mutaqin
Ya_ iba_di la_ kaufun alikumul yauma wa la_ antum tahzanu_n
Al lazina a_manu_ bi a_ya_tina_ wa ka_nu_ muslimin
Udkhulul jan nata antum wa azwa_jukum tuhbaru_n
Yutha_fu alaihim bisiha_fim min zahabiw wa akwa_b wa fiha_ ma_ tastahihil anfusu wa talaz zul ayun wa antum fiha_ kha_lidu_n
Wa tikal jan natul lati u_ritsumu_ha_ bima_ kuntum tamalu_n
Lakum fiha_ fa_kihatun katsiratum minha_ takulu_n
In nal mujrimina fi aza_bi jahanama kha_lidu_n
La_ yufat taru anhum wa hum fihi mublisu_n
Wa ma_ zalamna_hum wa la_kin ka_nu_ humuz za_limin
Wa na_dau ya_ ma_liku liyaqdi alaina_ rab buk qa_la in nakum ma_kitsu_n
Laqad jina_kum bil haq qi wa la_kina aksarakum lilhaq qi ka_rihu_n
Am abramu_ amran fa in na_ mubrimu_n
Am yahsabu_na an na_ la_ nasmau sir rahum wa najwa_hum bala_ wa rusuluna_ ladaihim yaktubu_n
Qul in ka_na lir rahma_ni waladun fa ana aw walul a_bidin
Subha_na rab bis sama_wa_ti wal ardi rab bil arsi am ma_ yasifun
Fazarhum yakhu_du_ wa yal abu_ hat ta_ yula_qu_ yauma humul lazi yu_adu_n
Wa huwal lazi fis sama_i ila_huw wa fil ardi ila_h wa huwal hakimul alim
Wa taba_rakal lazi lahu_ mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ wa indahu_ ilmus sa_ah wa ilaihi turjau_n

Wa qilihi ya_ rab bi in na ha_ ula_ I qaumul la_ yuminu_n
Fasfah anhum wa qul sala_mun fa saufa yalamu_n
Ha_ mim
Wal kita_bil mubin
In na_ anzalna_hu fi lailatim muba_ rakatin in na_ kun na_ munzirin
Fiha_ yufraqu kul lu amrin hakim
Amram min indina_ in na_ kun na_ mursilin
Rahmatam mir rab bik in nahu_ huwas samiul alim
Rab bis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ma_ bainahuma_ in kuntum mu_qinin
La_ ila_ha il la_ huwa yuhyil wa yumit rab bukum wa rab bu a_ba_i kumul aw walin
Bal hum fi sak kiy yalabu_n
Fartaqib yauma tatis sama_u bidu kha_nim mubin
Yagsan na_s ha_za_ aza_bun alim
Rab banaksif an nal aza_ba in na_ muminu_n
An na_ lahumuz zakra_ wa qad ja_ ahum rasu_lum mubin
Sum ma tawal lau anhu wa qa_lu_ mual lamum majnu_n
In na_ ka_siful aza_bi qalilan in nakum a_ idu_n
Yauma nabtisul batsatal kubra_ in na_ muntaqimu_n
Wa laqad fatan na_ qablahum qauma firauna wa ja_ ahum rasu_lun karim
An ad du_ ilay ya iba_dal la_h in ni lakum rasu_lun amin
Wa al la_ talu_ alal la_h in ni a_tikum bisul ta_nim mubin
Wa in ni uztu birab bi wa rab bikum an tarjumu_n
Wa il lam tuminu_ lil fatazilu_n
Fadaa_ rab bahu_ an na ha_ ula_ I qaumum mujrimu_n
Fa asri biiba_dil lailan in nakum mut tabau_n
Watrukil bahra rahwa_ in nahum jundum mugraqu_n
Kam taraku_ min jan na_tiw wa uyu_n
Wa zuru_iw wa maqa_min karim
Wa namatin ka_nu_ fiha_ fa_kihin

Wa laqadih tarna_hum ala_ ilmin alal a_lamin

In hiya il la_ mautatunal u_la_ wa ma_ nahnu bimunsarin
Fatu_ bi a_ba_ ina_ in kuntum sa_diqin
Ahum khairun am qaumu tub baiw wal lazina min qablihim ahlakna_hum in nahum ka_nu_ mujrimin
Wa ma_ khalaqnas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ la_ibin
Ma_ khalaqna_huma_ il la_ bilhaq qi wa la_kin na_ aksarahum la_ yalamu_n
In na yaumal fasli miqa_tuhum ajmain

In na_ syajarataz zaq qu_m
Taa_mul atsim
Kal muhli yagi fi butu_n

Sum ma sub bu_ fauqa rasihi min aza_bil hamim

In nal mut taqina fi maqa_min amin
Fi jan na_tiw wa uyu_n
Yalbasu_na min sundusiw wa istabraqim mutaqa_bilin
Kaza_lika wa zaw wajna_hum bihu_rin in
Yadu_na fiha_ bikul li fa_kihatin a_minin
La_ yazu_qu_na fihal mauta il lal mautatal u_la_ wa waqa_hum aza_bal jahim
Fadlam mir rab bik za_lika huwal fauzul azim
Fa in nama_ yas sarna_hu bilisa_nika la'al lahum yatazak karu_n
Fai taqib in nahum murtaqibu_n
Ha_ mim
Tan zilul kita_bi minal la_hil azizil hakim
In na fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi la a_ya_til lilmuminin
Wa fi khalqikum wa ma_ yabuts sumin da_b batin a_ya_tul liqaumiy yu_qinu_n
Wakhtila_fil laili wan naha_ri wa ma_ anzalal la_hu minas sama_i mir rizqin fa ahya_ bihil arda bada mautiha_ wa tasrifir riya_hi a_ya_tul liqaumiy yaqilu_n
Tilka a_ya_tul la_hi natlu_ha_ alaika bil haq qi fabi ay yi hadisim badal la_hi wa a_ya_tihi yuminu_n
Wailul likul li af fa_kin asim
Yasmau a_ya_til la_hi tutla_ alaihi sum ma yusir ru mustakbiran ka al lam yasmaha_ fabas sirhu biaza_bin alim
Wa iza_ alima min a_ya_tina_ saianit takazaha_ huzuwa_ ula_ ika lahum aza_bum muhin
Miw wara_ ihim jahan nam wa la_ yugni anhum ma_ kasabu_ sai aw wa la_ mat takazu_ min du_nil la_hi auliya_ wa lahum aza_bun azim
Ha_za_ huda_ wal lazina kafaru_ bi a_ya_ti rab bihim lahum aza_bum mir rijzin alim
Al la_hul lazi sak kara lakumul bahra litajriyal fulku fihi bi amrihi wa litabtagu_ min fadlihi wa la al lakum taskuru_n
Wa sak kara lakum ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi jamiam min in na fi za_lika la a_ya_til liaqumiy yatafak karu_n
Qul lil lazina a_manu_ yagfiru lil lazina la_ yarju_na ay ya_mal la_hi liyajziya qaumam bima_ ka_nu_ yaksibu_n
Man amila sa_lihan falinafsih wa man asa_ a fa'alaiha_ sum ma ila_ rab bikum turjau_n
Wa laqad a_taina_ bani isra_ ilal kita_ba wal hukma wan nubuw wata wa razaqna_hum minat tay yiba_ti wa fad dalna_hum alal a_lamin
Wa a_taina_hum bay yina_tim minal amr famaktalafu_ il la_ mim badi ma_ ja_ a humul ilmu bagyan bainahum in na rab baka yaqdi bainahum yaumal qiya_mati fima_ ka_nu_ fihi yakhtalifu_n
Sum ma jaalna_ka ala_ sari atim minal amri fat tabiha_ wa la_ tat tabiahwa_ al lazina la_ yalamu_n
In nahum lay yugnu_ anka minal la_hi sai a_ wa in naz za_limina baduhum auliya_ u badiw wal la_hu waliy yul mut taqin
Ha_za_ basa_ iru lin na_si wa hudaw wa rahmatul liqaumiy yu_qinu_n
Am hasibal lazinaj tarahus say yi a_ti an naj alahum kal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti sawa_ am mahya_hum wa mama_tuhum sa_ a ma_ yahkumu_n
Wa khalaqal la_hus sama_wa_ti wal arda bil haq qi wa litujza_ kul lu nafsin bima_ kasabat wa hum la_ yuzlamu_n
Afara aita manit takaza ila_hahu_ hawa_hu wa adal lahul la_hu ala_ ilmiw wa khatama ala_ samiihi wa qalbihi wa ja'ala ala_ basarihi gisa_wah famay yahdihi min nadil la_h afala_ tazak karu_n
Wa qa_lu_ ma_ hiya il la_ haya_tunad dun ya_ namu_tu wa nahya_ wa ma_ yuhlikuna_ il lad dah wa ma_ lahum biza_lika min ilmin in hum il la_ yahzun nu_n
Wa iza_ tutla_ alaihim a_ya_tuna_ bay yina_tim ma_ ka_na huj jatahum il la_ an qa_lu tu_ bi a_ba_ ina_ in kuntum sa_diqin
Qulil la_hu yuhyikum sum ma yumitukum sum ma yajmaukum ila_ yaumil qiya_matil la_ raiba fihi wa la_kin na aksaran na_si la_ yalamu_n
Wa lil la_hi mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ard wa yauma taqu_mus sa_atu yaumaiziy yakhsarul mubtilu_n
Wa tara_ kul la um matin ja_tsiyah kul lu um matin tud da_ ila_ kita_biha_ alyauma tujzauna ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
Ha_za_ kita_buna_ yantiqu alaikum bil haq in na_ kun na_ nastansiku ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
Fa am mal lazina a_manu_ wa amilus sa_liha_ti fayudkiluhum rab buhum fi rahmatih za_lika huwal fauzul mubin
Wa am mal lazina kafaru_ afalam takun a_ya_ti tutla_ alaikum fastak bartum wa kuntum qaumam mujrimin
Wa iza_ qila in na wadal la_hi haquw was sa_atu la_ raiba fiha_ qultum ma_ nadri mas sa_atu in nazun nu il la_ zan naw wa ma_ nahnu bimustaiqinin
Wa bada_ lahum say yi a_tu ma_ amilu_ wa ha_qa bihim ma_ ka_nu bihi yastahzi u_n
Wa qilal yauma nansa_kum kama_ nasitum liqa_ a yaumikun ha_za_ wa mawa_kumun na_ru wa ma_ lakum min na_sirin

Wa lahul kibriya_ u fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wahuwal azizul hakim
Ha_ mim
Tanzilul kita_bi minal la_hil azizil hakim
Ma_ halaqnas sama_wa_ti wal arda wa ma_ bainahuma_ il la_ bil haq qi wa ajalim musam ma_ wal lazina kafaru_ am ma_ unziru_ muridu_n
Qul ara aitum ma_ tadu_na min du_nil la_hi aru_ni ma_za_ halaqu_ minal ardi am lahum sirkun fis sama_wa_ti lu_ni bikita_bim min qabli ha_za_ au atsa_ratim min ilmin in kuntum sa_diqin
Wa man adhal lu mim may yadu_ min du_nil la_hi mal la_ yastajibu lahu_ ila_ yaumil qiya_mati wa hum an du a_ ihim ga_filu_n
Wa iza_ husyiran na_su ka_nu_ lahum ada_ aw wa ka_nu_ biiba_datihim ka_firin
Wa iza_ tutla_ alaihim a_ya_tuna_ bay yina_tin qa_lal lazina kafaru_ lilhaq qi lam ma_ ja_ ahum ha_za_ sihrum mubin
Am yaqu_lu_naf tara_h qul inif taraituhu_ fala_ tamiku_na li minal la_hi sai a_ huwa alamu bima_ tufidu_na fih kafa_ bihi sahidan bainu wa bainakum wa huwal gafu_rur rahim
Qul ma_ kuntu bidam minar rusuli wa ma_ adri ma_ yufalu bi wa la_ bikum in at tabiu il la_ ma_ yu_ha_ ilay ya wa ma_ ana il la_ nazirum mubin
Qul ara aitum in ka_na min indil la_hi wa kafartum bihi wa sahida sa_hidum min bani isra_ila ala_ mitslihi fa a_mana wastakbartum in nal la_ha la_yahdil qaumaz za_linin
Wa qa_lal lazina kafaru_ lil lazina a_manu_ lau ka_na kairam ma_ sabaqu_na ilaih wa iz lam yahtadu_ bihi fayaqu_lu_na ha_za_ ifkun qadim
Wa min qablihi kita_bu mu_sa_ ima_maw wa rahmah wa ha_za_ kita_bum mushad diqul lisa_nan arabiy yal liyunziral lazina zalamu_ wa busra_ lilmuhsinin
In nal lazina qa_lu_ rab bunal la_hu sum mas taqa_mu_ fala_ kaufun alaihim wa la_ hum yahzanu_n
Ula_ika asha_bul jan nati ha_lidina fiha_ jaza_an bima_ ka_nu_ yamalu_n
Wa was sainal insa_na biwa_lidaihi ihsa_na_ hamalat hu um muhu_ kurhaw wa wadaathu kurha_ wa hamluhu_ wa fisa_luhu sala_su_na sahra_ hat ta_ iza_ balaga asyudahu_ wa balaga arbaina sanatan qa_la rab bi auzini an askura nimatakal lati anamta alay ya wa ala_ wa_liday ya wa an amala sa_lihan tarda_hu wa aslih li fi zur riy yati in ni tubtu ilaika wa in ni minal muslimin
Ula_ ikal lazina nataqab balu anhum ahsana ma_ amilu_ wa nataja_wazu an say yi a_tihim fi asha_bil jan nah wadas sidqil lazi ka_nu_ yu_adu_n
Wal lazi qa_la liwa_lidaihi uf fil lakuma_ ataida_nini an uhraja wa qad halatil quru_nu min qabli wa huma_ yastagnitsa_nil la_ha wailaka a_min in na wadal la_hi haq qun fayaqu_lu ma_ ha_za_ il la_ asa_tirul aw walin

Al lazina kafaru_ wa sad du_ an sabilil la_hi adhal la ama_lahum

In na ha_za_ lahuwa haq qul yaqin
Fasab bih bismi rab bikal azim
Sab baha lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa huwal azizul hakim

Huwal aw walu wal a_khiru waz za_hiru wal ba_tinu wa huwa bikul li sai in alim
Huwal lazi halaqas sama_wa_ti wal arda fi sit tati aya ya_min sum mas tawa_ alal arsy yalamu ma_ yaliju fil ardhi wa ma_ yakhruju minha_ wa ma_ yanzilu minas sama_i wa ma_ yaruju fiha_ wa huwa ma'akum aina ma_ kuntum wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na basir
Lahu_ mulkus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa ilal la_hi turjaul umu_r
Yu_lijul laila fin naha_ri wa yu_lijun naha_ra fil lail wa huwa alimun biza_tis sudu_r

Wa ma_ lakum la_ tuminu_na bil la_hi war rasu_lu yadu_kum lituminu_ birab bikum wa qad akhaza misa_qakum in kuntum muminin

Ya ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ hal adul lukum ala_ tija_ratin tunjikum min aza_bin alim

Yagfir lakum zunu_bakum wa yudkilkum jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru wa masa_kina tay yibatan fi jan na_ti and, za_likal fauzul azim
Wa ukhra_ tuhib bu_naha_ nasrum minal la_hi wa fat hun qarib wa basiril muminin
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ ku_nu_ ansha_ral la_hi kama_ qa_la isabnu maryama lilhawa_riy yina man ansa_ri ilal la_h qa_lal hawa_riy yu_na nahnu ansha_rul la_hi fa a_manat ta_ifa fum min bani isra_ila wa kafarat ta_ifah fa ay yadnal lazina a_manu_ ala_ aduw wihim fa ashbahu_ za_hirin
Yusab bihu lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardi malikil qud du_sil azizil hakim
Huwal lazi baatsa fil um miy yina rasu_lam minhum yatlu_ alaihim a_ya_tihi wa yuzak kihim wa yual limuhumul kita_ba wal hikmah wa in ka_nu_ min qablu lafi dala_lim mubin
Wa a_kharina minhum lam ma_ yalhaqu_ bihim wa huwal azizul hakim
Za_lika fadul la_hi yutihi may yasya wal la_hu zul fadhil azhim
Matsalul lazina hum milut taura_ta suma ma lam yahmilu_ha_ kamatsalil hima_ri yahmilu asfa_ra_ bisa matsalul qaumil lazina kaz zabu_ bia_ya_til la_h wal la_hu la_ yahdil qaumaz za_limin
Qul ya_ ay yuhal lazina ha_du_ in zaantum an nakum auliya_u lil la_hi min du_nin na_si fa taman nawul mauta in kuntum sa_diqin
Wa la_ yataman naunahu_ abadan bima_ qad damat aidihim wal la_hu alimun biz za_limin
Qul in nal mautal lazi tafir ru_na minhu fa in nahu_ mula_qikum suma turad du_na ila_ a_limil gaibi was saha_dati fayunab bi ukum bima_ kuntum tamalu_n
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ iza_ nu_diya lis sala_ti miy yaumil jumuati fasau ila_ zikril la_hi wa zarul baia za_likum hairul lakum in kuntum talamu_n
Fa iza_ qudiyatish sala_tu fantasyiru_ fil ardi wabtaghu_ min fadlil la_hi wazkurul la_ha katsiral la al lakum tuflihu_n
Wa iza_ ra au tija_ratan au lahwanin fad du_ ilaiha_ wa taraku_ka qa_ima_ qul ma_ indal la_hi kairum minal lahwi wa minat tija_rah wal la_hu kairuf ra_ziqin
Iza_ ja_akal muna_fiqu_na qa_lu_ nashadu in naka larasu_lul la_h wal la_hu yalamu in naka larasu_luh wal la_hu yas hadu in nal muna_fiqina taka_zibu_n
It takazu_ aima_nahum jun natan fasad du_ an sabilil la_h in nahum sa_a ma_ ka_nu yamalu_n
Za_lika bi an nahum a_manu_ sum ma kafaru_ fatubia ala_ qulu_bihim fahum la_ yafqahu_n
Wa iza_ ra aitahum tujibuka ajsa_muhum wa iy yaqu_lu_ tasma liqaulihim ka an nahum husubum musan nadatun yabsabu_na kul la saihatin alaihim humul aduw wu fahzarhum qa_talahumul la_hu an na_ yufaku_n
Wa iza_ qila lahum taa_lau yastagfir lakum rasu_lul la_hi law wau ru u_sahum wa ra aitahum yashud du_na wahum mustakbiru_n
Sawa_un alaihim astagfarta lahum am lam tastagfi lahum lay yagfiral la_hu lahum in nal la_ha la_ yahdil qaumal la_siqin
Humul lazina yaqu_lu_na la_ tunfiqu_ ala_ man inda rasu_lil la_hi hata_ yanfadu du_ wa lil la_hi haza_inus sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa la_kinal muna_fiqina la_ yafqahu_n
Yaqu_lu_na la ir rajana_l ilal madinati layukhrijan nal a'az zu minhal azal wal lil la_hil iz zatu wa lirasu_lihi wa lilmuminina wa la_kin nal muna_fiqina la_ yalamu_n
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ la_ tulhikum amwa_lukum wa la_ aula_dukum an zikril la_hi wa may yafal za_lika fa ula_ ika humul ha_siru_n
Wa anfiqu_ mim ma_ razaqna_kum min qabli ay yatiya ahadakumul mautu layaqu_la rab bi lau la_ akh karta mi ila_ ajalin qaribin fa as sad daqa qa akum minas sa_lihin
Wa lay yu akhiral la_hu nafsan iza_ ja_ a ajaluha_ wal la_hu habi un bima_ tamalu_n
Yusabihu lil la_hi ma_ fis sama_wa_ti wa ma_ fil ardhi lahul hamdu wa huwa ala_ ku li syai in qadir
Huwal ladzi khalaqakum laminkum ka_firuw wa minkum mumin wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na bashir
Khalaqasa_ma_wa_ti wal ardha bil haq qi wa shaw warakum fa ahsana shuwa rakum wa ilaihil mashur
Ya lamu ma_  fis sama_wa_ti wal ardi wa yalamu ma_ tusu ru_na wa ma_ tulinu_n wal la_hu alimun biza_ tisudu_n
Alam yatikum naba ul lazina kafaru_ min qablu faza_qu_ wa ba_la amrihim wa lahum aza_bun alim
Zalika bi an nahu_ ka_nat tatihim rusuluhum bil bay yina_ti faqa_lu_ abasaru yahdu_nana_ fakafaru_ wa tawal lau wa istagnal la_h wal la_hu ganiy yun hamid
Za'amal lazina kafaru_ ahay yub atsu_ qul bala_ wa rab bu la tub atsun na sum ma latunab ba un na bima_ amiltum wa za_lika alal la_hi yasur
Fa a_minu_ bil la_hi wa rasu_lihi wan nu_ril lazi anzalna_ wal la_hu bima_ tamalu_na kabir
Yauma yajmaukum layaumil jami za_lika yaumut taga_hun wa may yumin bil la_hi wa yamal sa_lihay yukal fir anhu say yi a_tihi wa yud hilku jan na_tin taji min tahtihal anha_ru ha_lidina fiha_ abada_ za_likal fauzul azhim
Wal lazina kafaru_ wa kaz zabu_ bi a_ya_tina_ ula_ika asha_bun na_ri ha_lidina fiha_ wa bisal masi
Ma_ asha_ba mim musibatin il la_ bi iznil la_h wa may yumin bil la_hi yahdi qalbahu_ wal la_hu bikul li sai in alim
Wa atiul la_ha wa athiur rasu_la fa in tawal laitum fa in nama_ ala_ rasu_linal balagul mubin
Al la_hu la_ ila_ha il la_ huw wa alal la_hi falyatawak kalil muminu_n
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ in na min azwa_jikum wa aula_dikum aduw wal lakum fahzaru_hum wa in tafu_ wa tasfahu_ wa tagfiru_ fa in nal la_ha gafu_rur rahim
In nama_ amwa_lukum wa aula_dukum fitnah wal la_hu indahu_ ajrun azim
Fat taqul la_ha mastata tum wasmau_ wa atiu_ wa unfiqu_ khairal li anfisukum wa may yu_qa suh ha nafsihi fa ula_ika humul muflihu_n
In tuqridul la_ha qardan hasanay yuda_ifhu lakum wa yagfir lakum wal la_hu saku_run halim
A_limul gaibi was saha_datil azizul hakim
Ya_ ayuhan nabiy yu idza_ thal laq tumun nisa_ a fathal liqu_hun na li id datihin na wa ahshul id data wat taqul la_ha rab bakum la_ yakhrujna il la_ ay yatina bifa_hisyatim mubay yinah, wa tilka hudu_dul la_h, wa may yata'ad da hudu_dal la_hi faqad zhalama nafsahu_dal la_ha yuhditsu bada dza_lika amra_
Fa iza_ balagna ajalahun na fa amsi ku_hun na bimaru_fin au fa_riqu_hun na bimaru_fiwwa ashidu_ zawai adlim minkum wa aqimus saha_data lil la_hi zalikum yu_azhubihi man ka_na yuminu bil la_hi wal yaumil a_khir wa may yat taqil la_ha yajal lahu_ makhraja_
Wa yarzuqhu min haitsu la_ yahtasib, wa may yatakwak kal alal la_hi fa huwa hasbuh in nal la_ha ba_ligu amrih qad ja'alal la_hu likul li sai in qadra_
Wal la_i ya isna minal mahidi min nisa_ ikum inir tabtum faid datuhun na sala_tsatu ashuriw wal la_i lam yahidn wa ula_tul ahma_li ajalahuna ay yadana hamlahun wa may yat taqil la_ha yajal lahu_ min amrihi yusra_
Za_lika amrul la_hi anzalahu_ ilaikum wa may yat taqil la_ha yukaf fir anhu say yi a_tihi wa yuzim lahu_ ajra_
Askinu_hun na min haitsu sakantum miw wujdikum wa la_ tudha_r ru_huna lituday yiqu_ alihin wa in kun na_ ula_ti hamlin fa anfiqu_ alaihin na hat ta_ yadana hamlahun na fa in ardana lakum fa a_tu_huna uju_rahun na wa tamiru_ bainakum bimaru_fiw wa in taa_sartum fasaturdiu lahu_ ukhra_
Liyunfiq zu_ saatim min saatih wa man qudira alaihi rizquhu_ falyunfiq mim ma_ a_ta_hul la_h la_ yukal lifulla_hu nafsan il la_ ma_ a_ta_ha_ sayajalul la_hu bada usriy yusra_
Wa ka ay yim min qaryatin atat an amri rab biha_ wa rusulihi faha_sabna_ha_ hisa_ban sadidaw wa azzabna_ha_ aza_ban nukra_
Faza_qat waba_la amriha_ wa ka_na a_qibatu amriha_ khusra_
A'ad dal la_hu lahum aza_ban sadidan fat taqul la_ha ya_ ulil alba_bil lazina a_manu_ qad anzalal la_hu ilaikum zikra_
Rasu_lay yatlu_ alaikum a_ya_til la_hi mubay yina_til liyukrijal lazina a_manu_ wa amilush sa_liha_ti minaz zuluma_ti ilan nu_r wa may yumin bil la_hi wa yamal sa_lihay yudkilhu jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru ka_lidina fiha_ abada_ qad ahsanal la_hu  lahu_ rizqa_
Al la_hul lazi halaqa saba sama_wa_tiw wa minal ardi mitslahun yatanaz zalul amru bainahuna litalamu_ an nal la_ha ala_ kul li syai in qadiruw wa an nal la_ha qad aha_ta bikuli sai in ilma_
Ya_ ay yuhan nabiyu lima tuhar rimu ma_ ahal lal la_hu laka tabtagi marda_ta azwa_jik wal la_hu gafu_rur rahim
Qad faradal la_hu lakum tahil lata aima_nikum wal la_hu maula_kum wa huwal alimul hakim
Wa iz asar ran nabiyu ila_ badi azwa_jihi hadistsa falam ma_ nab ba at bihi wa azharahul la_hu alaihi ar rafa badahu_ wa arada an badin falam ma_ nab ba ahabihi qa_lat man an ba aka ha_za_ qa_la nab ba aniyal alimul kabir
In tatu_ba_ ilal la_hi faqad sagat qulu_bukuma_ wa in taza_hara_ alaihi la in nal la_ha huwa maula_hu wa jib rilu wa sa_lihul muminin wal mala_ ikatu bada za_lika zahir
Asa_ rab buhu_ in tal laqakun na ay yubdilahu_ azwa_jan kairan minkuna muslima_tim mumina_tin qa_nita_tin ta_ iba_tin a_bida_tin sa_iha_tin say yibatiw wa abka_ra_
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ qu_ anfusakum wa ahlikum na_raw wa qu_duhan na_su wal hija_ratu alaiha_ mala_ ikatun gila_zun sida_dul la_ yasu_nal la_ha ma_ amarahum wa yafalu_na ma_ yumaru_n
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina kafaru_la_ tatazirul yaum in nama_ tujzauna ma_ kuntum tamalu_n
Ya_ ay yuhal lazina a_manu_ tu_bu_ ilal la_hi taubatan nasu_ha_ asa_ rabukum ay yukaf fira ankum say yia_tikum wa yudhilakum jan na_tin tajri min tahtihal anha_ru yauma la_ yukhzil la_hun nabiy ya wal lazina a_manu_ maahu_ nu_ruhum yasa_baina aidihim wa bi aima_nihim ya qu_lu_na rab bana_ atmim lana_ nu_ rana_ wagfir lana_ in naka ala_ kul li sai in qadir
Ya ay yuhan nabiy yu ja_hidil kuf fa_ra wal muna_fiqina wagluz alaihim wa mawa_hum jahan nam wa bisal masir
Darabal la_hu matsalal lil lazina kafarum ra ata nu_hiw wamra ata lu_t ka_nata_ tahta abdaini min iba_dina_ sa_lihaini fakha_nata_huma_ falam yughniya_ anhuma_ minal la_hi sai aw wa qilad kulan na_ra maad da_ hilin
Wa  darabal la_hu matsalal lil lazina a_manum ra ata firaun iz qa_lat rabibni lil indaka baitan fil jan nati wa naj jini min firauna wa amalihi wa naj jini minal qaumiz za_limin
Wa maryamab nata imra_nal latu ahsanat farjaha_ fanafahna_ fihi mir ru_hina_ wa sad daqat bikalima_ti rab iha_ wa kutubihi wa ka_nat minal qa_nitin
Taba_rakal lazi biyadihil mulku wahuwa ala_ kulli syain qadir
Alazi halakal mauta wal haya_ta liyab luwakumay yukum ahsanu ama la_ wa huwal azizul gafu_r
Alazi halaqa saba sama_wa_tin tiba_qa_, ma_ tara_ fi halqir rahma_ni min tafa_wut farjiil  basara hal tara_ min futu_r

Iza ulqu_ fiha_ samiu_ laha_ sahiqaw wa hiya tafu_r
Taka_du tama yazu minal gaiz kulama_ ulqiya fiha_ faujun sa alahum hazanatuha_ alam yatikum nazir.
Qa_lu bala_ qad ja_ana_ nazirun fakaz zabna_ wa qulna_ ma_ naz zalal la_hu min syain in antum il la_ fi dala_lin kabir
Wa qa_lu lau kun na_ nasmau au naqilu ma_ kun na_ fi asha_bi sair
Fa tarafu_ bizan bihim fasuhqal liasha_bis sair
Inal lazina yaksyauna rabahum bil gaibi lahum magfiratu wa ajrun kabir

Wa man fil ardi jamian suma yunjih
Kal la_ in naha_ laza_
Naz za_atal lis sawa_
Tadu_ man adbara wa tawal la_
Wa jamaa fa aua_
In nal insa_na huliqa halu_a_
Iza mas sahus sar ru jazu_a_
Wa iza mas sahul hairu manu_a_
Il lal musal lin
Al lazinahum ala_ sala_tihim da_imu_n
Wal lazina fi amwa_lihim haq qum malu_m
Lis sa_ili wal mahru_m
Wal lazina yushad diqu_na biyaumidin
Wal lazina hum min aza_bi rabihim musfiqu_n
In na aza_ba rab bihim gairu mamu_n
Wal lazina hum lifu_rujihim ha_fizu_n
Il la_ ala_ az wa_jihim au ma_  malaka aima_nuhum fa in nahum gairu malu_min
Famanibtaga_ wara_a za_lika fa ula_ ika humul a_du_n
Wal lazina hum li ama_na_tihim waahdihim ra_u_n
Wal lazina hum bisaha_da_tihim qa_ imu_n
Wal lazina hum ala_ sa_la_tihim yuha_fizu_n
Ula_ ika fi jan na_tim mukramu_n
Fama_lil lazina kafaru_ qibalaka mutiin
Anil yamini wa anis sima_li izin
Ayatmau kulumrim minhum ayudkala  jan nata maim
Kal la_ in na_ halaqna_hum mim ma_ yalamu_n
Fala_ uqsimu birab bil masaya_riqi wal magha_ribi in na_ laqadiru_n
Ala_ an nubad dila kairam minhum wa ma_ nahnu bimasbu_qin
Fazarhum yaku_du_ wa yalabu_ bat ta_ yula_qu_ yaumahumul lazi yu_adu_n
Yauma yakhruju_na minal ajda_si sira_an ka an nahum ila_ nusubi yu_fidu_n
Ka_siatan absa_ruhum tarquhum zilah za_likal yaumul lazi ka_nu_ yu_adu_n
In na_ arsalna_ nu_han ila_ qaumilhi an anzir qaumaka min qabil ay yatiyahum aza_bun alim
Qa_la ya_ qaumi in ni lakum nazirum mubin
Anibudul la_ha wat taqu_hu wa atiu_n
Yagfir lakum min zunu_bikum wa yu akhirkum ila_ ajalim musama_ in na ajalal la_hi iza_ ja_ a la_ yuakhar lau kuntum talamu_n
Qa_la rab bi in ni daautu qaumi lai law wa naha_ra_
Falam yazidhum dua_ i il la_ fira_ra_
Wa in ni kul lama_ daautuhum litagfira lahum ja'alu_ asha_biahum fi a_za_nihim wastagsau siya_bahum wa ashar ru_ wastakbaru_s tikba_ra_
Suma in ni daautuhum jiha_ra_
Suma in ni alantu lahum wa asrartu lahum isra_ra_
Faqultus tagfiru_ rab bakum in nahu_ ka_na gaf fa_ra_
Yursilis sama_a alaikum midra_ra_
Wa yumdidkum bi amwa_liw wa banina wa yajal lakum jan na_tiw wa yaj al lakum anha_ra_
Ma_ lakum la_ tarju_na lil la_hi wa qa_ra_
Wa qad kalaqakum atwa_ra_
Alam tarau kaifa halaqal la_hu saba sama_wa_tin tiba_qa_
Wa ja'alal qamara fihin na nu_raw wa ja'alas samsa sira_ja_
Wal la_hu ambatakum minal ardi naba_ta_
Suma yuidukum fiha_ wa yukrijukum ikhra_ja_
Wal la_hu jaala lakumul arda bisa_ta_
Litasluku_ minha_ subulan fija_ja_
Qa_la nu_hur rabi in nahum ashauni wat tabau_ mal lam yazid hu ma_luhu_ wa waladuhu_ il la_ hasa_ra_
Wa makaru_ makran kub ba_ra_
Wa qa_lu_ la_ tadzarun na a_laihatakum wa la_ tadzarun na wad daw wa la_ suwa_aw wa la_ yagu_tsa wa yau_qa wa nasra_
Wa qad adal lu_ katsira_ wa la_ tazidih za_limina il la_ dala_la_
Mim ma_ kati a_tihim ugriqu_ faudhilu_ na_ran falam yajidu_ lahum min du_nil la_hi ansa_ra_
Wa qa_la nu_hur rab bi la_ tazar alal ardi minal ka_firina day ya_ra_
In naka in tazarhum yudhil lu_ iba_daka wa la_ yalidu_ il la_ fa_jiran kafa_ra_
Rabigfirli wa liwa_liday ya waliman dakhala baitiya muminaw wa lil muminina walmumina_t wa la_ tazidih za_limina ai la_ taba_ra_
Qul u_hiya ilay ya an nahustamaa nafarum minal jin ni faqa_lu_ in na_ samina_ qur a_nan ajaba_
Yahdi ilar rusdi fa a_man na_ bih wa lan nusrika birab bina_ ahada_
Wa an nahu_ taa_la_ jad du rab bina_ mat takhaza sa_hibataw wa la_ walada_
Wa an nahu_ ka_na yaqu_lu safihuna_ alal la_hi satata_
Wa an na_ zanan na_ al lan taqu_lal insu wal jin nu alal la_h kaziba_
Wa an nahu_ ka_na rija_lum minal insi yau_zu_na birija_lim minal jin nifaza_du_hum rahaqa_
Wa an nahum zan nu_ kama_ zanantum al lay yabasal lahu_ ahada_
Wa an na_ lamasna sama_a fawajadna_ha_ muliat harasan sadidaw wa suhuba_
Wa an na_ kun na_ naqudu minha_ maqa_ida lis sami famay yastami ila_na yajid lahu_ siha_bar rasa da_
Wa an na_la_ nadri asyar run urida biman fil ardi am ara_da bihim rabuhum rasada_
Wa an na_ min nas sa_lihu_na wamin na_ du_na za_lik kun na_ tara_iqa qida_da_
Wa an na_ zanan na_ alan nuji zal la_ha fil ardi wa lan nujizahu_ haraba_
Wa an na_ lam ma_ saminal huda_ a_man na_ bih famay yumin birabihi fala_ yaka_fu baksaw wa la_ rahaqa_
Wa an na_ minal muslimu_na wa minnal qa_situ_n faman aslama fa ula_ika tahar rau hataba_
Wa am mal qa_situ_na faka_nu_ lijahan nama hataba_
Wa al lawistaqa_mu_ alat tariqatila asqaina_hum ma_ an gadaqa_
Linsftinahum fih, wa may yuridh an dzikri rab bihi yasluk hu adza_ban sha'ada_
Wa an nal masa_jida lil la_hi fala_ tadu_ mala_hi ahada_
Wa an nahu_ lam ma_ qa_ma abdul la_hi yadu_hu  ka_du_ yaku_nu_na alaihi libada_
Qul in nama_ adu_ rab bi wa la_ usyriku bihi ahada_
Qul in ni la_ amliku lakum dhar raw wa la_ raswyada_
Qul in ni lay yujirani minal la_hi aha duw wa lan ajida min du_nihi mul tahada_
Il la_ bala_gham minal la_hi wa risa_ la_tih, wa may yashil la_ha wa rasu_ lahu_ fa in na lahu_ na_ra jahan nama kha_lidina fiha_ adada_
Hat ta_ idza_ ra au ma_ yu_ adu_na fayalamu_na man adhafu na_shiraw wa aqal lu adada_
Qul in adri aqaribum ma_ tu_adu_na am yajalu lahu_ rab bi  amada_
A_limul ghaibi fala_ yuzhhiru ala_ ghaibihi ahada_
Illa manirtadha_ mir rasu_lin fa in na hu_ yasluku min baini yadaihi wa min khalfihi rashada_
Liyalama an qad ablaqhu_ risa_la_ti rab bihim wa ahatha bima_ ladaihim wa ahsha_kul la syai in adada_
Ya_ ay yuhal muz zam mil
Qumil laila il la_ qalila_
Nishfahu_ awinqush minhu qalila_
Au zid alaihi wa rat tili qur a_na tai tila_
In na_ sanulqi alaika qaulan tsaqila_
In na na_syi atal laili hiya asyad du wath aw aqwamu qila_
In na fin naha_ri sabhan thawi la_
Wadzkurisma rab bika wa tabat tal ilaihi tabtila_
Rab bul masyriqi wal maghribi la_ ila_ ha il la_ huwa tat takhidz hu wakila_
Washbir ala_ ma_ yaqu_lu_na wahjur hum hajran jamila_
Wa dzami wal mukadz dzibina ulin namati wa mah hilhum qalila_
In na ladaina_ anka_law wa jahima_
Wa tha'a_man dza_ qhush shatiw wa adza_ban alima_
Yauma tarjuful ardhu wal jiba_lu wa ka_natil jiba_lu katsibam mahila_
In na_ arsalna_ ilaikum rasu_lan sya_ hidan alaikum kama_ arsalna_ firauna rasu_la_
Fa'asha_ firaunur rasu_la fa akhadz na_hu akhdzaw wabila_
Fakaifa tat taqu_na in kafartum yau may yajalul wilda_na syiha_
As sama_ u munfathirun bih, ka_na waduhu_ mafu_la_
In na ha_dzihi tadzkiratun faman sya_ at takhadza ila_ rab bihi sabila_
In na rab baka yalamu an naka taqu_ mu adna_ min tsulutsayil laili wa nish fahu_ wa tsulutsahu_ wa tha_ ifatum minal ladzina maak, wal la_hu yu qad dirul laila wan naha_r, alima al lan tuhshu_hu fata_ba alaikum faqra u_ ma_ tayas sara minal qura_n, alima an sayaku_nu minkum mardha_ wa a_ kharu_na yadhribu_na fil ardhi yabta qhu_na min fadhlil la_hi wa a_kharu_ na yuqa_tilu_na fi sabilil la_h, faqra u_ ma_ taya sara minhu wa aqimush shala_fa wa a_tuz zaka_ta wa aqridhul la_ha qardhan hasana_, wa ma tuqad dimu_ li anfusikum min khairin tajidu_hu  indal la_hi huwa khairin wa azhama ajra_, wastagfirul la_h, in nal la_ha ghafu_ru_r rahim
Ya_ ay yu yuhal mud dats tsir
